## 1. 通过对单个细胞进行全基因组与转录组联合分析解析乳腺癌的细胞起源

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776832)
**期刊：** Genomics, proteomics & bioinformatics
**PMID：** 41776832
**DOI：** 10.1093/gpbjnl/qzag021

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Unraveling Cell of Origin in Breast Cancer via Joint Profiling of Whole Genome and Transcriptome in Individual Cells.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无摘要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过单细胞水平的全基因组与转录组联合测序技术，解析乳腺癌的细胞起源。其核心方法是在同一单个细胞中整合基因组变异与转录组表达谱，有望在单细胞分辨率上建立基因型与表型的直接关联。该策略的创新性在于能够同时捕捉驱动突变的克隆起源和相应的转录组特征，为理解肿瘤异质性提供了强大的工具。然而，摘要的缺失使我们无法评估其具体发现、数据规模及该技术方法在复杂肿瘤微环境中应用的潜在局限性。

## 2. 突变型p53通过表观遗传重编程CXCL10促进CD8⁺ T细胞浸润并增强晚期前列腺癌的抗PD-1反应。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

> 无摘要。

## 8. Orosomucoid 2通过重塑丝氨酸和一碳代谢通路抑制自然杀伤细胞介导的抗肿瘤免疫，从而促进结直肠癌肝转移。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776586)
**期刊：** Molecular cancer
**PMID：** 41776586
**DOI：** 10.1186/s12943-026-02616-7

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Orosomucoid 2 promotes colorectal cancer liver metastasis by suppressing natural killer cell-mediated antitumor immunity by remodeling the serine and one-carbon metabolism pathway.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无摘要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在揭示Orosomucoid 2 (ORM2)在结直肠癌肝转移中的新机制。研究发现，ORM2通过重塑肿瘤细胞的丝氨酸和一碳代谢通路，抑制了自然杀伤（NK）细胞的抗肿瘤免疫功能，从而促进了肝转移的发生。这一发现将肿瘤代谢重编程与免疫逃逸机制联系起来，为理解转移提供了新的视角，并提示ORM2或相关代谢通路可能成为治疗靶点。然而，研究主要基于标题信息，具体实验模型、验证方法和临床相关性等细节尚不明确，其转化潜力有待进一步评估。

## 9. 肿瘤靶向IL2促进特异性CD8 T细胞私有克隆扩增以增强淋巴瘤控制

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776565)
**期刊：** Journal of experimental & clinical cancer research : CR
**PMID：** 41776565
**DOI：** 10.1186/s13046-026-03678-7

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Tumor-targeted IL2 promotes specific CD8 T cells private clonal expansion enhancing lymphoma control.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无摘要可用。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索肿瘤靶向递送IL-2（白细胞介素-2）对淋巴瘤免疫治疗的影响。其核心方法是通过靶向策略将IL-2特异性递送至肿瘤微环境，以激活并扩增识别肿瘤抗原的特异性CD8 T细胞克隆。研究发现，这种策略能有效促进这些T细胞的“私有”克隆扩增，从而增强对淋巴瘤的控制效果。其创新性在于将细胞因子治疗与精准靶向相结合，旨在提高疗效并可能减少全身毒性，但研究的局限性在于摘要信息缺失，具体实验模型、剂量效应及潜在副作用等关键细节尚不明确。

---

## 14. 胆道癌患者的围手术期治疗策略

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776242)
**期刊：** Nature reviews. Clinical oncology
**PMID：** 41776242
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41571-026-01130-5

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Perioperative approaches for patients with biliary tract cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Biliary tract cancers, encompassing intrahepatic, perihilar and distal cholangiocarcinoma and gallbladder cancer, are a heterogeneous group of highly aggressive malignancies. Most patients have unresectable disease at first presentation, and even those who undergo surgery are likely to have disease recurrence. Newer approaches have included liver transplantation for selected patients, and the integration of locoregional and systemic therapies has expanded the number of patients who can benefit from surgery. The advent of immune-checkpoint inhibitors and targeted therapies for patients with advanced-stage disease has prompted the exploration of these agents in earlier-stage disease settings. Despite this progress, treatment algorithms remain complex, necessitating a multidisciplinary and individualized approach to patient management. Future research should focus on optimizing patient selection through biomarker-driven strategies, including the integration of molecular profiles to guide the selection of systemic therapy, as well as refining the criteria for surgery and transplantation. These improvements will require global collaboration and novel clinical trial designs. In this Review, we describe evolving perioperative strategies for the management of patients with biliary tract cancers and highlight emerging directions in the field.

> **中文摘要：**
> 胆道癌，包括肝内胆管癌、肝门部胆管癌、远端胆管癌和胆囊癌，是一组异质性高、侵袭性强的恶性肿瘤。大多数患者在首次就诊时已为不可切除疾病，即使接受手术的患者也极有可能出现疾病复发。更新的治疗方法包括为特定患者进行肝移植，以及局部治疗与全身治疗的整合，从而扩大了能从手术中获益的患者群体。针对晚期疾病患者的免疫检查点抑制剂和靶向疗法的出现，促使人们开始探索这些药物在更早期疾病阶段的应用。尽管取得了这些进展，治疗决策流程仍然复杂，需要多学科协作和个体化的患者管理方法。未来的研究应侧重于通过生物标志物驱动的策略来优化患者选择，包括整合分子谱以指导全身治疗的选择，以及完善手术和移植的标准。这些改进将需要全球合作和创新的临床试验设计。在本综述中，我们描述了胆道癌患者管理中不断演变的围手术期策略，并强调了该领域的新兴方向。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本综述旨在系统阐述胆道癌围手术期治疗策略的演变与未来方向。其核心方法是通过整合现有文献，分析手术、肝移植、局部及全身治疗（包括免疫与靶向疗法）在围手术期的应用价值与挑战。文章发现，尽管治疗手段不断丰富，但胆道癌的诊疗仍高度复杂，需依赖多学科和个体化策略；其创新性在于前瞻性地提出了基于生物标志物和分子谱的精准患者选择是未来优化治疗的关键，并强调了全球合作与新型临床试验设计的必要性。局限性在于作为一篇综述，其结论主要基于对现有研究的总结与展望，而非提供新的原始临床数据。

---

## 15. 基于生成扩散人工智能与非对比磁共振成像的无对比剂胶质瘤血脑屏障状态识别

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776178)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41776178
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-69578-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Contrast-free identification of glioma blood-brain barrier status via generative diffusion AI and non-contrast MRI.

> **英文摘要：**
> Non-contrast MRI, routinely used for the preoperative diagnosis of glioma tumors and establishing treatment strategies, provides the potential for assessing blood-brain barrier (BBB) status without using gadolinium-based contrast agents (GBCA) which could cause adverse events. Additionally, generative artificial intelligence (AI) models enable the synthesis of contrast-enhanced images from non-contrast images. Despite this potential, the heterogeneity of GBCA-induced features in tumor areas and error accumulation from inaccurate synthesis largely limit the efficacy of conventional generative models. To address these limitations, we introduce a contrast-free BBB status identification model (CBSI) that can identify BBB status with high accuracy using non-contrast MR images and generative diffusion AI networks. Trained and validated on a multi-center dataset of 1,535 patients, CBSI achieves an area under the curve (AUC) of 81.31%, surpassing the performance of the model using only non-contrast MR (AUC = 72.76%) and demonstrating comparable performance to the T1Gd MR model (AUC = 88.68%) in an external test set. Furthermore, validation on two public datasets (BraTS-Africa and BraTS-GLI) supports the generalizability of CBSI in BBB status identification. Notably, with accurate BBB status of synthetic T1Gd, the performance of glioma segmentation and grading is improved significantly compared to existing methods. Generalizability analysis indicates that CBSI can facilitate BBB status identification using synthetic T1Gd findings, avoiding GBCA adverse effects and streamlining clinical workflows.

> **中文摘要：**
> 常规用于胶质瘤术前诊断和制定治疗策略的非对比磁共振成像，为评估血脑屏障状态提供了潜力，而无需使用可能引起不良事件的钆基对比剂。此外，生成式人工智能模型能够从非对比图像合成对比增强图像。尽管存在这种潜力，但肿瘤区域中GBCA诱导特征的异质性以及不准确合成导致的误差累积，在很大程度上限制了传统生成模型的有效性。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了一种无对比剂的血脑屏障状态识别模型，该模型能够利用非对比MR图像和生成扩散AI网络高精度地识别BBB状态。该模型在一个包含1,535名患者的多中心数据集上进行了训练和验证，其曲线下面积达到81.31%，超越了仅使用非对比MR的模型性能，并在外部测试集中表现出与T1Gd MR模型相当的性能。此外，在两个公共数据集上的验证支持了CBSI在BBB状态识别方面的普适性。值得注意的是，凭借合成T1Gd图像提供的准确BBB状态信息，胶质瘤分割和分级的性能相较于现有方法得到显著提升。普适性分析表明，CBSI可以利用合成的T1Gd结果促进BBB状态识别，从而避免GBCA的不良反应并简化临床工作流程。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在开发一种无需钆对比剂即可识别胶质瘤血脑屏障状态的方法。其核心创新在于结合非对比MRI与生成扩散AI模型，构建了CBSI模型，直接进行BBB状态分类，而非传统地先合成对比增强图像。研究发现，CBSI在外部测试中达到了与金标准T1Gd MRI模型相近的性能，并能提升下游胶质瘤分割与分级的准确性，展现了良好的泛化能力。该研究的创新性在于绕过了图像合成的误差累积问题，直接实现功能状态判定，具有重要的临床转化潜力；其局限性可能在于模型性能（AUC 81.31%）仍略低于金标准，且对多中心数据质量和标注一致性有较高依赖。

---

## 16. VISTA通过调控肿瘤相关巨噬细胞极化驱动胰腺肿瘤进展。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776161)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41776161
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70215-7

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** VISTA drives pancreatic tumor progression through modulation of the tumor-associated macrophage polarity.

> **英文摘要：**
> Pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma (PDAC) remains one of the deadliest malignancies due to its highly immunosuppressive tumor microenvironment (TME), which limits effective therapeutic interventions. Here, we demonstrate that V-domain immunoglobulin suppressor of T cell activation (VISTA) plays a crucial role in orchestrating macrophage polarity within the PDAC TME. Using murine PDAC models, we show that VISTA deficiency markedly impairs tumor growth, leading to prolonged survival. Functionally, VISTA deficiency is linked to a shift in tumor-associated macrophages (TAMs) from an immunosuppressive phenotype marked by secreted phosphoprotein 1 (SPP1), to one enriched for C-X-C motif chemokine ligand 9 (CXCL9), indicative of a pro-inflammatory state. This shift is accompanied by enhanced recruitment of CXCR3⁺ CD8⁺ T cells with sustained cytotoxic potential, among which terminal exhaustion-like CD8 T cell states are less prevalent. Additionally, VISTA-deficient TAMs exhibit increased antigen cross-presentation, further amplifying CD8 T cell response against tumors. These findings are corroborated by human PDAC data, which reflect similar immune reprogramming trends. By defining the role of VISTA in controlling Cxcl9:Spp1 ratio and modulating CD8⁺ T cell dynamics, this study positions VISTA inhibition as a promising strategy to reshape the TME and potentiate anti-tumor immunity in PDAC.

> **中文摘要：**
> 胰腺导管腺癌（PDAC）因其高度免疫抑制的肿瘤微环境（TME）而仍然是最致命的恶性肿瘤之一，这限制了有效的治疗干预。本文中，我们证明V结构域T细胞激活抑制性免疫球蛋白（VISTA）在协调PDAC TME内的巨噬细胞极化中起着关键作用。利用小鼠PDAC模型，我们发现VISTA缺陷显著损害肿瘤生长，并延长生存期。在功能上，VISTA缺陷与肿瘤相关巨噬细胞（TAMs）的表型转变相关，即从以分泌性磷蛋白1（SPP1）为标志的免疫抑制表型，转变为富含C-X-C基序趋化因子配体9（CXCL9）的表型，这指示了一种促炎状态。这种转变伴随着具有持续细胞毒潜能的CXCR3⁺ CD8⁺ T细胞的募集增强，其中终末耗竭样CD8 T细胞状态较少出现。此外，VISTA缺陷的TAMs表现出抗原交叉提呈能力增强，进一步放大了针对肿瘤的CD8 T细胞反应。这些发现在人类PDAC数据中得到证实，反映了类似的免疫重编程趋势。通过明确VISTA在控制Cxcl9:Spp1比率和调节CD8⁺ T细胞动态中的作用，本研究将VISTA抑制定位为一种重塑TME并增强PDAC抗肿瘤免疫的有前景的策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明VISTA在胰腺癌免疫抑制微环境中的关键作用。通过小鼠模型，研究揭示了VISTA缺失能通过重编程巨噬细胞极化（从SPP1⁺免疫抑制表型转向CXCL9⁺促炎表型），进而增强CD8⁺ T细胞的募集与功能，从而抑制肿瘤生长。其创新性在于将VISTA的功能与巨噬细胞极化及T细胞动态调控直接联系起来，并提出了靶向VISTA的治疗潜力。然而，研究主要基于动物模型，其结论在人类患者中的普适性及具体转化路径仍需更多临床前和临床研究验证。

---

## 17. HIV-seq揭示病毒血症期与抑制期HIV感染者体内HIV转录细胞的基因表达差异

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776157)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41776157
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-68797-3

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** HIV-seq reveals gene expression differences between HIV-transcribing cells from viremic and suppressed people with HIV.

> **英文摘要：**
> HIV-transcribing cells can perpetuate chronic inflammation in ART-suppressed people with HIV (PWH) and likely contribute to viral rebound after ART interruption. However, these cells are difficult to study using single-cell RNA-seq (scRNA-seq) due to their low frequency and low levels of HIV transcripts, which are usually not polyadenylated. By spiking in capture sequences targeting conserved regions of HIV during scRNA-seq - a new method we call "HIV-seq" - we detect double the mean number of HIV reads per cell from PWH. HIV RNA+ cells are enriched among T effector memory cells during both viremia and ART suppression but exhibit a cytotoxic signature during viremia only. In contrast, HIV-transcribing cells from ART-suppressed timepoints exhibit a distinct anti-inflammatory signature involving elevated TGF-β and diminished IFN signaling. These findings demonstrate that HIV-seq is a useful tool to better understand the mechanisms by which HIV-transcribing cells can persist during ART.

> **中文摘要：**
> HIV转录细胞可在抗逆转录病毒疗法（ART）抑制的HIV感染者（PWH）中维持慢性炎症，并可能在ART中断后导致病毒反弹。然而，由于这些细胞频率低且HIV转录本水平低（通常不含多聚腺苷酸尾），使用单细胞RNA测序（scRNA-seq）对其进行研究存在困难。通过在scRNA-seq过程中加入靶向HIV保守区域的捕获序列（我们称之为“HIV-seq”的新方法），我们从PWH样本中检测到的每个细胞的平均HIV读数增加了一倍。在病毒血症期和ART抑制期，HIV RNA+细胞均在T效应记忆细胞中富集，但仅在病毒血症期表现出细胞毒性特征。相比之下，来自ART抑制时间点的HIV转录细胞则表现出独特的抗炎特征，涉及TGF-β信号升高和IFN信号减弱。这些发现表明，HIV-seq是更好地理解HIV转录细胞在ART期间持续存在机制的有用工具。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在开发并应用一种名为“HIV-seq”的新型单细胞测序技术，以克服传统方法难以检测低频、非多聚腺苷酸化HIV转录本的局限。核心创新在于通过引入靶向HIV保守区的捕获序列，显著提升了HIV转录细胞的检测灵敏度。研究发现，尽管病毒血症期与ART抑制期的HIV转录细胞均富集于T效应记忆细胞亚群，但其基因表达谱存在显著差异：前者呈现细胞毒性特征，后者则表现为独特的抗炎特征。这为理解ART抑制下病毒持续存在及免疫失调的机制提供了新视角。然而，该方法的局限性在于主要揭示了转录组层面的关联，其功能学意义及在更广泛人群中的普适性仍需后续研究验证。

---

## 18. 对193个国家抗菌药物耐药性治理的评估，为2026年全球行动计划更新提供信息

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776078)
**期刊：** Nature medicine
**PMID：** 41776078
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41591-026-04257-1

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Evaluation of antimicrobial resistance governance across 193 countries to inform the 2026 Global Action Plan update.

> **英文摘要：**
> Antimicrobial resistance (AMR) poses a major global health threat, yet the effectiveness of national action plans (NAPs) remains uncertain. Here we developed a multidimensional One Health governance index through a structured Delphi expert consultation to evaluate AMR governance across 193 countries (2017-2022), integrating 269 policy documents, expert-weighted indicators and multinational survey and surveillance datasets. Difference-in-differences and joinpoint regression analyses were used to link governance to antimicrobial use, AMR prevalence and AMR-related mortality. Global governance scores improved from 30.7 to 44.5/100, although implementation and monitoring lagged behind policy design, particularly in animal and environmental sectors. A significant increase in AMR prevalence scores was observed only 5 years after NAP adoption (two-stage difference-in-differences, β = 2.43, 95% confidence interval (CI) 1.02-3.85, P < 0.05), underscoring the delayed impact of policy. Multisector engagement (early-adopting countries, β = 0.05, 95% CI 0.02-0.08, P < 0.01) and antimicrobial use surveillance system (early-adopting countries, β = 0.05, 95% CI 0.03-0.07, P < 0.01) showed the strongest associations with improvement in AMR outcomes. As the 2026 Global Action Plan update approaches, sustained financing and integrated One Health surveillance, with stronger environmental and agricultural engagement, are essential for translating NAPs into sustained reductions in resistance.

> **中文摘要：**
> 抗菌药物耐药性（AMR）构成了重大的全球健康威胁，然而国家行动计划（NAPs）的有效性仍不确定。本研究通过结构化的德尔菲专家咨询，开发了一个多维度的“同一健康”治理指数，用以评估193个国家（2017-2022年）的AMR治理情况，整合了269份政策文件、专家加权指标以及多国调查和监测数据集。研究采用双重差分法和连接点回归分析，将治理情况与抗菌药物使用、AMR流行率和AMR相关死亡率联系起来。全球治理得分从30.7分提高到了44.5分（满分100分），但实施和监测落后于政策设计，尤其是在动物和环境领域。仅在NAP采纳5年后才观察到AMR流行率评分的显著增加（两阶段双重差分法，β = 2.43，95%置信区间（CI）1.02-3.85，P < 0.05），这突显了政策的延迟影响。多部门参与（早期采纳国家，β = 0.05，95% CI 0.02-0.08，P < 0.01）和抗菌药物使用监测系统（早期采纳国家，β = 0.05，95% CI 0.03-0.07，P < 0.01）与AMR结局的改善显示出最强的关联。随着2026年全球行动计划更新的临近，持续的资金投入和整合的“同一健康”监测，以及更强的环境和农业部门参与，对于将NAPs转化为耐药性的持续降低至关重要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过构建一个多维度的“同一健康”治理指数，系统评估全球193个国家的AMR治理现状，为2026年全球行动计划更新提供循证依据。其创新性在于整合了政策文本、专家权重和多源监测数据，并运用双重差分等因果推断方法量化了治理措施与AMR结局间的关联及延迟效应。核心发现揭示了全球治理虽有进步但实施滞后，且多部门协同与使用监测是改善结局的关键驱动因素。局限性在于，作为观察性研究，尽管采用了高级统计方法，但仍可能存在未测量的混杂因素，且主要依赖国家层面的聚合数据，难以捕捉子国家层面的异质性。

---

## 19. GITR激活通过挽救耗竭状态，增强从胶质母细胞瘤扩增的肿瘤浸润淋巴细胞的抗肿瘤免疫。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776051)
**期刊：** Oncogene
**PMID：** 41776051
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41388-026-03705-z

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** GITR activation potentiates anti-tumor immunity of tumor-infiltrating lymphocytes expanded from glioblastoma by rescuing exhaustion.

> **英文摘要：**
> Autologous tumor-infiltrating lymphocyte (TIL) therapy holds transformative potential for solid tumors, yet its efficacy in glioblastoma remains limited by T cell exhaustion and immunosuppression. In the current study, we optimized an effective and reliable method for in vitro expansion of TILs from glioblastoma lesions and assessed their tumor-killing capacity both in vitro and in vivo. Single-cell RNA sequencing (scRNA-seq) of expanded TILs uncovered their heterogeneity and identified a cytotoxic tissue-resident memory (TRM) CD8 TIL subset with a unique exhaustion signature. Notably, the co-stimulatory factor GITR (encoded by TNFRSF18) is highly expressed not only on immunosuppressive regulatory T (Treg) cells but also on exhausted CD8 TILs. GITR agonism via αGITR antibody achieved dual effects: it directly enhanced CD8 TIL activation while simultaneously abrogating Treg-mediated immunosuppression. This dual-action mechanism synergized with αPD-1 therapy to amplify TIL reactivation, significantly enhancing tumor control in vivo. Mechanistically, GITR activation potentiated anti-tumor responses by promoting immunological synapse (IS) formation and function in TILs via the NF-κB/KALRN signaling axis. Our findings established GITR as a crucial regulator of CD8 TIL anti-tumor immunity, positioning GITR targeting as a novel strategy to improve TIL therapy for glioblastoma, with promising implications for clinical application.

> **中文摘要：**
> 自体肿瘤浸润淋巴细胞（TIL）疗法对实体瘤具有变革性潜力，但其在胶质母细胞瘤中的疗效仍受限于T细胞耗竭和免疫抑制。在本研究中，我们优化了一种有效且可靠的体外扩增胶质母细胞瘤病灶TIL的方法，并在体外和体内评估了其肿瘤杀伤能力。对扩增TIL的单细胞RNA测序（scRNA-seq）揭示了其异质性，并鉴定出一个具有独特耗竭特征的细胞毒性组织驻留记忆（TRM）CD8 TIL亚群。值得注意的是，共刺激因子GITR（由TNFRSF18编码）不仅在免疫抑制性调节性T（Treg）细胞上高表达，也在耗竭的CD8 TIL上高表达。通过αGITR抗体进行的GITR激动实现了双重效应：它直接增强了CD8 TIL的活化，同时消除了Treg介导的免疫抑制。这种双重作用机制与αPD-1疗法协同作用，放大了TIL的再活化，显著增强了体内肿瘤控制。从机制上讲，GITR激活通过NF-κB/KALRN信号轴促进TIL中免疫突触（IS）的形成和功能，从而增强了抗肿瘤反应。我们的研究结果确立了GITR是CD8 TIL抗肿瘤免疫的关键调节因子，将靶向GITR定位为改善胶质母细胞瘤TIL疗法的新策略，具有广阔的临床应用前景。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在克服胶质母细胞瘤TIL疗法中T细胞耗竭与免疫抑制的瓶颈。研究者通过优化TIL体外扩增方法，结合单细胞测序鉴定出具有独特耗竭特征的CD8 TRM亚群，并创新性地发现GITR在耗竭CD8 TIL和Treg上均高表达。核心发现是GITR激动剂具有双重作用机制——直接激活CD8 TIL并抑制Treg功能，且能与PD-1阻断协同增效，其下游通过NF-κB/KALRN轴促进免疫突触形成。该研究创新性地将GITR靶向定位为增强TIL疗法的新策略，机制阐述清晰，但结论主要基于临床前模型，其人体安全性与疗效仍需临床试验验证。

---

## 20. 银杏双黄酮靶向GRP78，诱导骨肉瘤内质网应激与免疫激活的双重通路。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776050)
**期刊：** Oncogene
**PMID：** 41776050
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41388-026-03704-0

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Ginkgetin targets GRP78 to induce dual pathways of ER stress and immune activation in osteosarcoma.

> **英文摘要：**
> Osteosarcoma is an aggressive malignancy characterized by rapid proliferation and a propensity for metastasis. The endoplasmic reticulum (ER) chaperone GRP78, a critical regulator of osteosarcoma progression, represents a promising therapeutic target. In this study, we identified the natural compound ginkgetin (Gink) as a novel GRP78 inhibitor. Cellular thermal shift assays, surface plasmon resonance, and mutagenesis studies revealed that Gink directly binds to GRP78, with K296 serving as a key interaction site. In vitro, Gink suppressed osteosarcoma cell proliferation, migration, and invasion while inducing apoptosis and autophagy by activating the PERK-eIF2α-ATF4 pathway. Co-immunoprecipitation assays showed that Gink competitively disrupted GRP78-PERK interaction. In orthotopic and patient-derived xenograft models, Gink treatment markedly attenuated tumor growth and metastasis. Gink also reprogrammed the tumor immune microenvironment by reducing M2 macrophage polarization and synergizing with anti-PD1 therapy to enhance CD8 T-cell activity. Accordingly, Gink could be developed as a GRP78-targeting agent that triggers ER stress and immune activation, offering a dual-pronged therapeutic strategy against osteosarcoma. Ginkgetin (Gink) directly binds to GRP78 in a competitive manner, disrupting the interaction between GRP78 and PERK. This leads to PERK activation and phosphorylation, which in turn phosphorylates eIF2α to trigger ATF4 transcription. Ultimately, this cascade induces apoptosis and autophagy, inhibiting cancer progression. Additionally, Gink suppresses M2 macrophage polarization and enhances CD8 T cell cytotoxicity, both of which contribute to the prevention of cancer development.

> **中文摘要：**
> 骨肉瘤是一种侵袭性恶性肿瘤，以快速增殖和易转移为特征。内质网（ER）伴侣蛋白GRP78是骨肉瘤进展的关键调节因子，是一个有前景的治疗靶点。本研究鉴定出天然化合物银杏双黄酮（Gink）是一种新型的GRP78抑制剂。细胞热位移分析、表面等离子共振和诱变研究表明，Gink直接结合GRP78，其中K296是关键相互作用位点。在体外，Gink通过激活PERK-eIF2α-ATF4通路，抑制骨肉瘤细胞增殖、迁移和侵袭，同时诱导细胞凋亡和自噬。免疫共沉淀实验表明，Gink竞争性地破坏了GRP78与PERK的相互作用。在原位和患者来源的异种移植模型中，Gink治疗显著减弱了肿瘤生长和转移。Gink还通过减少M2巨噬细胞极化，并与抗PD1疗法协同增强CD8 T细胞活性，从而重编程了肿瘤免疫微环境。因此，Gink可被开发为一种靶向GRP78的药物，既能触发内质网应激，又能激活免疫，为骨肉瘤提供一种双管齐下的治疗策略。银杏双黄酮（Gink）以竞争性方式直接结合GRP78，破坏GRP78与PERK之间的相互作用。这导致PERK激活和磷酸化，进而磷酸化eIF2α以触发ATF4转录。最终，这一级联反应诱导细胞凋亡和自噬，抑制癌症进展。此外，Gink抑制M2巨噬细胞极化并增强CD8 T细胞毒性，两者均有助于预防癌症发展。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索天然化合物银杏双黄酮（Gink）作为GRP78抑制剂在骨肉瘤治疗中的双重作用机制。研究综合运用了分子互作验证（如CETSA、SPR）、细胞功能实验以及体内模型，严谨地证实了Gink通过竞争性结合GRP78的K296位点，解除其对PERK的抑制，从而激活PERK-eIF2α-ATF4通路诱导内质网应激相关的细胞凋亡与自噬。其创新性在于不仅阐明了Gink直接靶向GRP78的抗肿瘤细胞自主效应，更揭示了其重塑肿瘤免疫微环境（抑制M2极化、协同抗PD1疗法）的免疫调节功能，为开发“靶向治疗+免疫调节”的联合策略提供了新思路。然而，摘要未提及该化合物的体内毒性数据及潜在脱靶效应，其临床转化潜力仍需进一步评估。

---

## 21. L1TD1通过增强ABCC3 mRNA稳定性促进结直肠黏液腺癌进展。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41776049)
**期刊：** Oncogene
**PMID：** 41776049
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41388-026-03716-w

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** L1TD1 promotes colorectal mucinous adenocarcinoma progression by enhancing ABCC3 mRNA stability.

> **英文摘要：**
> Colorectal mucinous adenocarcinoma (MAC), a distinct subtype of adenocarcinoma (AC) characterized by extracellular mucus production. However, the specific regulatory role of mucus production in MAC development remains underexplored. In this study, scRNA-seq analyses revealed that L1TD1 expression was significantly greater in MAC than in adjacent noncancerous tissues. L1TD1 is an RNA-binding protein that has been reported to regulate mRNA stability and stemness-associated transcriptional programs in cancer cells. Further experiments confirmed that L1TD1 expression was elevated in MAC compared to normal tissues and L1TD1 promoted mucus production and accelerated tumor cell proliferation and metastasis. Mechanistically, further analysis revealed the RNA recognition motif (RRM) domain of L1TD1 binds to the 3' untranslated region (3'-UTR) of ABCC3 mRNA, thus increasing its stability. In addition, ABCC3 inhibition reversed L1TD1 overexpression-induced mucus production and MAC progression. Collectively our findings demonstrate that L1TD1 binds to the GUGU motif within ABCC3 mRNA and upregulates ABCC3 expression, which subsequently activates the MAPK signaling pathway and promotes mucin production and accelerates MAC progression. These results also provide essential evidence for investigating the mechanisms of mucus production and tumor progression in MAC.

> **中文摘要：**
> 结直肠黏液腺癌（MAC）是腺癌（AC）的一种独特亚型，其特征是细胞外黏液产生。然而，黏液产生在MAC发展中的具体调控作用仍未得到充分探索。本研究通过单细胞RNA测序分析发现，L1TD1在MAC中的表达显著高于癌旁非癌组织。L1TD1是一种RNA结合蛋白，据报道可调节癌细胞的mRNA稳定性和干性相关转录程序。进一步的实验证实，与正常组织相比，L1TD1在MAC中表达升高，并且L1TD1促进了黏液产生，加速了肿瘤细胞的增殖和转移。机制上，进一步分析揭示L1TD1的RNA识别基序（RRM）结构域与ABCC3 mRNA的3'非翻译区（3'-UTR）结合，从而增加其稳定性。此外，抑制ABCC3逆转了L1TD1过表达诱导的黏液产生和MAC进展。总之，我们的研究结果表明，L1TD1结合ABCC3 mRNA内的GUGU基序并上调ABCC3表达，随后激活MAPK信号通路，促进黏蛋白产生并加速MAC进展。这些结果也为研究MAC中黏液产生和肿瘤进展的机制提供了重要证据。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明RNA结合蛋白L1TD1在结直肠黏液腺癌（MAC）进展中的具体作用机制。研究综合运用单细胞测序、功能实验和分子机制分析，发现L1TD1通过其RRM结构域结合并稳定ABCC3 mRNA，进而激活MAPK通路，驱动黏液产生和肿瘤恶性进展。其创新性在于首次揭示了L1TD1-ABCC3轴调控MAC黏液表型的分子通路，为这一特殊亚型提供了潜在治疗靶点。局限性在于研究主要基于细胞和动物模型，其临床转化价值及在MAC患者中的普遍性仍需进一步验证。

---

## 22. 脂肪组织中的GPR146驱动脂肪-肝脏互作并促进小鼠肝脏脂肪变性。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775759)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41775759
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70136-5

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** GPR146 in adipose tissue drives adipose-liver crosstalk and promotes hepatic steatosis in mice.

> **英文摘要：**
> The limited therapeutic options for metabolic dysfunction-associated steatotic liver disease (MASLD) underscore the need for deeper mechanistic insight and new treatment strategies. Here, we identify the orphan G protein-coupled receptor GPR146 as a regulator of hepatic steatosis through adipose-liver crosstalk. Human genetic analyses link the GPR146 locus to circulating markers of liver injury and inflammation. In mice, both constitutive and acute GPR146 depletion protect against diet-induced obesity and hepatic steatosis. Notably, adipose-specific, but not liver-specific, GPR146 deletion reduces hepatic lipid accumulation by limiting free fatty acid (FFA) influx. Mechanistically, GPR146 promotes adipogenesis in preadipocytes via Gαq-PKC-AKT signaling, increasing lipid storage capacity, and enhances lipolysis in mature adipocytes through ERK activation, elevating circulating FFA. Together, these coordinated actions increase FFA delivery to the liver, promoting triglyceride accumulation. Our findings establish GPR146 as a pleiotropic regulator of adipose tissue biology and a potential therapeutic target for MASLD.

> **中文摘要：**
> 代谢功能障碍相关脂肪性肝病（MASLD）的有限治疗选择，凸显了对更深入机制见解和新治疗策略的需求。本研究通过脂肪-肝脏互作，鉴定出孤儿G蛋白偶联受体GPR146是肝脏脂肪变性的一个调节因子。人类遗传学分析将GPR146基因座与循环中的肝损伤和炎症标志物联系起来。在小鼠中，无论是组成性还是急性敲除GPR146，均能防止饮食诱导的肥胖和肝脏脂肪变性。值得注意的是，脂肪组织特异性（而非肝脏特异性）敲除GPR146通过限制游离脂肪酸（FFA）的流入，减少了肝脏脂质积累。从机制上讲，GPR146通过Gαq-PKC-AKT信号通路促进前脂肪细胞的脂肪生成，增加脂质储存能力；并通过激活ERK增强成熟脂肪细胞的脂解作用，从而升高循环FFA水平。这些协同作用共同增加了FFA向肝脏的输送，促进了甘油三酯的积累。我们的研究结果确立了GPR146是脂肪组织生物学的一个多效性调节因子，也是MASLD的一个潜在治疗靶点。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索代谢功能障碍相关脂肪性肝病（MASLD）的新机制与治疗靶点。通过整合人类遗传学分析、小鼠基因敲除模型及组织特异性功能研究，作者系统揭示了孤儿受体GPR146在脂肪-肝脏轴中的关键作用。其核心发现是，脂肪组织中的GPR146通过双重机制——促进前脂肪细胞分化以增加储脂能力，同时增强成熟脂肪细胞脂解以释放游离脂肪酸——共同驱动肝脏脂肪变性。该研究的创新性在于明确了GPR146的组织特异性功能及其多效性调控网络，为靶向脂肪组织干预肝脏疾病提供了新思路；局限性在于主要基于小鼠模型，其在人类病理中的精确作用及靶向治疗的可行性仍需进一步临床前及临床研究验证。

---

## 23. 有丝分裂中的微同源介导的断裂诱导复制促进染色体合成。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775729)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41775729
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70086-y

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Mitotic microhomology-mediated break-induced replication promotes chromoanasynthesis.

> **英文摘要：**
> Chromoanasynthesis is a form of complex chromosomal rearrangement (CCR) commonly detected in cancers and congenital disorders, but the mechanism underlying its generation remain elusive. Here we develop a single-molecule long-read DNA sequencing approach to characterise ultra-complex mutational events, consistent with chromoanasynthesis, occurring at shortened telomeres and sub-telomeric DNA double-strand breaks in human cells. Our data reveal that chromoanasynthesis is generated by microhomology-mediated break-induced replication (MM-BIR), occurring specifically in mitosis. Surprisingly, this mitotic pathway involves a collaboration between microhomology-mediated end-joining (MMEJ) and BIR, where MMEJ proteins initiate a Polδ-dependent BIR pathway that is regulated by PIF1, POLD3 and PCNA. This pathway is highly prone to template switching and can generate dramatic amplification of genomic loci in a single event. Our findings help explain the extreme mutagenic nature of chromoanasynthesis and establish mitotic MM-BIR as a key driver of CCRs, with important implications for the origin of cancers and congenital disorders.

> **中文摘要：**
> 染色体合成是一种常见于癌症和先天性疾病中的复杂染色体重排形式，但其产生的机制尚不清楚。本研究开发了一种单分子长读长DNA测序方法，用于表征人类细胞中发生在端粒缩短和亚端粒DNA双链断裂处的、与染色体合成一致的超复杂突变事件。我们的数据显示，染色体合成是由微同源介导的断裂诱导复制（MM-BIR）产生的，并且特异性地发生在有丝分裂中。令人惊讶的是，这一有丝分裂途径涉及微同源介导的末端连接（MMEJ）与BIR之间的协作，其中MMEJ蛋白启动了一个由PIF1、POLD3和PCNA调控的、依赖于Polδ的BIR通路。该通路极易发生模板转换，并能在单一事件中导致基因组位点的剧烈扩增。我们的发现有助于解释染色体合成的极端致突变性，并将有丝分裂MM-BIR确立为复杂染色体重排的关键驱动因素，这对理解癌症和先天性疾病的发生具有重要意义。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在揭示染色体合成这一复杂染色体重排的分子机制。作者创新性地开发了单分子长读长测序方法，精准捕捉了端粒区域发生的超复杂突变事件。核心发现是，染色体合成由特异于有丝分裂的微同源介导断裂诱导复制（MM-BIR）驱动，该通路整合了MMEJ与BIR，并由PIF1、POLD3和PCNA调控，具有高度的模板转换倾向和基因组扩增能力。这一发现从根本上解释了染色体合成高度致突变的特性，将MM-BIR确立为癌症和先天性疾病中复杂重排的关键机制，具有重要理论价值；但研究主要基于体外细胞模型，其在体内生理或病理环境中的普遍性和调控细节仍需进一步探索。

---

## 24. 克隆进化分析揭示胰腺导管内乳头状黏液性肿瘤恶性转化的模式

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775703)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41775703
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-69762-w

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Clonal evolutionary analysis reveals patterns of malignant transformation of Intraductal Papillary Mucinous Neoplasms of the pancreas.

> **英文摘要：**
> Intraductal papillary mucinous neoplasms (IPMNs) are critical precursors to pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma, a highly lethal cancer characterized by late detection and rapid progression. Here we integrate multi-region whole-genome and transcriptome sequencing to trace the evolution of IPMN, constructing detailed phylogenetic trees to provide insights into subclonal architectures and progression pathways. Our analysis identifies two distinct evolutionary trajectories: one driven by a single ancestral clone, and another involving multiple independent ancestral clones. We further explore the roles of mutational signatures and structural variants in promoting clonal evolution and the emergence of new subclones. Complementing these genomic findings, our transcriptomic analysis reveals unique gene expression profiles and variations in the immune landscape that correlate with different progression stages of IPMN. These insights reveal the complex molecular dynamics of IPMN heterogeneity and progression, highlighting the need to refine early detection and treatment strategies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 导管内乳头状黏液性肿瘤（IPMNs）是胰腺导管腺癌的关键前体病变，后者是一种以发现晚、进展快为特征的高度致死性癌症。本研究整合了多区域全基因组和转录组测序技术，以追踪IPMN的进化过程，构建了详细的系统发育树，从而深入解析其亚克隆结构和进展路径。我们的分析识别出两种不同的进化轨迹：一种由单一祖细胞克隆驱动，另一种则涉及多个独立的祖细胞克隆。我们进一步探讨了突变特征和结构变异在促进克隆进化及新亚克隆出现中的作用。作为基因组发现的补充，我们的转录组分析揭示了与IPMN不同进展阶段相关的独特基因表达谱和免疫微环境变化。这些发现揭示了IPMN异质性和进展的复杂分子动力学，强调了改进早期检测和治疗策略的必要性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过多组学整合分析，深入解析胰腺导管内乳头状黏液性肿瘤（IPMN）向胰腺癌恶性转化的克隆进化模式。其核心方法在于结合多区域全基因组与转录组测序，构建高分辨率的系统发育树。主要发现是识别出单克隆起源与多克隆起源两种不同的进化轨迹，并揭示了驱动克隆进化的基因组特征（如突变特征、结构变异）及伴随的转录组与免疫微环境变化。该研究的创新性在于从时间和空间维度系统描绘了IPMN的分子进化全景，为理解其异质性提供了新框架；局限性可能在于样本量、对特定驱动事件的验证深度，以及将发现转化为临床可操作标志物的距离。

---

## 25. 转录因子ZMYM3通过上调CTTN并诱导侵袭伪足形成促进肝细胞癌转移。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775697)
**期刊：** Cell death & disease
**PMID：** 41775697
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41419-026-08506-6

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Transcriptional factor ZMYM3 promotes hepatocellular carcinoma metastasis by upregulating CTTN and inducing invadopodia formation.

> **英文摘要：**
> Hepatocellular carcinoma (HCC) is characterized by high invasiveness and metastatic potential, leading to poor prognosis. Therefore, understanding the molecular mechanisms underlying HCC invasion and metastasis is essential for developing effective therapeutic strategies. This study investigates the role of ZMYM3 in HCC invasion and metastasis. Analysis of The Cancer Genome Atlas (TCGA) and Gene Expression Omnibus (GEO) datasets, along with immunohistochemistry, revealed that ZMYM3 is upregulated in HCC tissues and associated with recurrence and poor prognosis. Single-cell sequencing data indicated higher ZMYM3 expression in portal vein tumor thrombus compared to primary lesions, suggesting its involvement in metastasis. Functional assays demonstrated that ZMYM3 enhances HCC cell proliferation, invasion, and metastasis. RNA sequencing identified that ZMYM3 promotes invadopodia formation and epithelial-mesenchymal transition (EMT) in HCC cells. Further chromatin immunoprecipitation sequencing and mechanistic studies showed that ZMYM3 directly binds to the promoter of CTTN, a key gene regulating invadopodia formation, thereby increasing its expression. This upregulation contributes to the enhanced invasive and metastatic capabilities of HCC cells. Our findings identify ZMYM3 overexpression as a predictor of high recurrence risk and poor prognosis in HCC patients. Mechanistically, ZMYM3 promotes invadopodia formation primarily through the upregulation of CTTN, thereby augmenting the invasive and metastatic potential of HCC cells. These results highlight the critical role of ZMYM3 in HCC progression and metastasis.ZMYM3 promotes hepatocellular carcinoma metastasis by upregulating CTTN and inducing invadopodia formation.

> **中文摘要：**
> 肝细胞癌（HCC）具有高侵袭性和转移潜能的特点，导致预后不良。因此，理解HCC侵袭和转移的分子机制对于制定有效的治疗策略至关重要。本研究探讨了ZMYM3在HCC侵袭和转移中的作用。通过对癌症基因组图谱（TCGA）和基因表达综合（GEO）数据集的分析以及免疫组织化学染色，发现ZMYM3在HCC组织中表达上调，并与复发和不良预后相关。单细胞测序数据显示，与原发性病灶相比，门静脉癌栓中的ZMYM3表达更高，提示其参与转移过程。功能实验证明，ZMYM3增强了HCC细胞的增殖、侵袭和转移能力。RNA测序发现，ZMYM3促进了HCC细胞中侵袭伪足的形成和上皮-间质转化（EMT）。进一步的染色质免疫共沉淀测序和机制研究表明，ZMYM3直接结合到CTTN（一个调控侵袭伪足形成的关键基因）的启动子区域，从而增加其表达。这种上调促进了HCC细胞侵袭和转移能力的增强。我们的研究结果确定ZMYM3过表达是HCC患者高复发风险和不良预后的预测因子。从机制上讲，ZMYM3主要通过上调CTTN来促进侵袭伪足的形成，从而增强HCC细胞的侵袭和转移潜能。这些结果突显了ZMYM3在HCC进展和转移中的关键作用。ZMYM3通过上调CTTN并诱导侵袭伪足形成促进肝细胞癌转移。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明转录因子ZMYM3在肝细胞癌（HCC）侵袭转移中的功能和机制。研究团队整合了TCGA、GEO等多组学数据库分析、单细胞测序、体外功能实验以及染色质免疫共沉淀测序（ChIP-seq）等多种技术手段。核心发现是ZMYM3通过直接转录激活CTTN基因，促进侵袭伪足形成和上皮-间质转化（EMT），从而驱动HCC转移。其创新性在于首次揭示了ZMYM3-CTTN轴在HCC转移中的关键作用，为预后判断提供了新的生物标志物。局限性在于研究主要基于临床数据和体外实验，其体内转移促进作用和作为治疗靶点的潜力有待进一步的动物模型和临床前研究验证。

---

## 26. 间充质基质细胞通过PGE2/cAMP信号通路调控人造血干细胞的存活与再生。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775691)
**期刊：** Cell death & disease
**PMID：** 41775691
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41419-026-08502-w

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Mesenchymal stromal cells modulate survival and regeneration of human hematopoietic stem cells via PGE2/cAMP signaling.

> **英文摘要：**
> Ionizing radiation and chemotherapy significantly impair hematopoietic stem and progenitor cell (HSPC) function, increasing the risk of bone marrow failure and secondary malignancies. Mesenchymal stromal cells (MSCs), critical regulators within the hematopoietic niche, maintain HSPC quiescence, self-renewal, survival, and differentiation. However, the specific pro-regenerative signaling pathways activated by MSCs in human HSPCs remain incompletely defined. Here, we show that bone marrow-derived MSCs effectively suppress irradiation-induced apoptosis and preserve the in vivo repopulation capacity of human HSPCs. Transcriptomic analysis of HSPCs revealed a pronounced upregulation of CREB target genes following MSC co-culture, consistent with increased activation of the cAMP/CREB signaling pathway. Mechanistically, MSC-secreted prostaglandin E2 (PGE2) emerged as a key mediator of cAMP induced response in HSPCs. Notably, the protective effect of Forskolin/IBMX persisted for up to 72 hours post-irradiation and significantly enhanced HSPC self-renewal. At the molecular level, we revealed reduced pro-apoptotic ASPP1 and PUMA expression, elevated p21 and stabilized anti-apoptotic MCL1 and BCL-XL proteins in human HSPCs treated with cAMP pathway agonists. Overall, our findings highlight the pivotal role of PGE2/cAMP/CREB signaling axis as a central mediator of MSC-mediated protection of human HSPCs under genotoxic stress and identify pharmacological cAMP activation as a promising strategy to protect human HSPCs against DNA damage-induced hematotoxicity.

> **中文摘要：**
> 电离辐射和化疗会显著损害造血干细胞和祖细胞（HSPC）的功能，增加骨髓衰竭和继发性恶性肿瘤的风险。间充质基质细胞（MSCs）作为造血微环境中的关键调节因子，维持着HSPC的静息、自我更新、存活和分化。然而，MSCs在人HSPC中激活的具体促再生信号通路仍未完全阐明。本研究显示，骨髓来源的MSCs能有效抑制辐射诱导的细胞凋亡，并保留人HSPC的体内重建能力。对HSPC的转录组学分析显示，在与MSCs共培养后，CREB靶基因显著上调，这与cAMP/CREB信号通路激活增强相一致。从机制上讲，MSC分泌的前列腺素E2（PGE2）是HSPC中cAMP诱导反应的关键介质。值得注意的是，Forskolin/IBMX的保护作用在辐射后可持续长达72小时，并显著增强了HSPC的自我更新能力。在分子水平上，我们发现在经cAMP通路激动剂处理的人HSPC中，促凋亡蛋白ASPP1和PUMA的表达降低，p21表达升高，而抗凋亡蛋白MCL1和BCL-XL则趋于稳定。总之，我们的研究结果强调了PGE2/cAMP/CREB信号轴作为MSCs在基因毒性应激下保护人HSPC的核心介质的关键作用，并指出药理性激活cAMP是保护人HSPC免受DNA损伤诱导的血液毒性的一个有前景的策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明间充质基质细胞（MSCs）保护人造血干细胞（HSPCs）免受基因毒性损伤的具体分子机制。通过共培养、转录组分析和分子生物学实验，研究者发现MSCs通过分泌PGE2激活HSPCs内的cAMP/CREB信号轴，从而抑制凋亡、促进自我更新并维持其体内重建能力。其创新性在于系统揭示了PGE2/cAMP/CREB这一核心信号通路在MSC介导的辐射防护中的作用，并提出了药理性激活cAMP作为潜在治疗策略。然而，研究主要基于体外和动物模型，其临床转化效果及长期安全性仍需进一步验证。

## 27. 长链非编码RNA ADEI/miR-93-3p/STAT3轴通过调控PD-1/PD-L1检查点促进EB病毒阳性弥漫大B细胞淋巴瘤进展与免疫逃逸。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775689)
**期刊：** Cell death & disease
**PMID：** 41775689
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41419-026-08532-4

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Long noncoding RNA ADEI/miR-93-3p/STAT3 axis promotes Epstein-Barr virus-positive diffuse large B-cell lymphoma progression and immune evasion through regulating the PD-1/PD-L1 checkpoint.

> **英文摘要：**
> Epstein-Barr virus (EBV) is an important pathogenic factor of lymphoma; EBV+diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) has a worse prognosis with standard chemotherapy than EBV-DLBCL. Long noncoding (Lnc)-RNAs are key regulators of cancer pathways and biomarkers of disease. As natural protective carriers of noncoding RNAs, exosomes can stably transmit signals during tumor development. We explored the role of exosomal lncRNAs in the occurrence and development of EBV-related DLBCL. In this study, we identified a novel lncRNA lncADEI, which was upregulated in EBV + DLBCL and was positively correlated with DLBCL cell proliferation and clonogenesis. LncADEI positively regulated STAT3 via miR-93-3P, and STAT3 transcriptionally activated programmed death ligand-1 to promote immune evasion of DLBCL cells. LncADEI could be transferred by exosomes and promote the proliferation and immune evasion of DLBCL. LncADEI was highly expressed in serum exosomes from EBV + DLBCL patients and was associated with worse clinicopathological features. In conclusion, lncADEI participated in the progression and immune evasion of EBV + DLBCL and was differentially expressed in serumal exosomes. LncADEI may be a promising strategy for treating EBV-associated lymphoid malignancies.

> **中文摘要：**
> EB病毒（EBV）是淋巴瘤的重要致病因子；EBV阳性弥漫大B细胞淋巴瘤（DLBCL）在接受标准化疗时预后比EBV阴性DLBCL更差。长链非编码RNA是癌症通路的关键调控因子和疾病生物标志物。作为非编码RNA的天然保护性载体，外泌体可在肿瘤发展过程中稳定传递信号。我们探讨了外泌体lncRNA在EBV相关DLBCL发生发展中的作用。本研究鉴定出一种新型lncRNA lncADEI，它在EBV阳性DLBCL中表达上调，并与DLBCL细胞增殖和克隆形成能力呈正相关。LncADEI通过miR-93-3P正向调控STAT3，而STAT3转录激活程序性死亡配体-1，从而促进DLBCL细胞的免疫逃逸。LncADEI可被外泌体转移，并促进DLBCL的增殖和免疫逃逸。LncADEI在EBV阳性DLBCL患者的血清外泌体中高表达，并与更差的临床病理特征相关。总之，lncADEI参与了EBV阳性DLBCL的进展和免疫逃逸，并在血清外泌体中差异表达。LncADEI可能是治疗EBV相关淋巴系统恶性肿瘤的一个有前景的策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索外泌体lncRNA在EBV阳性DLBCL中的作用机制。通过鉴定并验证新型lncRNA lncADEI，揭示了其通过miR-93-3p/STAT3轴调控PD-L1表达，从而驱动肿瘤增殖与免疫逃逸的分子通路。创新性地将外泌体信号传递、lncRNA调控网络与免疫检查点联系起来，并提示血清外泌体lncADEI作为潜在生物标志物和治疗靶点。局限性在于研究主要基于细胞和患者样本关联分析，其具体的体内功能、临床转化价值及与其他信号通路的交互作用有待进一步实验验证。

## 28. 利用网膜转移灶中脂质驱动的免疫代谢通路以增强卵巢癌患者的免疫治疗效果。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775684)
**期刊：** Signal transduction and targeted therapy
**PMID：** 41775684
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41392-026-02594-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Harnessing lipid-driven immunometabolic pathways in omental metastases to enhance immunotherapy in patients with ovarian cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Immunotherapy with immune checkpoint blockade (ICB) in epithelial ovarian carcinoma (EOC) shows limited clinical benefit only for a small subset of patients. Overall response rates are low, so that overcoming immunotherapy resistance and improved stratification are key. In this study, we investigated the immunometabolic landscape of EOC with a focus on omental metastases, identifying lipid-laden macrophages as central elements for actionable therapeutic vulnerabilities and giving rise to biomarkers for improved patient stratification. Using patient-derived explants, we demonstrated a functional dichotomy inside the typically lipid-rich microenvironment of omental metastases: augmented maintenance of effector T cell function, while lipid uptake and processing by tumor-associated macrophages (TAMs) induces oxidative stress-dependent signaling programs, which drive macrophage dysfunction and immune suppression. Pharmacological modulation of lipid-driven signaling pathways through CCR5 inhibition (inflammation modulation through maraviroc) or blockade of the lipid scavenger receptor CD36 reprograms TAMs, restores T cell activity, and enhances antitumor immune responses within lipid-rich tumor niches. Mechanistically, studies in humanized mouse models reveal that maraviroc-mediated CCR5 inhibition induces transcriptional programs associated with immune activation in stressed, lipid-laden human TAMs. Consistent with these mechanistic insights, we demonstrated that the specific immunometabolic niche in omental metastases is clinically associated with responsiveness to ICB. We propose a non-invasive radiomics and machine-learning-based analysis of imaging data to assess omental involvement for patient stratification.

> **中文摘要：**
> 免疫检查点阻断（ICB）疗法在上皮性卵巢癌（EOC）中仅对一小部分患者显示出有限的临床获益。总体缓解率较低，因此克服免疫治疗耐药性和改善患者分层是关键。本研究聚焦于网膜转移灶，探究了EOC的免疫代谢特征，发现脂质富集的巨噬细胞是潜在治疗靶点的核心要素，并可衍生出用于改善患者分层的生物标志物。利用患者来源的组织外植体，我们证明了在网膜转移灶典型的脂质丰富微环境中存在功能二分性：一方面效应T细胞功能得以增强维持，另一方面肿瘤相关巨噬细胞（TAMs）对脂质的摄取和处理会诱导氧化应激依赖性信号通路，从而驱动巨噬细胞功能障碍和免疫抑制。通过CCR5抑制（使用马拉韦罗调节炎症）或阻断脂质清道夫受体CD36来对脂质驱动信号通路进行药理学调控，可重编程TAMs、恢复T细胞活性，并增强脂质丰富肿瘤微环境内的抗肿瘤免疫应答。机制上，在人源化小鼠模型中的研究表明，马拉韦罗介导的CCR5抑制能在处于应激状态、脂质富集的人源TAMs中诱导与免疫激活相关的转录程序。与这些机制见解一致，我们证明了网膜转移灶中特定的免疫代谢微环境在临床上与对ICB的应答性相关。我们提出了一种基于影像组学和机器学习的非侵入性影像数据分析方法，以评估网膜受累情况，用于患者分层。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过靶向脂质驱动的免疫代谢通路，克服卵巢癌网膜转移灶对免疫检查点阻断（ICB）的耐药性。研究团队综合运用患者组织外植体、人源化小鼠模型及药理学干预，揭示了脂质富集微环境中巨噬细胞功能失调的核心机制，并验证了CCR5抑制剂（马拉韦罗）和CD36阻断剂的重编程潜力。其创新性在于将基础免疫代谢机制与临床转化（如患者分层）紧密结合，并提出了利用影像组学进行无创评估的策略；局限性在于所提出的治疗策略和分层方法仍需在前瞻性临床试验中得到进一步验证。

---

## 29. SHP2上的一个热点磷酸化位点驱动癌蛋白激活与耐药性。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775683)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41775683
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70060-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A hotspot phosphorylation site on SHP2 drives oncoprotein activation and drug resistance.

> **英文摘要：**
> SHP2 is a phosphatase and a critical mediator of receptor tyrosine kinase (RTK)-driven RAS/mitogen-activated protein kinase (MAPK) signaling. Despite promising preclinical data, SHP2 inhibitors have shown minimal clinical efficacy, with no defined clinical mechanisms of primary resistance. Here, we elucidate phosphorylation of SHP2 at tyrosine 62 (pY62) as a hotspot phosphorylation site in the proteome and RTK-driven tumor types in patients. We demonstrate that SRC family kinases directly phosphorylate SHP2 at Y62, downstream of but not directly phosphorylated by RTKs. Using biochemical and biophysical analyses, we show that SHP2 enforces an open, active conformation, resulting in constitutive phosphatase activation that is sufficient to activate MAPK signaling and confer resistance to allosteric SHP2 inhibitors. These findings establish that SHP2 pY62 is a phosphorylation hotspot phenocopying mutational activation, a mechanism of primary resistance to SHP2 inhibitors, and a cancer drug target distinct from wildtype SHP2.

> **中文摘要：**
> SHP2是一种磷酸酶，也是受体酪氨酸激酶（RTK）驱动的RAS/丝裂原活化蛋白激酶（MAPK）信号通路的关键介质。尽管临床前数据令人鼓舞，但SHP2抑制剂在临床上疗效甚微，且其原发性耐药的临床机制尚未明确。在此，我们阐明SHP2酪氨酸62位点（pY62）的磷酸化是蛋白质组和患者RTK驱动肿瘤类型中的一个热点磷酸化位点。我们证明SRC家族激酶直接在Y62位点磷酸化SHP2，该过程位于RTKs下游，但并非由RTKs直接磷酸化。通过生化和生物物理分析，我们发现pY62迫使SHP2形成开放的、活跃的构象，导致其组成型磷酸酶激活，这足以激活MAPK信号通路并赋予对变构SHP2抑制剂的耐药性。这些发现证实，SHP2 pY62是一个模拟突变激活的磷酸化热点，是SHP2抑制剂原发性耐药的一种机制，也是一个不同于野生型SHP2的癌症药物靶点。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明SHP2抑制剂临床疗效不佳的机制。通过识别酪氨酸62位点（Y62）为患者肿瘤中的磷酸化热点，并揭示SRC家族激酶介导的磷酸化事件，研究团队从临床现象回溯至分子机制。核心发现是pY62通过诱导SHP2构象改变，使其组成型激活，从而驱动MAPK信号并导致对变构抑制剂的耐药。这一发现创新性地将翻译后修饰（磷酸化）与致癌突变的功能后果（组成型激活）联系起来，不仅揭示了原发性耐药的新机制，还提出了pY62-SHP2作为独立于野生型蛋白的新治疗靶点。局限性在于，研究主要基于生化与生物物理分析，其在体内肿瘤模型和更广泛癌症类型中的普适性及临床转化潜力仍需进一步验证。

---

## 30. 靶向共享非突变抗原和共享突变BRAF新抗原的黑色素瘤疫苗联合激动型CD40抗体（CDX-1140）与TLR3激动剂（poly-ICLC）的I/II期临床试验。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775435)
**期刊：** Journal for immunotherapy of cancer
**PMID：** 41775435
**DOI：** 10.1136/jitc-2025-013613

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Phase I/II clinical trial of a melanoma vaccine targeting shared non-mutated antigens and a shared mutated BRAF neoantigen with an agonistic CD40 antibody (CDX-1140) plus TLR3 agonist (poly-ICLC).

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: For patients with high-risk melanoma who are unresponsive or intolerant to immune checkpoint inhibitors, cancer vaccines may provide benefit with a favorable toxicity profile. CD4 T cells provide essential help to dendritic cells (DCs) for optimal CD8 T cell priming in the antitumor response, and induction of tumor-cognate CD4 T cell responses may enhance vaccine efficacy. We report on a first-in-human approach to treat patients with high-risk melanoma using a vaccine composed of six non-mutated melanoma-specific helper peptides (6MHP) and a shared mutated BRAF-V600E neoantigen helper peptide (mBRAF) co-administered locally with a TLR3 agonist (poly-ICLC) and agonistic CD40 antibody (CDX-1140).
> 
> METHODS: Adults with high-risk melanoma arising from cutaneous, mucosal, or ocular primary sites who were rendered clinically free of disease after definitive treatment were enrolled to this nonrandomized phase I/II trial (NCT04364230) designed to assess safety and immunogenicity. Participants received vaccine (6MHP+mBRAF+poly-ICLC) with a dose-escalation allocation of CDX-1140 into the vaccine mixture at one of four dose levels (50, 200, 800, 3000 μg). Vaccines were administered at 3-week intervals for four doses. Primary endpoints were safety and peripheral CD4 T cell response. Exploratory analysis to characterize the vaccine site microenvironment was performed.
> 
> RESULTS: Of 22 eligible participants, 11 (50%) had ocular melanoma. Sixteen (73%) received the maximum CDX-1140 dose. Toxicities were limited to grade 1 or 2 treatment-related adverse events, with no dose-limiting toxicities reported. Peripheral CD4 T cell responses to 6MHP were found ex vivo in six (27%, 95% CI 11% to 50%), including four with the maximum CDX-1140 dose. One had a durable and persistent T cell response to week 25. T cell responses to mBRAF did not meet criteria for positivity ex vivo, but one participant had a durable response after in vitro stimulation, with expansion of multifunctional Th1-polarized CD4 T cells. Favorable immune-related changes were observed at the vaccine site, including CDX-1140-mediated increases in mature (DC-LAMP) DCs.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: The vaccine was safe, well-tolerated, and immunogenic. Optimization of vaccines that include agonistic CD40 antibody is needed to enhance immunogenicity. Induction of a multifunctional CD4 T cell response to mBRAF supports targeting shared mutated neoantigens with melanoma vaccines.
> 
> TRIAL REGISTRATION NUMBER: NCT04364230.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：对于对免疫检查点抑制剂无应答或不耐受的高危黑色素瘤患者，癌症疫苗可能提供获益且具有较好的安全性。在抗肿瘤反应中，CD4 T细胞为树突状细胞（DCs）提供必要的辅助以实现最佳的CD8 T细胞启动，诱导肿瘤特异性CD4 T细胞反应可能增强疫苗效力。我们报告了一种首次用于人体的方法，使用一种由六种非突变黑色素瘤特异性辅助肽（6MHP）和一种共享的突变BRAF-V600E新抗原辅助肽（mBRAF）组成的疫苗，局部联合TLR3激动剂（poly-ICLC）和激动型CD40抗体（CDX-1140）治疗高危黑色素瘤患者。
> 
> 方法：本研究是一项非随机I/II期试验（NCT04364230），旨在评估安全性和免疫原性。入组了经根治性治疗后达到临床无病状态、原发灶为皮肤、黏膜或眼部的成人高危黑色素瘤患者。受试者接受疫苗（6MHP+mBRAF+poly-ICLC）注射，其中CDX-1140以剂量递增方式（四个剂量水平之一：50、200、800、3000 μg）分配至疫苗混合物中。疫苗每3周给药一次，共四剂。主要终点是安全性和外周CD4 T细胞反应。进行了探索性分析以表征疫苗接种部位的微环境。
> 
> 结果：在22名符合条件的参与者中，11名（50%）患有眼部黑色素瘤。16名（73%）接受了最大剂量的CDX-1140。毒性仅限于1级或2级治疗相关不良事件，未报告剂量限制性毒性。在六名（27%，95% CI 11% 至 50%）参与者中离体检测到针对6MHP的外周CD4 T细胞反应，其中四名接受了最大剂量的CDX-1140。一名参与者对6MHP的T细胞反应持续至第25周。针对mBRAF的T细胞反应未达到离体阳性的标准，但一名参与者在体外刺激后产生了持久反应，表现为多功能Th1极化CD4 T细胞的扩增。在疫苗接种部位观察到有利的免疫相关变化，包括CDX-1140介导的成熟（DC-LAMP）DCs的增加。
> 
> 结论：该疫苗安全、耐受性良好且具有免疫原性。需要优化包含激动型CD40抗体的疫苗以增强免疫原性。诱导针对mBRAF的多功能CD4 T细胞反应支持了在黑色素瘤疫苗中靶向共享突变新抗原的策略。
> 
> 试验注册号：NCT04364230。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究是一项创新的I/II期临床试验，旨在探索一种联合新型佐剂（激动型CD40抗体和TLR3激动剂）的黑色素瘤多肽疫苗在高危患者中的安全性与免疫原性。其核心方法是将靶向共享非突变抗原与共享突变新抗原（BRAF-V600E）的辅助肽相结合，旨在通过激活CD4 T细胞来增强整体抗肿瘤免疫。研究发现该方案安全性良好，并成功诱导了针对非突变抗原的CD4 T细胞反应，且初步观察到针对共享突变新抗原的多功能Th1细胞反应，这为靶向常见驱动突变的疫苗策略提供了概念验证。然而，研究也提示免疫原性有待进一步提高，且样本量较小、非随机设计限制了其结论的普遍性，未来需在更大规模试验中优化方案并验证临床疗效。

---

## 31. 癌症免疫学与免疫治疗中的T细胞受体测序：是什么、何时、何地、为何以及如何应用。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775434)
**期刊：** Journal for immunotherapy of cancer
**PMID：** 41775434
**DOI：** 10.1136/jitc-2025-013499

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** TCR sequencing in cancer immunology and immunotherapy: what, when, where, why, and how.

> **英文摘要：**
> T-cell receptors (TCRs) are generated through somatic recombination of variable (V), diversity (D), and joining (J) gene segments, resulting in an extraordinarily diverse receptor repertoire that is essential for immune surveillance and host defense. TCR sequencing (TCR-seq) has emerged as a powerful tool for comprehensive characterization of the adaptive immune repertoire, offering deep insights into T-cell diversity, antigen specificity, and clonal dynamics.TCR-seq enables the tracking of T-cell clones across both temporal and spatial dimensions. From a longitudinal perspective, it allows for the monitoring of clonal dynamics before and after therapeutic interventions or over the course of disease progression. Temporal shifts in clonal composition can reveal the persistence, contraction, or expansion of specific T-cell populations, thereby providing valuable information on the durability of immune responses and the efficacy of treatments. From a spatial standpoint, TCR-seq facilitates comparative analyses of repertoires across distinct anatomical compartments, including tumors, blood, and lymph nodes. Such analyses yield insights into tissue-specific immune responses, T-cell trafficking, and infiltration patterns. Moreover, the ability to track antigen-specific T-cell clones enables the visualization and quantification of tumor-specific immune responses. Advances in spatial TCR-seq now integrate spatial context with clonal identity and repertoire diversity, further illuminating complex immune architecture within tissue microenvironments. Nonetheless, despite the development of various approaches for antigen specificity prediction, further advances are needed to improve their accuracy and generalizability.A wide range of TCR-seq platforms are currently available, including DNA-based and RNA-based protocols, short-read and long-read sequencing technologies, and bulk and single-cell approaches. Each method presents unique advantages in terms of resolution, throughput, cost, and biological relevance. For instance, DNA-based TCR-seq is well suited for longitudinal tracking of clonal populations, whereas RNA-based approaches are advantageous for detecting actively transcribed, antigen-responsive clones. Short-read sequencing offers high-throughput capabilities, while long-read and paired-chain sequencing provide comprehensive structural and functional information on TCRs. Additionally, computational methods, including machine learning algorithms and motif-based clustering, are increasingly employed to infer antigen specificity directly from TCR-seq data.In this review, we examine the current landscape of TCR-seq through the lenses of what, when, where, why, and how, highlighting recent technological developments and emerging applications that are shaping the field of immune repertoire analysis.

> **中文摘要：**
> T细胞受体（TCRs）通过可变区（V）、多样性区（D）和连接区（J）基因片段的体细胞重组产生，形成了极其多样化的受体库，这对免疫监视和宿主防御至关重要。TCR测序（TCR-seq）已成为全面表征适应性免疫库的强大工具，为深入理解T细胞多样性、抗原特异性和克隆动态提供了可能。TCR-seq能够在时间和空间两个维度上追踪T细胞克隆。从纵向角度看，它允许监测治疗干预前后或疾病进展过程中的克隆动态。克隆组成的时间变化可以揭示特定T细胞群体的持续存在、收缩或扩增，从而为免疫反应的持久性和治疗效果提供有价值的信息。从空间角度看，TCR-seq有助于对不同解剖部位（包括肿瘤、血液和淋巴结）的受体库进行比较分析。此类分析有助于理解组织特异性免疫反应、T细胞迁移和浸润模式。此外，追踪抗原特异性T细胞克隆的能力使得肿瘤特异性免疫反应的可视化和量化成为可能。空间TCR-seq的进展现在将空间背景与克隆身份和受体库多样性相结合，进一步阐明了组织微环境内复杂的免疫结构。然而，尽管已经开发了多种抗原特异性预测方法，但仍需进一步改进以提高其准确性和普适性。目前存在多种TCR-seq平台，包括基于DNA和基于RNA的方案、短读长和长读长测序技术、以及群体和单细胞方法。每种方法在分辨率、通量、成本和生物学相关性方面都具有独特的优势。例如，基于DNA的TCR-seq非常适合克隆群体的纵向追踪，而基于RNA的方法则有利于检测活跃转录、对抗原响应的克隆。短读长测序提供高通量能力，而长读长和配对链测序则提供关于TCR的全面结构和功能信息。此外，包括机器学习算法和基于基序的聚类在内的计算方法正越来越多地用于直接从TCR-seq数据推断抗原特异性。在这篇综述中，我们通过是什么、何时、何地、为何以及如何应用的视角审视了TCR-seq的当前格局，重点介绍了塑造免疫库分析领域的最新技术发展和新兴应用。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

这篇综述旨在系统阐述TCR测序（TCR-seq）在癌症免疫学和免疫治疗中的全方位应用框架。其核心目的是通过“是什么、何时、何地、为何、如何”的结构，全面解析TCR-seq作为解析适应性免疫库关键工具的技术原理、应用场景与价值。文章总结了TCR-seq在时空维度上追踪T细胞克隆动态、比较不同组织免疫库以及量化肿瘤特异性免疫反应的能力，并介绍了从DNA/RNA基础到单细胞、从短读到长读测序等多种技术平台及其计算分析方法。其创新性在于整合了空间TCR-seq等前沿技术，将克隆信息与组织微环境架构相结合。然而，文章也明确指出，尽管预测抗原特异性的方法有所发展，但其准确性和普适性仍有待提升，这是当前领域面临的主要局限性。

---

## 32. 局部免疫治疗研究与药物开发的优先事项。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775433)
**期刊：** Journal for immunotherapy of cancer
**PMID：** 41775433
**DOI：** 10.1136/jitc-2025-014222

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Priorities for local immunotherapy research and drug development.

> **英文摘要：**
> Local immunotherapy comprises broad classes of therapeutics that aim to trigger a robust "in situ" immune response that can ultimately generate systemic antitumor immunity. These agents are appealing as resistance to standard immune checkpoint inhibitors has been linked to a lack of baseline immune activity or immune suppressive elements in the tumor microenvironment. By administering agents directly to the tumor microenvironment, local immune therapies can both stimulate immune response and attempt to "reprogram" or subvert the effects of immune suppressive cell populations. Proof of concept for the benefit of local immune therapy has been demonstrated by several Food and Drug Administration-approved therapies.A "Summit on Intralesional Immunotherapy" was held in September 2024, which comprised lectures and discussion from an international panel of experts on local immune therapy. In this consensus paper, we will discuss unique considerations for local immunotherapy development across the continuum from pre-clinical and early-stage investigation through registration intent clinical trials.Early phase trials offer an opportunity to gain understanding of the biologic activity of candidate therapies and determine optimal dosing schedules. For local immunotherapies, it is most informative to measure the direct effect of the therapy in the tumor microenvironment at both injected and non-injected tumor sites. Carefully planned pharmacodynamic endpoints using on-treatment biopsies and novel imaging strategies to track immune cell activity will maximize the insights from early phase trials. For promising local therapies, selecting the proper patient population and treatment setting are critical. In order to intervene before the tumor microenvironment has reached a fixed immune suppressive state, local immunotherapies may best be suited as part of neoadjuvant or frontline metastatic therapy regimens. We also highlight several specific classes of local immunotherapy under investigation including oncolytic viruses, radiation, messenger RNA, Toll-like receptor agonists, stimulator of interferon gene agonists, CD40 agonists and cytokines.Novel local therapies currently being investigated are poised to expand the field and show promising activity in generating systemic antitumor immunity. Thoughtful trial design in both early stage as well as registration intent settings will accelerate the advancement of this field.

> **中文摘要：**
> 局部免疫治疗包含广泛的治疗类别，旨在触发强大的“原位”免疫反应，最终产生全身性抗肿瘤免疫。这些药物具有吸引力，因为对标准免疫检查点抑制剂的耐药性与肿瘤微环境中缺乏基线免疫活性或免疫抑制成分有关。通过将药物直接施用于肿瘤微环境，局部免疫疗法既可以刺激免疫反应，又可以尝试“重编程”或颠覆免疫抑制细胞群的作用。局部免疫疗法获益的概念验证已通过几种美国食品药品监督管理局批准的疗法得到证实。2024年9月召开了“病灶内免疫治疗峰会”，该峰会包括来自国际局部免疫治疗专家小组的讲座和讨论。在这篇共识文章中，我们将讨论局部免疫治疗从临床前和早期研究到注册意向临床试验的整个开发过程中独特的考量因素。早期试验为理解候选疗法的生物活性和确定最佳给药方案提供了机会。对于局部免疫疗法，测量疗法在注射部位和非注射部位肿瘤微环境中的直接效果最具信息价值。精心设计的药效学终点，如使用治疗中活检和追踪免疫细胞活性的新型成像策略，将最大化早期试验的洞察力。对于有前景的局部疗法，选择合适的患者人群和治疗环境至关重要。为了在肿瘤微环境达到固定的免疫抑制状态之前进行干预，局部免疫疗法可能最适合作为新辅助或一线转移治疗方案的一部分。我们还重点介绍了几类正在研究中的特定局部免疫疗法，包括溶瘤病毒、放射治疗、信使RNA、Toll样受体激动剂、干扰素基因刺激蛋白激动剂、CD40激动剂和细胞因子。目前正在研究的新型局部疗法有望拓展该领域，并在产生全身性抗肿瘤免疫方面显示出有前景的活性。在早期阶段以及注册意向试验中深思熟虑的试验设计将加速这一领域的进展。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文是一篇基于2024年病灶内免疫治疗峰会的共识性文章，核心目的是系统阐述局部免疫治疗从基础研究到临床开发全链条的优先事项与关键考量。文章方法上，不仅总结了局部免疫疗法的基本原理（如克服肿瘤微环境免疫抑制、诱导全身免疫），还具体提出了早期临床试验中评估生物活性的最佳策略（如多点活检、新型成像）以及患者选择和治疗时机（如新辅助/一线治疗）的建议。其创新性在于整合了多种新兴疗法（如mRNA、STING激动剂等）的开发经验，并强调了“局部给药、全身起效”的转化研究范式。局限性在于作为共识性前瞻文章，其提出的具体策略和优先事项尚需未来临床试验数据的进一步验证和支持。

---

## 33. 体成分对纳武利尤单抗联合伊匹木单抗治疗转移性透明细胞肾细胞癌疗效的影响。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775432)
**期刊：** Journal for immunotherapy of cancer
**PMID：** 41775432
**DOI：** 10.1136/jitc-2025-014363

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Influence of body composition on the efficacy of nivolumab plus ipilimumab for metastatic clear cell renal cell carcinoma.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Immune checkpoint inhibitor therapy (ICI) with nivolumab+ipilimumab is a first-line (1L) standard for metastatic clear cell renal cell carcinoma (ccRCC), yet outcomes remain heterogeneous. Increasing evidence suggests that host factors influence the tumor microenvironment and response to ICI. Although higher body mass index (BMI) has been associated with improved outcomes in several malignancies, BMI is an imprecise surrogate for underlying adipose and muscle compartments. We evaluated the association between body composition and outcomes with 1L nivolumab+ipilimumab in metastatic ccRCC.
> 
> METHODS: We retrospectively analyzed patients with mccRCC treated with 1L nivolumab+ipilimumab at MD Anderson Cancer Center between June 2015 and February 2024. Body composition was measured using an artificial intelligence segmentation tool at the L3 vertebra from pretreatment CT scans obtained within 45 days prior to starting therapy. Endpoints included real-world progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS). Multivariable Cox regression models, guided by directed acyclic graphs, evaluated associations between continuous body composition measures and outcomes, incorporating non-linear cubic splines. An exploratory analysis used single-cell RNA sequencing from 12 treatment-naïve patients with metastatic ccRCC, stratified by median Skeletal Muscle Mass Index (SMMi) and Subcutaneous Adipose Tissue Index (SATi) values.
> 
> RESULTS: Among 309 patients (80.3% male, median age 61.9 years; 61.8% intermediate-risk and 28.5% poor-risk), increasing SMMi and SATi were independently associated with shorter PFS (HR 1.50, 95% CI 1.05 to 2.15 per 3-unit increase; and HR 1.39, 95% CI 1.01 to 1.90 per 10-unit increase). The associations of BMI, visceral adiposity, and skeletal muscle density with PFS were inconclusive. OS associations for all body-composition measures were likewise indeterminate. In the single-cell cohort, low SMMi was associated with numerically higher T-cell fractions (p=0.064), fewer myeloid cell proportions (p=0.10), and higher IDO1 expression.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: Greater subcutaneous adiposity and skeletal muscle mass were associated with shorter PFS among patients with metastatic ccRCC treated with 1L nivolumab+ipilimumab. These findings support the concept that host body composition influences the heterogeneous clinical benefit observed with ICI in metastatic ccRCC.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：纳武利尤单抗联合伊匹木单抗的免疫检查点抑制剂疗法是转移性透明细胞肾细胞癌的一线标准治疗，但疗效仍存在异质性。越来越多的证据表明，宿主因素影响肿瘤微环境和对免疫检查点抑制剂的反应。尽管较高的身体质量指数与多种恶性肿瘤的较好预后相关，但BMI是潜在脂肪和肌肉成分的不精确替代指标。我们评估了转移性透明细胞肾细胞癌患者一线接受纳武利尤单抗联合伊匹木单抗治疗时，体成分与临床结局之间的关联。
> 
> 方法：我们回顾性分析了2015年6月至2024年2月期间在MD安德森癌症中心接受一线纳武利尤单抗联合伊匹木单抗治疗的转移性透明细胞肾细胞癌患者。体成分测量使用人工智能分割工具，基于治疗开始前45天内获得的CT扫描图像，在第三腰椎水平进行分析。研究终点包括真实世界无进展生存期和总生存期。在因果有向无环图的指导下，采用多变量Cox回归模型评估连续体成分指标与结局之间的关联，并纳入非线性三次样条函数。一项探索性分析使用了12例初治转移性透明细胞肾细胞癌患者的单细胞RNA测序数据，这些患者根据骨骼肌质量指数和皮下脂肪组织指数的中位值进行分层。
> 
> 结果：在309例患者中，骨骼肌质量指数和皮下脂肪组织指数的增加均独立地与较短的无进展生存期相关。BMI、内脏脂肪含量和骨骼肌密度与无进展生存期的关联均不明确。所有体成分指标与总生存期的关联同样不确定。在单细胞队列中，较低的骨骼肌质量指数在数值上与较高的T细胞比例、较低的髓系细胞比例以及较高的IDO1表达相关。
> 
> 结论：在接受一线纳武利尤单抗联合伊匹木单抗治疗的转移性透明细胞肾细胞癌患者中，较高的皮下脂肪含量和骨骼肌质量与较短的无进展生存期相关。这些发现支持了宿主体成分影响转移性透明细胞肾细胞癌患者接受免疫检查点抑制剂治疗所观察到的异质性临床获益这一概念。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在超越传统BMI，通过精准的CT影像组学测量体成分，探索其与转移性透明细胞肾细胞癌一线免疫联合治疗疗效的关联。研究创新性地结合了大规模临床队列的生存分析和基于单细胞RNA测序的探索性机制研究。核心发现是较高的皮下脂肪和骨骼肌质量与更差的无进展生存期相关，这挑战了传统“肥胖悖论”的简单认知，并提示特定脂肪/肌肉分布可能通过影响肿瘤免疫微环境（如T细胞、髓系细胞、IDO1）来调节疗效。局限性包括回顾性设计、总生存期关联不明确，以及单细胞队列样本量较小、结果多为数值趋势，需前瞻性验证。

---

## 34. 溶瘤免疫疗法RP1（vusolimogene oderparepvec）通过STING介导的干扰素信号通路影响免疫细胞，从而介导对抗PD-1疗法的反应性。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775431)
**期刊：** Journal for immunotherapy of cancer
**PMID：** 41775431
**DOI：** 10.1136/jitc-2025-013692

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Effects of oncolytic immunotherapy with RP1 (vusolimogene oderparepvec) on immune cells mediate responsiveness to anti-PD-1 via STING-mediated interferon signaling.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Antitumor immune responses induced by oncolytic immunotherapy (OI) are often followed by upregulation of programmed death-ligand 1 (PD-L1). As such, the combination of OI with blockade of the programmed cell death protein-1 (PD-1)/PD-L1 axis has demonstrated therapeutic activity in preclinical and clinical trials. The purpose of this study is to understand further the immune-mediated mechanism of interaction between oncolytic viruses and anti-PD-1 therapy.
> 
> METHODS: Tumor cells and immune cells (splenocytes) were cultured separately, or in co-culture with vusolimogene oderparepvec, an oncolytic herpes simplex virus expressing the fusogenic gibbon-ape leukemia virus-fusogenic membrane glycoprotein protein (GALV) and granulocyte-macrophage colony-stimulating factor (GM-CSF), also known as RP1. Viral replication, interferon (IFN) responses and PD-L1 expression were analyzed using wild-type, IFNAR1, TNFAR1 and STING knockout splenocytes. In vivo studies evaluated immune cell infiltrates into the tumor following RP1 administration with anti-PD-1 therapy.
> 
> RESULTS: RP1 replication was evident in tumor cells but not splenocytes. This was also accompanied by upregulated IFN expression in cultured splenocytes that was absent in cultured tumor cells. However, when these cell types were co-cultured, splenocytes mediated an interferon response to RP1 via STING that was transmitted to tumor cells in a non-touch-dependent manner. Tumor cells responded to these input signals via upregulation of cell surface major histocompatibility complex-I and PD-L1 through tumor intrinsic JAK-STAT signaling. In vivo, an IFN signature was observed following intratumoral injection of RP1, both in injected and non-injected tumors, which was further increased when combined with anti-PD-1 therapy. Marked upregulation of PD-L1 was observed in tumors injected with RP1 accompanied by the recruitment of CD11b+Ly6G+neutrophils into the tumor microenvironment, which stained positive for PD-L1.
> 
> CONCLUSION: Overall, the data demonstrate that RP1 remodels the tumor microenvironment through a combination of direct and indirect effects on both tumor and immune cells, resulting in an overall more inflamed phenotype.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：溶瘤免疫疗法（OI）诱导的抗肿瘤免疫反应常伴随程序性死亡配体1（PD-L1）的上调。因此，OI联合阻断程序性细胞死亡蛋白-1（PD-1）/PD-L1轴已在临床前和临床试验中显示出治疗活性。本研究旨在进一步理解溶瘤病毒与抗PD-1疗法之间相互作用的免疫介导机制。
> 
> 方法：将肿瘤细胞和免疫细胞（脾细胞）分别培养，或与vusolimogene oderparepvec（一种表达融合性长臂猿白血病病毒融合膜糖蛋白（GALV）和粒细胞-巨噬细胞集落刺激因子（GM-CSF）的溶瘤单纯疱疹病毒，也称为RP1）共培养。使用野生型、IFNAR1敲除、TNFAR1敲除和STING敲除的脾细胞分析病毒复制、干扰素（IFN）反应和PD-L1表达。体内研究评估了RP1联合抗PD-1疗法给药后免疫细胞向肿瘤的浸润情况。
> 
> 结果：RP1在肿瘤细胞中复制明显，但在脾细胞中不复制。同时，培养的脾细胞中IFN表达上调，而培养的肿瘤细胞中则无此现象。然而，当这两种细胞类型共培养时，脾细胞通过STING介导了对RP1的干扰素反应，并以非接触依赖的方式传递给肿瘤细胞。肿瘤细胞通过其内在的JAK-STAT信号通路上调细胞表面主要组织相容性复合物-I和PD-L1，从而对这些输入信号作出反应。在体内，瘤内注射RP1后，在注射和未注射的肿瘤中均观察到IFN特征信号，当与抗PD-1疗法联合时，该信号进一步增强。在注射RP1的肿瘤中观察到PD-L1显著上调，并伴有CD11b+Ly6G+中性粒细胞向肿瘤微环境的募集，这些中性粒细胞PD-L1染色呈阳性。
> 
> 结论：总体而言，数据显示RP1通过对肿瘤细胞和免疫细胞的直接和间接作用相结合，重塑了肿瘤微环境，导致整体上更具炎症性的表型。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在深入探究溶瘤病毒RP1与抗PD-1疗法协同作用的免疫机制。通过精巧的体外共培养与体内实验设计，结合基因敲除技术，研究揭示了RP1通过免疫细胞（脾细胞）的STING通路产生干扰素信号，并以非接触方式传递给肿瘤细胞，进而上调肿瘤细胞PD-L1表达的“远隔效应”机制。这一发现阐明了溶瘤病毒如何“预热”肿瘤微环境、增强免疫检查点抑制剂疗效的关键环节，为联合疗法的优化提供了重要的理论依据。然而，研究主要聚焦于机制探索，其临床转化潜力和在更广泛肿瘤类型中的普适性仍需后续验证。

---

## 35. 通过引入跨膜CD28结构域，增强学术型CAR-T ARI0002h对正常及低BCMA表达骨髓瘤细胞的抗肿瘤活性。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775430)
**期刊：** Journal for immunotherapy of cancer
**PMID：** 41775430
**DOI：** 10.1136/jitc-2025-011864

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Enhanced antitumoral activity of the academic CAR-T ARI0002h against normal and low BCMA-expressing myeloma cells after incorporating a transmembrane CD28 domain.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: B-cell maturation antigen (BCMA) is the main target for chimeric antigen receptor (CAR)-T cells in multiple myeloma (MM), demonstrating promising outcomes. However, unlike what happens with CART19 in lymphoblastic leukemia and non-Hodgkin's lymphoma, a high proportion of patients will relapse after CAR-T BCMA therapy due to insufficient antigen expression, low CAR-T cell persistence and/or T-cell exhaustion. In other B cell malignancies, second-generation anti-CD19 4-1BB CARs with CD28-transmembrane domain (TMD) have shown high efficacy and a favorable toxicity profile. We have developed a second-generation CD8α-TM BCMA-4-1BBζ CAR-T product, ARI0002h (Cesnicabtagene-autoleucel) for patients with relapsed/refractory MM. We hypothesized that replacing the TMD of ARI0002h with a CD28-TMD could increase efficacy and reduce tumor escape while maintaining a tolerable toxicity profile.
> 
> METHODS: We generated CAR-T cells using T-cells isolated from buffy coats and evaluated the efficacy and fitness of CAR-Ts at day 8-10 of expansion against several MM cell lines. In vitro analyses included cytotoxicity, proliferation, cytokine secretion, T-cell subset markers, activation and exhaustion profiling, metabolomic assays, and RNA-seq after multiple tumor challenges. In in vivo xenograft studies using NSG mice, with tumor cells expressing GFP-ffLuc, disease progression was monitored weekly via bioluminescence imaging.
> 
> RESULTS: Despite showing similar in vitro performance regarding cytotoxicity, proliferation and cytokine production, ARI2h-TM28 outperforms ARI0002h in a low BCMA expression setting and achieves superior in vivo tumor control and survival in relapse models with antigen downregulation. Furthermore, ARI2h-TM28 showed an optimized metabolic profile, more oxidative and energetic compared with ARI0002h, with downregulation of proinflammatory genes in CD8 T cells, contributing altogether both to reduced exhaustion and increased persistence of the CARs, improving their efficacy in preclinical models.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: Incorporating a CD28-TMD into the ARI0002h CAR enhances tumor control even in relapse models with downregulation of the target antigen, offering improved long-term disease management. This modification increases potency against MM tumor cell lines with both normal and reduced BCMA expression, demonstrating superior metabolic endurance and in vivo activity.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：B细胞成熟抗原（BCMA）是多发性骨髓瘤（MM）中嵌合抗原受体（CAR）-T细胞的主要靶点，已显示出良好的疗效。然而，与CART19在淋巴细胞白血病和非霍奇金淋巴瘤中的情况不同，很大一部分患者在CAR-T BCMA治疗后仍会复发，原因包括抗原表达不足、CAR-T细胞持久性低和/或T细胞耗竭。在其他B细胞恶性肿瘤中，带有CD28跨膜结构域（TMD）的第二代抗CD19 4-1BB CARs已显示出高效能和良好的毒性特征。我们为复发/难治性MM患者开发了第二代CD8α-TM BCMA-4-1BBζ CAR-T产品ARI0002h（Cesnicabtagene-autoleucel）。我们假设，将ARI0002h的TMD替换为CD28-TMD可以在保持可耐受毒性特征的同时提高疗效并减少肿瘤逃逸。
> 
> 方法：我们使用从血沉棕黄层中分离的T细胞生成CAR-T细胞，并在扩增第8-10天评估CAR-Ts针对多种MM细胞系的疗效和适应性。体外分析包括细胞毒性、增殖、细胞因子分泌、T细胞亚群标志物、活化和耗竭特征分析、代谢组学检测以及多次肿瘤攻击后的RNA-seq。在使用NSG小鼠的体内异种移植研究中，肿瘤细胞表达GFP-ffLuc，通过生物发光成像每周监测疾病进展。
> 
> 结果：尽管在细胞毒性、增殖和细胞因子产生方面表现出相似的体外性能，但在低BCMA表达环境下，ARI2h-TM28优于ARI0002h，并在抗原下调的复发模型中实现了更优的体内肿瘤控制和生存期。此外，与ARI0002h相比，ARI2h-TM28显示出优化的代谢特征，更具氧化性和能量性，同时CD8 T细胞中促炎基因下调，这些共同作用有助于减少CARs的耗竭并增加其持久性，从而在临床前模型中提高其疗效。
> 
> 结论：将CD28-TMD整合到ARI0002h CAR中，即使在靶抗原下调的复发模型中也能增强肿瘤控制，为改善长期疾病管理提供了可能。这种修饰增强了对具有正常和降低BCMA表达的MM肿瘤细胞系的效力，并显示出更优越的代谢耐受性和体内活性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过结构域工程改造，提升靶向BCMA的CAR-T疗法在抗原逃逸或低表达环境下的疗效。其核心方法是将学术型CAR-T产品ARI0002h的跨膜区由CD8α替换为CD28，并系统评估了改造后细胞（ARI2h-TM28）的体外功能、代谢特征及体内抗肿瘤活性。研究发现，跨膜区替换虽未显著改变体外杀伤等基础功能，但赋予了CAR-T细胞更优的代谢适应性和持久性，从而在低抗原或复发模型中实现了更强的肿瘤控制。其创新性在于通过跨膜区这一非信号传导结构域的改造，间接优化了CAR-T细胞的代谢状态和耗竭抵抗能力，为克服MM治疗中的抗原逃逸问题提供了新思路；局限性在于研究主要基于临床前模型，其安全性和临床转化效果仍需后续验证。

---

## 36. 数据何在？免疫检查点抑制剂停药后迟发性与慢性免疫相关不良事件的监测与管理：来自癌症免疫治疗学会关于生存照护及长期数据需求的专家见解。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775429)
**期刊：** Journal for immunotherapy of cancer
**PMID：** 41775429
**DOI：** 10.1136/jitc-2025-012823

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Where is the data? Delayed and chronic irAE surveillance and management after cessation of ICIs: expert insights from SITC on survivorship care and the need for long-term data.

> **英文摘要：**
> Immune checkpoint inhibitors (ICIs) have revolutionized cancer therapy, offering durable responses and prolonged survival. However, these therapies also present unique challenges, particularly with the onset of immune-related adverse events (irAEs), which can manifest during treatment either acutely and/or become chronic or emerge long after treatment cessation. Delayed, chronic, and re-emergent irAEs often require tailored survivorship care, including coordination across multiple disciplines focused on oncology, specialty care, and primary care. Despite the increased usage of ICIs, there is limited longitudinal data guiding the surveillance, diagnosis, attribution, and management of irAEs after ICI treatment. To address these gaps, the Society for Immunotherapy of Cancer convened an Expert Panel to deliberate best practices and identify research opportunities for improving post-treatment care. This paper outlines these expert insights into irAE surveillance, coordination and continuity across care transitions and settings, and clinical management strategies. The paper also underscores the importance of clinicians' understanding of irAE onset patterns, multidisciplinary coordination, and the urgent need in the field for the development of a comprehensive irAE registry. By addressing these critical gaps, the oncology community can better support the growing population of ICI-treated cancer survivors, ensuring improved quality of life and care outcomes.

> **中文摘要：**
> 免疫检查点抑制剂（ICIs）已经彻底改变了癌症治疗，提供了持久的应答和延长的生存期。然而，这些疗法也带来了独特的挑战，尤其是免疫相关不良事件（irAEs）的发生，这些事件可能在治疗期间急性发作和/或转为慢性，或在治疗停止后很久才出现。迟发性、慢性和再发性irAEs通常需要量身定制的生存照护，包括跨肿瘤学、专科医疗和初级保健等多学科的协调。尽管ICIs的使用日益增加，但指导ICI治疗后irAEs监测、诊断、归因和管理的纵向数据仍然有限。为了弥补这些不足，癌症免疫治疗学会召集了一个专家小组，以审议最佳实践并确定改善治疗后照护的研究机会。本文概述了这些专家关于irAE监测、跨照护过渡和不同场景的协调与连续性以及临床管理策略的见解。本文还强调了临床医生理解irAE发生模式、多学科协调的重要性，以及该领域迫切需要建立一个全面的irAE登记系统。通过解决这些关键差距，肿瘤学界可以更好地支持日益增长的接受ICI治疗的癌症幸存者群体，确保改善生活质量和照护结果。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文旨在解决ICI治疗后迟发性和慢性irAE监测与管理中存在的关键数据缺口。其核心方法是召集专家小组，通过共识形成关于监测、跨学科协调和临床管理的实践见解。主要发现是，现有纵向数据严重不足，并强调了建立综合性irAE登记系统的紧迫性。文章的创新性在于系统性地聚焦于治疗后的长期生存照护这一新兴领域，但其局限性在于提出的解决方案（如建立登记系统）尚属倡议阶段，缺乏具体的实施路径和初步数据支持。

---

## 37. 细胞生物学与疾病中的核磷酸肌醇信号传导。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41775263)
**期刊：** Developmental cell
**PMID：** 41775263
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.devcel.2026.02.004

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Nuclear phosphoinositide signaling in cell biology and disease.

> **英文摘要：**
> Phosphatidylinositol phosphates (PIPs), or phosphoinositides, are minor yet essential phospholipids that govern diverse cellular processes, from membrane trafficking to signal transduction. While traditionally studied within the cell membranes, emerging evidence reveals their dynamic metabolism and critical functions in the nucleus, particularly within the non-membrane nucleoplasm, continually reshaping our understanding of the nuclear PIP-lipidome and its therapeutic potential. However, an updated overview of the nuclear PIP landscape and its selective modulators remains lacking. This review addresses this gap by providing an integrated summary of nuclear PIP signaling components, encompassing their structures, species, distribution, transport, and metabolic regulation. A focus is placed on pharmacological modulation, including inhibitors and activators targeting nuclear phosphatidylinositol (PI/PtdIns) transfer proteins and PIP-metabolizing enzymes, with attention to structure-based inhibitor classes and representative clinical-stage compounds. We conclude by outlining therapeutic opportunities that arise from targeting the nuclear PIP pathway, particularly in the context of cancer, cardiovascular disease, and neurodegeneration.

> **中文摘要：**
> 磷脂酰肌醇磷酸（PIPs），或称磷酸肌醇，是含量虽少但至关重要的磷脂，调控着从膜运输到信号转导等多种细胞过程。虽然传统上主要在细胞膜内进行研究，但新出现的证据揭示了它们在细胞核内，特别是在非膜性的核质中，具有动态代谢和关键功能，不断重塑着我们对核PIP脂质组及其治疗潜力的理解。然而，目前仍缺乏对核PIP概况及其选择性调节剂的最新概述。本综述通过提供核PIP信号传导组分的整合性总结来填补这一空白，涵盖其结构、种类、分布、转运和代谢调控。重点聚焦于药理学调控，包括靶向核磷脂酰肌醇（PI/PtdIns）转运蛋白和PIP代谢酶的抑制剂和激活剂，并关注基于结构的抑制剂类别和具有代表性的临床阶段化合物。最后，我们概述了靶向核PIP通路所带来的治疗机遇，特别是在癌症、心血管疾病和神经退行性疾病的背景下。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本综述旨在系统梳理细胞核内磷酸肌醇信号传导的研究现状，填补该领域缺乏系统性总结的空白。其核心方法是对核PIP信号组分（结构、分布、代谢等）进行整合性总结，并重点评述靶向关键蛋白（如转运蛋白和代谢酶）的药理学调节剂。主要发现是，核内PIP具有动态代谢和重要功能，靶向其通路为癌症、心血管及神经退行性疾病提供了新的治疗机遇。其创新性在于将传统膜信号分子拓展至非膜性核环境，并聚焦于临床前/临床阶段的药理学工具，但作为综述，其结论主要基于现有证据整合，本身不产生新的实验数据。

---

## 38. 纳武利尤单抗±伊匹木单抗用于经治晚期神经内分泌癌患者：GCO-001 NIPINEC随机II期试验

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41774886)
**期刊：** Journal of clinical oncology : official journal of the American Society of Clinical Oncology
**PMID：** 41774886
**DOI：** 10.1200/JCO-25-01657

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Nivolumab ± Ipilimumab in Patients With Pretreated Advanced Neuroendocrine Carcinoma: The GCO-001 NIPINEC Randomized Phase II Trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: There is no standard second-line therapy for gastroenteropancreatic (GEP) and lung large-cell neuroendocrine carcinoma (NEC) after the failure of platinum-based chemotherapy. This study aimed to investigate the efficacy of nivolumab ± ipilimumab. METHODS: The GCO-001-NIPINEC (ClinicalTrials.gov identifier: NCT03591731) trial was a noncomparative, open-label, phase II trial. The main inclusion criteria were age ≥18 years, performance status (PS) ≤2, advanced large- and small-cell GEP-NEC and large-cell lung NEC, and second- or third-line treatment for NECs refractory to platinum-based chemotherapy. Patients were randomly assigned (1:1) and stratified by age and PS to receive nivolumab (3 mg/kg/once every 2 weeks) ± ipilimumab (1 mg/kg/once every 6 weeks) for 2 years or until progression or unacceptable toxicity. The primary end point was objective response rate (ORR) at 8 weeks, assessed by investigators. RESULTS: A total of 185 patients (91 in the nivolumab arm and 94 in the nivolumab-ipilimumab arm) were enrolled between December 2018 and March 2021; 169 were analyzed (median age of 64.5 years, 71% male, 91% PS 0-1). The main primary tumor locations were lungs (50%), colorectal (15%), gastroesophageal (14%), and pancreatic (13%) regions. The ORR at 8 weeks was 7.2% (95% CI, 2.7 to 15.1]) in the nivolumab arm and 14.0% (95% CI, 7.4 to 23.1) in the nivolumab-ipilimumab arm. The best ORR was 9.6% and 20.9%, respectively, whereas the median progression-free and overall survival were approximately 2 months and 6 months in both arms. One treatment-related death occurred, in the nivolumab arm. The grade 3-4 adverse events (≥5%) were asthenia (13%), gamma-glutamyl transferase increase (10%), alkaline phosphatase increase (9%), dyspnea (7%), and anemia (6%) in the nivolumab-ipilimumab arm. CONCLUSION: Nivolumab-ipilimumab could be a second-/third-line treatment option for patients with NECs. However, given the limited magnitude of benefit, studies are warranted to evaluate its use earlier and/or associated with chemotherapy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：对于胃肠胰（GEP）和肺大细胞神经内分泌癌（NEC）患者，在铂类化疗失败后尚无标准二线治疗方案。本研究旨在探讨纳武利尤单抗±伊匹木单抗的疗效。方法：GCO-001-NIPINEC试验（ClinicalTrials.gov标识符：NCT03591731）是一项非比较性、开放标签的II期试验。主要纳入标准为：年龄≥18岁，体能状态（PS）≤2，晚期大细胞和小细胞GEP-NEC以及大细胞肺NEC，且为对铂类化疗耐药的NEC的二线或三线治疗。患者按1:1随机分配，并按年龄和PS分层，接受纳武利尤单抗（3 mg/kg/每2周一次）±伊匹木单抗（1 mg/kg/每6周一次）治疗，持续2年或直至疾病进展或出现不可接受的毒性。主要终点是研究者评估的8周客观缓解率（ORR）。结果：2018年12月至2021年3月期间，共入组185例患者（纳武利尤单抗组91例，纳武利尤单抗-伊匹木单抗组94例）；其中169例纳入分析（中位年龄64.5岁，71%为男性，91% PS 0-1）。主要原发肿瘤部位为肺部（50%）、结直肠（15%）、胃食管（14%）和胰腺（13%）。8周ORR在纳武利尤单抗组为7.2%（95% CI，2.7至15.1），在纳武利尤单抗-伊匹木单抗组为14.0%（95% CI，7.4至23.1）。最佳ORR分别为9.6%和20.9%，而两组的中位无进展生存期和总生存期均约为2个月和6个月。纳武利尤单抗组发生1例治疗相关死亡。纳武利尤单抗-伊匹木单抗组发生率≥5%的3-4级不良事件为乏力（13%）、γ-谷氨酰转移酶升高（10%）、碱性磷酸酶升高（9%）、呼吸困难（7%）和贫血（6%）。结论：纳武利尤单抗-伊匹木单抗可作为NEC患者的二线/三线治疗选择。然而，鉴于获益程度有限，有必要进行研究以评估其在更早期使用和/或与化疗联合使用的效果。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索免疫检查点抑制剂（纳武利尤单抗±伊匹木单抗）在铂类化疗失败的晚期神经内分泌癌（NEC）患者中的疗效，填补了该领域二线治疗方案的空白。研究设计为非比较性随机II期试验，主要终点为8周客观缓解率（ORR）。结果显示，联合治疗组（纳武利尤单抗-伊匹木单抗）的ORR（14.0%）高于单药组（7.2%），但两组的中位生存期均较短（约6个月），提示疗效有限且生存获益不显著。其创新性在于首次在随机试验中评估了双免疫疗法在此类难治性肿瘤中的应用，但局限性在于疗效绝对值不高，且存在明确的毒性，未来需探索与化疗联合或更早期使用的策略。

## 39. 全国性乳腺X线摄影筛查在服务不足的庞大亚群体中的实施情况。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41774876)
**期刊：** Journal of clinical oncology : official journal of the American Society of Clinical Oncology
**PMID：** 41774876
**DOI：** 10.1200/JCO-25-01659

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Nationwide Mammographic Screening Among a Large Population of Underserved Subgroups.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: This national study was undertaken to determine screening mammography rates among transgender and gender diverse (TGD) individuals. METHODS: TGD individuals and cisgender women who qualified to receive screening mammography based on American College of Radiology guidelines were identified in the longitudinal OptumLabs Data Warehouse. The primary end point was the percentage of patients who had high rates of screening (>75% recommended screenings). Multivariable analyses were conducted in a matched population of transgender men to cisgender women to identify and adjust for factors associated with high adherence. Individuals were matched at a 1:4 ratio (transgender men: cisgender women) on age, race/ethnicity, year of enrollment in their health care plan, and duration of follow-up. RESULTS: This study focused on 10,478 TGD individuals (3,778 transgender men; 1,294 transgender women; 5,406 with gender dysphoria not meeting other TGD criteria, NMOT) and 6,218,369 cisgender women. For transgender men, transgender women, individuals with gender dysphoria NMOT, and cisgender women, high mammography rates were observed in 41.1% (95% CI, 39.5 to 42.6), 7.4% (95% CI, 6.0 to 8.8), 11.9% (95% CI, 11.0 to 12.7), and 38.3% (95% CI, 38.3 to 38.4), respectively ( < .0001). When transgender men were compared with 15,112 matched cisgender women, an age-based differential association was observed between sex and high mammography rates (interaction  = .0003); compared with cisgender women, transgender men appeared more likely to manifest high rates of screening at age 40-49 years (odds ratios [ORs], 1.38 [95% CI, 1.28 to 1.50];  < .0001) and 50-59 years (OR, 1.57 [95% CI, 1.35 to 1.81];  < .0001) but not in the older age groups. CONCLUSION: The relatively high rates of screening mammography in cisgender women and transgender men suggest clinicians are offering mammography to individuals who are at average or high breast cancer risk, as compared with cisgender women, and not to transgender women at low risk.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的： 这项全国性研究旨在确定跨性别及性别多元（TGD）个体的乳腺X线摄影筛查率。方法： 在纵向的OptumLabs数据仓库中，根据美国放射学会指南，识别出符合接受筛查性乳腺X线摄影条件的TGD个体和顺性别女性。主要终点是具有高筛查率（>75%推荐筛查）的患者百分比。在跨性别男性与顺性别女性的匹配人群中进行了多变量分析，以识别和调整与高依从性相关的因素。个体按1:4的比例（跨性别男性：顺性别女性）根据年龄、种族/民族、加入其医疗保健计划的年份以及随访持续时间进行匹配。结果： 本研究聚焦于10,478名TGD个体（3,778名跨性别男性；1,294名跨性别女性；5,406名不符合其他TGD标准的性别焦虑个体，NMOT）和6,218,369名顺性别女性。对于跨性别男性、跨性别女性、性别焦虑NMOT个体和顺性别女性，高乳腺X线摄影筛查率分别为41.1%（95% CI，39.5至42.6）、7.4%（95% CI，6.0至8.8）、11.9%（95% CI，11.0至12.7）和38.3%（95% CI，38.3至38.4）（P < .0001）。当将跨性别男性与15,112名匹配的顺性别女性进行比较时，观察到性别与高乳腺X线摄影筛查率之间存在基于年龄的差异关联（交互作用P = .0003）；与顺性别女性相比，跨性别男性在40-49岁（比值比[OR]，1.38 [95% CI，1.28至1.50]；P < .0001）和50-59岁（OR，1.57 [95% CI，1.35至1.81]；P < .0001）更可能表现出高筛查率，但在更年长的年龄组则不然。结论： 顺性别女性和跨性别男性中相对较高的筛查性乳腺X线摄影率表明，临床医生正在向具有平均或高乳腺癌风险的个体提供乳腺X线摄影，而不是向低风险的跨性别女性提供。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究利用大型纵向数据库，首次在全国层面系统评估了跨性别及性别多元（TGD）群体与顺性别女性在乳腺X线摄影筛查依从性上的差异。其核心发现揭示了显著的群体间差异：跨性别男性筛查率与顺性别女性相当甚至更高，而跨性别女性筛查率极低，这提示当前筛查实践可能主要基于乳腺癌风险感知而非性别认同本身。研究的创新性在于大规模量化了TGD亚群体的筛查现状，并识别出年龄与性别认同在筛查依从性上的交互作用。然而，研究依赖于管理数据，可能无法捕捉筛查决策背后的具体临床情境、患者意愿或社会障碍，且对“性别焦虑NMOT”群体的分类需谨慎解读其临床意义。

> **英文摘要：**

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探究SLAMF6分子在肿瘤免疫微环境中的作用。核心发现是SLAMF6作为一个负向调控因子，能够抑制T细胞功能，从而限制机体的抗肿瘤免疫反应。这一发现揭示了肿瘤免疫逃逸的一个潜在新机制，为开发靶向SLAMF6以增强T细胞功能的免疫治疗策略提供了理论依据。然而，研究的具体实验模型、调控通路细节及在人体中的验证情况尚不明确，是其主要的局限性。

## 41. 猫科动物癌症：突变全景图编录。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41774833)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41774833
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-NW2026-0022

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Feline Cancers: Cat-aloging the Mutational Landscape.

> **英文摘要：**
> Whole-genome sequencing of nearly 500 paired tumor-normal cat tissue samples, representing 13 cancers, has uncovered strong similarities with the human oncogenome, including recurrently mutated TP53 as a driver of multiple tumor types. This is the first time the domestic feline oncogenome has been comprehensively characterized, and the human parallels support utilizing cats more frequently in comparative oncology.

> **中文摘要：**
> 对近500份代表13种癌症的配对肿瘤-正常猫组织样本进行全基因组测序，揭示了其与人类肿瘤基因组的高度相似性，包括作为多种肿瘤类型驱动因素的TP53基因反复突变。这是首次对家猫肿瘤基因组进行全面表征，其与人类的相似性支持在比较肿瘤学中更频繁地利用猫作为模型。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过大规模全基因组测序，首次系统性描绘家猫肿瘤的突变全景图。核心发现是猫与人类肿瘤基因组存在高度相似性，特别是TP53作为跨癌种的共同驱动基因。这一成果的创新性在于填补了家猫肿瘤基因组学的空白，并有力论证了猫作为人类癌症比较研究模型的独特价值。局限性在于摘要未提及具体的突变谱差异或潜在的治疗转化路径，需阅读全文以获取更深入的机制与临床关联信息。
