## 42. Lisocabtagene maraleucel治疗复发或难治性大B细胞淋巴瘤患者的真实世界结局。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41774517)
**期刊：** Blood
**PMID：** 41774517
**DOI：** 10.1182/blood.2025031733

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Real-world outcomes for lisocabtagene maraleucel in patients with relapsed or refractory large B-cell lymphoma.

> **英文摘要：**
> This study assessed real-world effectiveness and safety of lisocabtagene maraleucel (liso-cel) in patients with relapsed/refractory (R/R) large B-cell lymphoma (LBCL), including those with high-risk disease, secondary central nervous system (sCNS) involvement, comorbidities, and poor fitness, using data in the Center for International Blood and Marrow Transplant Research Registry from 5 Feb 2021 to 4 Feb 2025. Eligible patients (N=1116) received liso-cel and had ≥1 effectiveness and safety assessment after infusion, including 195 in the second-line setting, 71 with sCNS, and 257 with transformed LBCL. Median age was 71.1 years (range, 21.5‒91.2), with 72.3% ≥65 years. Within the overall population, 6.6% had Eastern Cooperative Oncology Group performance status of ≥2, 53.4% had ≥1 comorbidity, and median number of prior lines of therapy was 3 (range, 1‒16). Median study follow-up was 12.6 months (95% confidence interval [CI], 12.5‒12.8). Among effectiveness-evaluable patients (n=1109), objective response rate was 81.2% and complete response rate was 71.3%. Duration of response, progression-free survival, and overall survival rates (95% CI) at 12 months were 60.2% (56.4‒63.9), 51.2% (48.0‒54.4), and 67.6% (64.5‒70.6), respectively. Cytokine release syndrome was reported in 51.0% of patients, with grade ≥3 events in 2.5%. Immune effector cell-associated neurotoxicity syndrome was reported in 26.6% of patients, with grade ≥3 events in 9.2%. The 12-month nonrelapse mortality rate was 6.1% (95% CI, 4.6‒7.8). These real-world data reinforce the effectiveness and safety of liso-cel in this broad population of patients with R/R LBCL, including younger patients and those with high-risk disease features.

> **中文摘要：**
> 本研究利用国际血液和骨髓移植研究中心登记处2021年2月5日至2025年2月4日的数据，评估了lisocabtagene maraleucel（liso-cel）在复发/难治性（R/R）大B细胞淋巴瘤（LBCL）患者中的真实世界有效性和安全性，这些患者包括高危疾病、继发性中枢神经系统（sCNS）受累、合并症和体能状态差的患者。符合条件的患者（N=1116）接受了liso-cel治疗，并在输注后进行了≥1次有效性和安全性评估，其中包括195例二线治疗患者、71例sCNS受累患者和257例转化型LBCL患者。中位年龄为71.1岁（范围：21.5‒91.2），其中72.3%的患者年龄≥65岁。在总体人群中，6.6%的患者美国东部肿瘤协作组体能状态评分≥2分，53.4%的患者有≥1种合并症，既往治疗线数的中位数为3（范围：1‒16）。中位研究随访时间为12.6个月（95%置信区间[CI]，12.5‒12.8）。在可评估有效性的患者（n=1109）中，客观缓解率为81.2%，完全缓解率为71.3%。12个月时的缓解持续时间、无进展生存率和总生存率（95% CI）分别为60.2%（56.4‒63.9）、51.2%（48.0‒54.4）和67.6%（64.5‒70.6）。51.0%的患者报告了细胞因子释放综合征，其中≥3级事件占2.5%。26.6%的患者报告了免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征，其中≥3级事件占9.2%。12个月非复发死亡率为6.1%（95% CI，4.6‒7.8）。这些真实世界数据进一步证实了liso-cel在这一广泛的R/R LBCL患者群体（包括年轻患者和具有高危疾病特征的患者）中的有效性和安全性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在利用真实世界登记数据，全面评估CAR-T疗法liso-cel在广泛、复杂的R/R LBCL患者群体（包括高龄、高危、sCNS受累等）中的表现。研究纳入了超过1100例患者，随访时间超过一年，提供了关于疗效（ORR 81.2%， CR 71.3%）和安全性（CRS和ICANS发生率及严重程度）的详实数据。其创新性在于填补了关键临床试验在特殊亚组人群和长期随访数据上的空白，证实了liso-cel在真实临床实践中的稳健疗效和可控毒性。局限性主要源于真实世界研究的固有属性，如非随机设计、潜在的混杂因素以及相对有限的随访时间，可能影响对长期结局的精确评估。

---

## 43. 抗CD7抗同源杀伤嵌合抗原受体T细胞治疗复发/难治性急性髓系白血病。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41774512)
**期刊：** Blood
**PMID：** 41774512
**DOI：** 10.1182/blood.2025032299

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Anti-CD7 fratricide-resistant chimeric antigen receptor T cells for relapsed/refractory acute myeloid leukemia.

> **英文摘要：**
> Autologous second-generation CD7-directed CAR T-cells, expressing an anti-CD7 protein expression blocker to prevent self-killing fratricide, were infused in three pediatric/young adult patients with relapsed/refractory CD7+ acute myeloid leukemia resulting in measurable residual disease negativity. The safety profile was favorable.

> **中文摘要：**
> 表达抗CD7蛋白表达阻断剂以防止自我杀伤性同源杀伤的自体第二代靶向CD7的CAR T细胞，被输注给三名患有复发/难治性CD7阳性急性髓系白血病的儿童/年轻成人患者，结果实现了可测量残留病灶阴性。安全性特征良好。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索抗同源杀伤的靶向CD7的CAR-T细胞疗法在复发/难治性CD7阳性急性髓系白血病中的初步应用。其核心方法创新在于通过表达抗CD7蛋白表达阻断剂，有效解决了CAR-T细胞因靶向自身CD7而发生的自相残杀问题。初步临床结果显示，三名患者均达到了可测量残留病灶阴性，且安全性良好，为这一难治性白血病亚型提供了新的治疗思路。然而，研究样本量极小，仅为初步探索，其长期疗效和安全性仍需更大规模研究验证。

---

## 44. 基于分子印迹合成受体的多参数生物可吸收传感器用于阿霉素检测

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41774065)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41774065
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202524369

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Multiparametric Bioresorbable Sensor for Doxorubicin Detection via Molecularly Imprinted Synthetic Receptors.

> **英文摘要：**
> Monitoring chemotherapeutic drug concentrations directly at the tumor site remains a critical unmet need in oncology, as conventional pharmacokinetic assessments based on systemic circulation fail to capture the spatial and temporal heterogeneity of drug distribution within solid tumors. Here, we report a bioresorbable, multiparametric optical sensor designed for the in situ detection of the chemotherapeutic agent doxorubicin. The sensor integrates a nanostructured porous silica scaffold with a molecularly imprinted polymer (MIP) synthetic receptor that provides shape- and chemistry-selective recognition of doxorubicin molecules. Molecular binding events are transduced through two orthogonal optical signals: i) shifts in effective optical thickness and ii) fluorescence intensity changes, enabling accurate and self-validating quantification across clinically relevant concentration ranges. The sensor operates reliably in serum with a limit of detection as low as 0.1 µg/mL, and exhibits reversible performance with minimal signal drift (<15.3%) over 12 weeks -consistent with standard chemotherapy regimens. In vivo implantation studies in mice confirm biodegradation and biocompatibility, with no evidence of local or systemic toxicity. This platform introduces a versatile strategy for multiparametric, bioresorbable chemical sensing using MIP synthetic receptors, establishing a foundation for future implantable diagnostics in precision chemotherapy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 直接在肿瘤部位监测化疗药物浓度仍然是肿瘤学中一个关键的未满足需求，因为基于全身循环的传统药代动力学评估无法捕捉药物在实体瘤内分布的时空异质性。在此，我们报道了一种生物可吸收的多参数光学传感器，专为化疗药物阿霉素的原位检测而设计。该传感器集成了纳米结构多孔二氧化硅支架与分子印迹聚合物合成受体，后者能提供对阿霉素分子的形状和化学选择性识别。分子结合事件通过两个正交的光学信号进行转导：i) 有效光学厚度的偏移，以及 ii) 荧光强度的变化，从而能够在临床相关浓度范围内实现准确且可自我验证的定量。该传感器在血清中可靠运行，检测限低至0.1 µg/mL，并在12周内表现出可逆性能，信号漂移极小（<15.3%），与标准化疗方案的时间一致。在小鼠体内植入研究证实了其生物降解性和生物相容性，无局部或全身毒性的证据。该平台引入了一种利用MIP合成受体进行多参数、生物可吸收化学传感的通用策略，为未来精准化疗中的可植入诊断奠定了基础。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决实体瘤内化疗药物分布异质性监测的临床难题，开发了一种创新的生物可吸收传感器。其核心方法是将分子印迹聚合物合成受体与多孔硅支架集成，并通过双光学信号（有效光学厚度偏移与荧光强度变化）实现阿霉素的高选择性、自验证检测。研究发现该传感器在血清中灵敏度高（检测限0.1 µg/mL）、长期稳定性好（12周内信号漂移<15.3%），且在小鼠模型中证实了其生物相容性与可降解性。其创新性在于首次将MIP受体与生物可吸收多参数光学传感平台结合，为开发用于精准化疗的长期植入式诊断设备奠定了基础；局限性在于目前研究尚处于概念验证和小鼠实验阶段，其人体内的长期性能、免疫反应及大规模制造工艺仍需进一步探索。

---

## 45. 北美经肛全直肠系膜切除术（taTME）治疗直肠癌多中心II期试验的长期结果

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41773887)
**期刊：** Annals of surgery
**PMID：** 41773887
**DOI：** 10.1097/SLA.0000000000007044

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Long-Term Results of the North American Phase II taTME Multicenter Trial for Rectal Cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> OBJECTIVE/SUMMARY BACKGROUND DATA: Transanal TME (taTME) facilitates sphincter preservation in low rectal cancer. Preliminary results and functional outcomes from the North American multicenter phase II taTME trial (NCT03144765) have been published. Three-year outcomes are reported.
> 
> METHODS: Patients with stage I-III rectal adenocarcinoma were enrolled across 11 centers (2017-2022). Endpoints included TME grade, 3-year overall survival (OS), disease-free survival (DFS), cancer-specific survival (CCS), recurrence, late (beyond 90 d) complications, and stoma-free survival. Surveillance followed NCCN guidelines, with pelvic MRI at 3 years to assess for pelvic sidewall recurrence when possible. Kaplan-Meier analysis assessed oncologic outcomes.
> 
> RESULTS: One hundred patients underwent taTME for tumors at a median of 5.8 cm from the anal verge, with intersphincteric resection in 36% and handsewn anastomosis in 54%. Median follow-up was 50.9 months. Late complications occurred in 32 patients, including 21 severe (CD≥3). Late anastomotic complications occurred in 5 patients; one required surgical revision. Estimated 3-year OS, CSS, and DFS were 93.7%, 96.6%, and 84.6%, respectively. Distant复发 occurred in 15 patients (median 17.6 mo), most commonly in the lung and liver. Locoregional复发 occurred in two patients. Preoperative N stage, lymph node yield, tumor deposits, and perineural invasion were associated with recurrence. Among 100 patients diverted at taTME, 97% were stoma-free at three years; four patients later underwent secondary diversion.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: Three-year outcomes of this multicenter trial support the safety and efficacy of taTME in resectable mid and low rectal tumors, with outcomes comparable to contemporary studies. Longer term oncologic and functional outcomes are needed.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的/背景资料摘要：经肛全直肠系膜切除术（taTME）有助于低位直肠癌的保肛。北美多中心II期taTME试验（NCT03144765）的初步结果和功能结局已发表。本文报告其三年结局。
> 
> 方法：在11个中心（2017-2022年）入组了I-III期直肠腺癌患者。终点包括TME质量分级、3年总生存期（OS）、无病生存期（DFS）、癌症特异性生存期（CSS）、复发、晚期（超过90天）并发症以及无造口生存期。随访遵循NCCN指南，在可能的情况下于3年时进行盆腔MRI以评估盆腔侧壁复发。采用Kaplan-Meier法分析肿瘤学结局。
> 
> 结果：100例患者接受了taTME，肿瘤距肛缘中位距离为5.8厘米，其中36%进行了括约肌间切除术，54%进行了手工吻合。中位随访时间为50.9个月。32例患者发生晚期并发症，其中21例为严重并发症（Clavien-Dindo分级≥3级）。5例患者发生晚期吻合口并发症；其中1例需要手术修复。估计的3年OS、CSS和DFS分别为93.7%、96.6%和84.6%。15例患者发生远处复发（中位时间17.6个月），最常见于肺和肝。2例患者发生局部区域复发。术前N分期、淋巴结检出数、肿瘤沉积和神经侵犯与复发相关。在taTME时行转流性造口的100例患者中，97%在三年时无造口；4例患者后续接受了二次转流。
> 
> 结论：本多中心试验的三年结局支持taTME在可切除的中低位直肠肿瘤中的安全性和有效性，其结果与当代研究相当。需要更长期的肿瘤学和功能结局数据。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在报告北美多中心II期taTME试验的三年长期结局，核心目的是评估该技术在可切除中低位直肠癌中的安全性与有效性。研究采用前瞻性多中心设计，纳入了100例患者，系统评估了肿瘤学结局、晚期并发症及功能保留（如无造口生存）。主要发现显示taTME能实现较高的3年生存率（OS 93.7%， DFS 84.6%）和出色的保肛率（97%无造口），其肿瘤学结果与现有研究相当，验证了该技术的近期疗效。其创新性在于提供了来自北美人群的、随访时间较长的多中心数据，但局限性在于仍需更长期的肿瘤学和功能结局数据来全面评估其远期影响，且样本量相对有限。

## 46. 靶向AML的金属-多酚纳米平台通过诱导铁死亡-ICD级联反应增强抗肿瘤免疫。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41773746)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41773746
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202520544

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** AML-Targeted Metal-Polyphenol Nanoplatform Induces Ferroptosis-ICD Cascade for Antitumor Immunity Boosting.

> **英文摘要：**
> Acute myeloid leukemia (AML) remains a therapeutic challenge due to its low immunogenicity and immunosuppressive tumor microenvironment (iTME). We developed a ferritin-based nanoplatform (Fe-SH@Fn) co-delivering shikonin (SH) and Fe to synergistically induce ferroptosis and activate immunogenic cell death (ICD). Ferritin, a ligand for CD71, which is overexpressed on AML cells, enables tumor targeting and encapsulates Fe-SH formed by coordination between SH and Fe. In AML cells, high intracellular glutathione triggers Fe-SH@Fn disassembly: Fe reduces to Fe to drive Fenton reaction-mediated ferroptosis, while SH induces ICD. This dual effect boosts the release of damage-associated molecular patterns, remodeling the microenvironment by promoting dendritic cell maturation, enhancing CD8 T cell infiltration, and reducing regulatory T cells. In vivo, Fe-SH@Fn achieved 81.25% tumor growth inhibition in subcutaneous AML model and extended median survival by 2.8-fold in orthotopic AML model without systemic toxicity. This work presents a translatable strategy that overcomes AML immunosuppression through targeted drug delivery and synergistic ferroptosis-ICD activation.

> **中文摘要：**
> 急性髓系白血病（AML）因其低免疫原性和免疫抑制性肿瘤微环境（iTME）而仍是治疗难题。我们开发了一种基于铁蛋白的纳米平台（Fe-SH@Fn），其共递送紫草素（SH）和铁（Fe），以协同诱导铁死亡并激活免疫原性细胞死亡（ICD）。铁蛋白是CD71的配体，而CD71在AML细胞上过表达，这赋予了纳米平台肿瘤靶向能力，并能封装由SH和Fe通过配位作用形成的Fe-SH。在AML细胞内，高浓度的细胞内谷胱甘肽触发Fe-SH@Fn解组装：Fe被还原为Fe，驱动芬顿反应介导的铁死亡，而SH则诱导ICD。这种双重效应促进了损伤相关分子模式的释放，通过促进树突状细胞成熟、增强CD8 T细胞浸润以及减少调节性T细胞来重塑肿瘤微环境。在体内，Fe-SH@Fn在皮下AML模型中实现了81.25%的肿瘤生长抑制，在原位AML模型中使中位生存期延长了2.8倍，且无全身毒性。这项工作提出了一种可转化的策略，通过靶向药物递送和协同的铁死亡-ICD激活来克服AML的免疫抑制。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在克服AML低免疫原性与免疫抑制微环境的治疗挑战。其核心策略是构建一种基于铁蛋白的靶向纳米平台，通过共递送紫草素与铁离子，在AML细胞内协同触发铁死亡与免疫原性细胞死亡级联反应。研究发现，该平台能有效重塑肿瘤免疫微环境，并在体内模型中显著抑制肿瘤生长、延长生存期且无系统毒性。创新性在于巧妙利用CD71靶向和谷胱甘肽响应性释放，实现了铁死亡与ICD的时空协同，为AML免疫治疗提供了新思路；局限性在于摘要未提及对复发或耐药模型的效果，且临床转化潜力尚待进一步验证。

---

## 47. 一种基于人工抗体的工具箱加速了对“暗基因组”编码的隐藏微蛋白的验证。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41773075)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41773075
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202515707

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** An Artificial Antibody-Based Toolbox Accelerates Validation of Hidden Microproteins Encoded by the Dark Genome.

> **英文摘要：**
> Microproteins encoded by small open reading frames are a pivotal blind spot redefining the conventional protein-coding assumptions. However, the annotation of the "dark proteome" remains time- and labor-consuming due to the limited efficiency, sensitivity, and comprehensiveness of existing validation methods. To address these issues, we developed a comprehensive toolbox called CLAIMID to achieve accelerated and ultrasensitive validation at multiple biological scales. As the core of CLAIMID, molecularly imprinted polymers (MIPs), which are synthesized artificial antibodies toward putative microproteins, provide ultrasensitive and precise annotation in combination with surface-enhanced Raman scattering (SERS) detection. The excellent specificity, comparable to antibodies, of MIPs enables high anti-interference against biological matrix. The adaptability of MIPs engineering confers the rigorous validations by CLAIMID at multiple scales (single living cells, cell populations, and tissues) and diverse detection formats (SERS-based immunoassay and imaging, and mass spectrometric identification). Through CLAIMID, we rapidly confirmed the protein-level translation of four predicted microproteins-previously supported only by computational or ribosome profiling data-across various cell lines, and further identified three as potential tumor biomarkers, thereby demonstrating its university to putative microproteins. Together, we present an annotation toolbox with unparalleled efficiency, sensitivity, and scalability, moving forward for the advent of intriguing microprotein biology era.

> **中文摘要：**
> 由小开放阅读框编码的微蛋白是重新定义传统蛋白质编码假设的关键盲点。然而，由于现有验证方法的效率、灵敏度和全面性有限，“暗蛋白质组”的注释仍然耗时耗力。为了解决这些问题，我们开发了一个名为CLAIMID的综合工具箱，旨在多个生物学尺度上实现加速且超灵敏的验证。作为CLAIMID的核心，分子印迹聚合物（MIPs）是针对假定微蛋白合成的人工抗体，结合表面增强拉曼散射（SERS）检测，提供了超灵敏且精确的注释。MIPs具有与抗体相当的优异特异性，使其对生物基质具有高抗干扰能力。MIPs工程的可适应性使得CLAIMID能够在多个尺度（单个活细胞、细胞群体和组织）和多种检测形式（基于SERS的免疫分析和成像，以及质谱鉴定）上进行严格验证。通过CLAIMID，我们快速确认了四种预测微蛋白（先前仅得到计算或核糖体分析数据支持）在多种细胞系中的蛋白质水平翻译，并进一步鉴定出其中三种为潜在的肿瘤生物标志物，从而证明了其对假定微蛋白的普适性。总之，我们提出了一种具有无与伦比的效率、灵敏度和可扩展性的注释工具箱，推动着引人入胜的微蛋白生物学时代的到来。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决“暗蛋白质组”中微蛋白验证的技术瓶颈，开发了名为CLAIMID的综合工具箱。其核心创新在于利用分子印迹聚合物（MIPs）作为人工抗体，结合SERS检测，实现了对微蛋白的超灵敏、高特异性验证，并具备从单细胞到组织层面的多尺度、多模式检测能力。研究成功验证了四个预测微蛋白的翻译，并发现其中三个是潜在的肿瘤标志物，展示了该工具在微蛋白功能注释和生物标志物发现中的强大潜力。然而，摘要未提及该方法的潜在局限性，例如MIPs针对不同微蛋白的合成效率、大规模应用的标准化流程，以及其在复杂临床样本中的验证深度，这些可能是未来需要探索的方向。

---

## 48. GNL3调控雄激素受体转录程序以驱动去势抵抗性前列腺癌及免疫逃逸。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41772945)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41772945
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202516411

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** GNL3 Orchestrates AR Transcriptional Programs to Drive Castration-Resistant Prostate Cancer and Immune Evasion.

> **英文摘要：**
> Androgen receptor (AR) signaling is a primary oncogenic driver of castration-resistant prostate cancer (CRPC), yet the mechanism remains incompletely understood. Through proteomic profiling of CRPC and primary PCa cells, we identify G Protein Nucleolar 3 (GNL3) as a novel AR coregulator. GNL3 physically interacts with AR, enhances its chromatin occupancy, and directly coactivates transcriptional programs that promote cell proliferation, including NEK2 and CDC20. Concurrently, GNL3 functions as a corepressor of immune-responsive genes such as CXCL10 and TAP1 via class I histone deacetylases (HDACs), thereby facilitating CD8+ T cell elimination and establishing an immunosuppressive tumor microenvironment. GNL3 expression and AR-GNL3 complex formation progressively increase from normal prostate to CRPC and correlate with poor clinical outcomes. Functionally, GNL3 knockdown sensitizes CRPC cells to AR antagonists and impairs tumor growth and metastasis. Furthermore, we demonstrate that combinatorial inhibition of NEK2, class I HDACs, and AR signaling can be a potential therapeutic strategy for CRPC. Overall, these findings establish GNL3 as a dual-function AR coregulator and therapeutic target, providing mechanistic insights into transcriptional regulation and immune evasion in advanced PCa.

> **中文摘要：**
> 雄激素受体（AR）信号通路是去势抵抗性前列腺癌（CRPC）的主要致癌驱动因素，但其机制尚未完全阐明。通过对CRPC和原发性前列腺癌细胞的蛋白质组学分析，我们鉴定出G蛋白核仁蛋白3（GNL3）是一种新型的AR共调节因子。GNL3与AR发生物理相互作用，增强其在染色质上的占据，并直接共激活促进细胞增殖的转录程序，包括NEK2和CDC20。同时，GNL3通过I类组蛋白去乙酰化酶（HDACs）发挥免疫应答基因（如CXCL10和TAP1）的共阻遏物功能，从而促进CD8+ T细胞的清除并建立免疫抑制性肿瘤微环境。GNL3的表达及AR-GNL3复合物的形成从正常前列腺到CRPC呈进行性增加，并与不良临床结局相关。在功能上，敲低GNL3可使CRPC细胞对AR拮抗剂敏感，并损害肿瘤生长和转移。此外，我们证明联合抑制NEK2、I类HDACs和AR信号通路可能是一种潜在的CRPC治疗策略。总之，这些发现确立了GNL3作为一种双功能AR共调节因子和治疗靶点，为晚期前列腺癌的转录调控和免疫逃逸机制提供了新的见解。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明CRPC中AR信号通路调控的新机制。通过蛋白质组学分析，作者发现GNL3是一个关键的AR共调节因子，其创新性地揭示了GNL3的双重功能：一方面作为共激活因子促进促增殖基因表达，另一方面通过HDACs抑制免疫基因，驱动免疫逃逸。研究将分子机制与临床预后、潜在联合治疗策略（NEK2/HDAC/AR抑制）紧密联系，为CRPC治疗提供了新靶点。然而，摘要未提及GNL3调控AR信号的具体上游机制，且联合疗法的体内有效性与安全性仍需后续实验验证。

---

## 49. 甲基斑蝥酰亚胺通过抑制细胞周期蛋白依赖性激酶1（CDK1）并诱导氧化凋亡抑制肝癌。

> **英文摘要：**

> **中文摘要：**

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探讨甲基斑蝥酰亚胺（Methyl-cantharidimide）在肝癌治疗中的作用机制。研究聚焦于该化合物通过抑制细胞周期关键激酶CDK1，并诱导一种新型细胞死亡方式——氧化凋亡（oxeiptosis），从而发挥抗肿瘤效应。其创新性在于揭示了该化合物独特的双重作用机制，特别是诱导氧化凋亡这一非经典死亡途径，为肝癌治疗提供了新的潜在靶点。然而，由于摘要缺失，其具体实验模型、体内外验证数据以及潜在的局限性尚不明确。

## 50. 人工智能模型：变革胃肠道癌症的早期诊断与精准治疗

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41772662)
**期刊：** Molecular cancer
**PMID：** 41772662
**DOI：** 10.1186/s12943-026-02589-7

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Artificial intelligence models: transforming early diagnosis and precise treatment of gastrointestinal cancers.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无摘要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

## 53. 多功能RNA解旋酶DDX39A通过调控WISP1可变剪接诱导免疫抑制性巨噬细胞极化，从而驱动胶质母细胞瘤进展。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41772197)
**期刊：** Oncogene
**PMID：** 41772197
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41388-026-03715-x

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** The multifunctional RNA helicase DDX39A drives glioblastoma progression by modulating WISP1 alternative splicing that induces an immunosuppressive macrophage polarization.

> **英文摘要：**
> Glioblastoma (GB) is a highly complex ecosystem characterized by numerous interactions between tumor cells and the surrounding tumor microenvironment (TME). Splicing factors play a pivotal role in processing nascent pre-mRNA and are important in the progression of cancer, making them promising molecular targets. In this study, we demonstrate that the DEAD-box helicase 39 A (DDX39A), a RNA helicase with several important roles in RNA metabolism and cellular processes, is significantly upregulated in GB and is primarily expressed in tumor cells, leading to an immunosuppressive macrophage polarization. Through in vitro and in vivo studies, we demonstrate that reducing DDX39A expression in GB results in reduced tumor growth and invasion. Mechanistically, through RNA-seq and RIP-seq, we identified WISP1 as a critical downstream effector of DDX39A. DDX39A stabilizes WISP1 pre-mRNA through alternative splicing regulation, thereby activating the AKT signaling pathway. We further demonstrate that WISP1, when secreted by tumor cells, functions as a paracrine signaling molecule that promotes the development of immunosuppressive tumor-associated macrophages (TAMs). Additionally, we demonstrate that Fluphenazine hydrochloride binds to and inhibits DDX39A, thereby suppressing GB growth, invasion, and the immunosuppressive function of macrophages. DDX39A thus represents a potential candidate for glioma-targeted therapy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 胶质母细胞瘤（GB）是一个高度复杂的生态系统，其特征是肿瘤细胞与周围肿瘤微环境（TME）之间存在大量相互作用。剪接因子在处理新生前体mRNA中起着关键作用，并且在癌症进展中至关重要，这使其成为有前景的分子靶点。在本研究中，我们证明DEAD-box解旋酶39 A（DDX39A）——一种在RNA代谢和细胞过程中具有多种重要作用的RNA解旋酶——在GB中显著上调，并且主要在肿瘤细胞中表达，导致免疫抑制性巨噬细胞极化。通过体外和体内研究，我们证明降低GB中DDX39A的表达可减少肿瘤生长和侵袭。从机制上讲，通过RNA-seq和RIP-seq，我们确定WISP1是DDX39A的关键下游效应因子。DDX39A通过可变剪接调控稳定WISP1前体mRNA，从而激活AKT信号通路。我们进一步证明，WISP1由肿瘤细胞分泌时，可作为旁分泌信号分子，促进免疫抑制性肿瘤相关巨噬细胞（TAMs）的发育。此外，我们证明盐酸氟奋乃静可结合并抑制DDX39A，从而抑制GB的生长、侵袭以及巨噬细胞的免疫抑制功能。因此，DDX39A代表了胶质瘤靶向治疗的潜在候选靶点。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明RNA解旋酶DDX39A在胶质母细胞瘤（GB）进展中的功能和机制。研究者综合运用体内外模型、RNA-seq和RIP-seq等技术，发现DDX39A通过调控WISP1的可变剪接，激活AKT通路，并诱导免疫抑制性肿瘤相关巨噬细胞（TAMs）极化，从而促进GB进展。其创新性在于将RNA代谢调控、肿瘤细胞内在信号通路与肿瘤微环境免疫重塑联系起来，并鉴定出盐酸氟奋乃静作为潜在的DDX39A抑制剂。局限性在于，研究主要聚焦于DDX39A-WISP1轴，对于DDX39A是否通过其他底物或通路影响GB进展，以及盐酸氟奋乃静在临床前模型中的具体药效和毒性仍需进一步探索。

---

## 56. BCDX2-CX3与DX2-CX3复合物组装并稳定RAD51丝状体。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41772053)
**期刊：** Nature
**PMID：** 41772053
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41586-026-10314-z

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** BCDX2-CX3 and DX2-CX3 complexes assemble and stabilize RAD51 filaments.

> **英文摘要：**
> The repair of DNA double-strand breaks by homologous recombination (HR) is essential for genomic integrity, and its dysregulation is a hallmark of cancer. Central to HR is the RAD51 recombinase, whose assembly into a nucleoprotein filament is governed by five RAD51 paralogs (RAD51B, RAD51C, RAD51D, XRCC2, XRCC3). Mutations in any of these proteins predispose individuals to multiple cancers or genetic disorders. These paralogs are thought to form two functionally separate complexes, BCDX2 (RAD51B-C-D-XRCC2) and CX3 (RAD51C-XRCC3), that act independently at different stages of HR. Here, we demonstrate that all five paralogs can assemble into a single, ATP-dependent BCDX2-CX3-RAD51 supercomplex. The architecture of this assembly bound to single-stranded DNA (ssDNA) reveals a contiguous filament where the CX3 module stacks atop BCDX2, creating a protofilament template for RAD51 filament formation. We further identify a novel, RAD51B-independent DX2-CX3 complex (RAD51D-XRCC2-RAD51C-XRCC3) functioning as a stable RAD51 anchor on ssDNA, and we capture it in multiple states, including capping RAD51 filament segment. These distinct assemblies are differentially regulated by ATPase activity, defining a dynamic BCDX2-CX3 "loader" and a stable DX2-CX3 "anchor" that provide functional modularity to the HR machinery. This work provides a unifying mechanism for human RAD51 paralog function and delivers an atomic blueprint for interpreting disease-causing mutations.

> **中文摘要：**
> 通过同源重组（HR）修复DNA双链断裂对于基因组完整性至关重要，其失调是癌症的一个标志。HR的核心是RAD51重组酶，其组装成核蛋白丝状体由五个RAD51旁系同源物（RAD51B、RAD51C、RAD51D、XRCC2、XRCC3）调控。这些蛋白中任何一种发生突变都会使个体易患多种癌症或遗传性疾病。这些旁系同源物被认为形成两个功能上独立的复合物：BCDX2（RAD51B-C-D-XRCC2）和CX3（RAD51C-XRCC3），它们在HR的不同阶段独立发挥作用。在此，我们证明所有五个旁系同源物可以组装成一个单一的、ATP依赖的BCDX2-CX3-RAD51超复合物。该组装体与单链DNA（ssDNA）结合的结构揭示了一个连续的丝状体，其中CX3模块堆叠在BCDX2之上，为RAD51丝状体的形成创建了一个原丝模板。我们进一步鉴定了一个新的、不依赖RAD51B的DX2-CX3复合物（RAD51D-XRCC2-RAD51C-XRCC3），它在ssDNA上充当稳定的RAD51锚定点，并且我们捕获了它的多种状态，包括封盖RAD51丝状体片段。这些不同的组装体受ATP酶活性差异调节，定义了一个动态的BCDX2-CX3“加载器”和一个稳定的DX2-CX3“锚定点”，为HR机制提供了功能模块性。这项工作为人类RAD51旁系同源物的功能提供了一个统一的机制，并为解释致病突变提供了原子水平的蓝图。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明RAD51旁系同源物在HR中的精确作用机制。通过结构生物学方法，作者揭示了所有五个旁系同源物可形成ATP依赖的超复合物，并首次鉴定出独立的DX2-CX3复合物。其核心创新在于提出了一个统一的功能模型，将先前认为独立的复合物整合为动态的“加载器”与稳定的“锚定点”，为理解HR的精细调控提供了全新框架。然而，研究主要基于体外结构分析，这些复合物在活细胞内的动态组装与调控及其在特定癌症背景下的功能验证，是未来需要探索的方向。

---

## 57. 弱势女性宫颈癌及高级别病变风险：一项系统综述与荟萃分析

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771925)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41771925
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70050-w

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Risk of cervical cancer and high-grade lesions in vulnerable women a systematic review and meta-analysis.

> **英文摘要：**
> Cervical cancer is largely preventable, yet causes around 300,000 deaths annually, disproportionately affecting vulnerable women. In here, we aim to estimate the risk of high-grade cervical lesions and cervical cancer among vulnerable populations in high- and upper-middle-income countries. We conduct a systematic review and meta-analysis of studies published up to February 2024 (from 2004 for HIV) across four databases. Risk of bias is assessed using the Newcastle-Ottawa Scale. We include women with low socioeconomic status, migrants, prisoners, sex workers, women with substance use disorders, mental illness, and living with HIV. The primary outcome is the pooled risk of cervical cancer and high-grade lesions; the secondary outcome is subgroup-specific risk. The analysis focuses on biologically defined females, with sex determined by author reporting. In this work, based on 127 studies, we show that vulnerable women face higher risks of cervical cancer (RR2.78; 95%CI 2.32-3.32) and high-grade lesions (RR 2.5; 95%CI 2.05-3.04), with high heterogeneity supporting equity-focused prevention strategies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 宫颈癌在很大程度上是可预防的，但每年仍导致约30万人死亡，且对弱势女性的影响尤为严重。本研究旨在评估高收入和中高收入国家弱势人群中高级别宫颈病变及宫颈癌的风险。我们对截至2024年2月（HIV相关研究自2004年起）发表在四个数据库中的研究进行了系统综述和荟萃分析。使用纽卡斯尔-渥太华量表评估偏倚风险。纳入的女性包括社会经济地位低下者、移民、囚犯、性工作者、物质使用障碍女性、精神疾病患者以及HIV感染者。主要结局是宫颈癌和高级别病变的汇总风险；次要结局是各亚组的特异性风险。分析聚焦于生物学定义的女性，其性别由作者报告确定。本研究基于127项研究，结果表明，弱势女性面临更高的宫颈癌风险（RR 2.78；95%CI 2.32-3.32）和高级别病变风险（RR 2.5；95%CI 2.05-3.04），高度异质性的结果支持采取以公平为导向的预防策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究聚焦于宫颈癌防控的公平性问题，通过系统综述和荟萃分析，量化了高收入及中高收入国家中多种弱势女性群体（如社会经济地位低下者、移民、HIV感染者等）的宫颈癌及癌前病变风险。其核心创新在于将多种脆弱性因素纳入统一分析框架，并提供了明确的汇总风险比，强有力地证明了健康不平等现象的存在。方法学上，研究遵循了严格的系统综述规范，并进行了偏倚评估。然而，研究也指出结果存在高度异质性，这提示不同亚组间的风险驱动因素可能不同，是未来研究需要细化的方向。总体而言，该研究为制定和实施更具针对性和公平性的宫颈癌预防策略提供了关键证据。

---

## 58. 用于位点特异性抗体药物偶联物工程化的超分子卷曲螺旋肽平台。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771920)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41771920
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70094-y

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Supramolecular coiled-coil peptide platform for site-specific antibody drug conjugate engineering.

> **英文摘要：**
> Antibody conjugates play a central role across multiple healthcare sectors with a prime example being antibody-drug conjugates (ADCs). Although widely used lysine and hinge cysteine conjugation methods yield products, the lack of site-specificity and spatial control along with the highly heterogeneous composition are significant limitations. Herein, we describe a facile supramolecular assembly method based on heterodimer coiled-coil formation for site-specific antibody conjugation that perseveres antibody antigen binding sites for target engagement. The platform method affords uniform loading of diverse payloads including anti-cancer agents, polymers, enzymes, fluorophores, etc. under mild aqueous conditions. Further, the facile convergent approach capitalizes on the independent strengths and flexibility of protein expression and peptide chemistry culminating in a final self-assembly step. An ADC loaded with monomethyl auristatin E targeting ErbB2/Her2 positive tumors significantly reduces tumor体积 in a human ovarian cancer xenograft model outperforming the antibody alone with validated performance against a best-in-class therapeutic.

> **中文摘要：**
> 抗体偶联物在多个医疗领域发挥着核心作用，其中抗体药物偶联物（ADCs）是一个主要例子。虽然广泛使用的赖氨酸和铰链区半胱氨酸偶联方法能够产生产品，但缺乏位点特异性和空间控制，以及高度异质的组成是显著的局限性。在此，我们描述了一种基于异源二聚体卷曲螺旋形成的简便超分子组装方法，用于位点特异性抗体偶联，该方法保留了抗体的抗原结合位点以用于靶标结合。该平台方法能够在温和的水相条件下，实现对多种有效载荷（包括抗癌剂、聚合物、酶、荧光团等）的均匀负载。此外，这种简便的汇聚式方法利用了蛋白质表达和肽化学各自独立的优势和灵活性，最终通过一个自组装步骤完成。一种负载了单甲基澳瑞他汀E、靶向ErbB2/Her2阳性肿瘤的ADC，在人类卵巢癌异种移植模型中显著减小了肿瘤体积，其效果优于单独使用抗体，并且其性能经过验证，可与同类最佳疗法相媲美。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决传统抗体药物偶联物（ADC）因非特异性偶联导致的异质性问题。其核心创新在于开发了一种基于异源二聚体卷曲螺旋肽的超分子自组装平台，实现了抗体的位点特异性、均一性修饰，同时保留了抗体的抗原结合能力。该平台方法通用性强，可在温和条件下负载多种类型载荷，并通过汇聚式策略简化了制备流程。体内实验证明，基于此平台构建的靶向Her2的ADC在卵巢癌模型中展现出优于单独抗体、且与同类最佳疗法相当的抗肿瘤活性。然而，摘要未提及该平台方法的潜在免疫原性、大规模生产的可行性以及与传统偶联方法在稳定性、药代动力学方面的系统比较，这些是未来转化应用需关注的方向。

---

## 59. 出版者更正：OTX2-PAX3信号轴调控第3组髓母细胞瘤细胞命运。

**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41771917
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70147-2

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Publisher Correction: An OTX2-PAX3 signaling axis regulates Group 3 medulloblastoma cell fate.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无摘要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文为《自然-通讯》期刊的一则出版者更正，其原始研究聚焦于髓母细胞瘤（第3组）的分子机制。研究核心在于揭示了OTX2与PAX3之间的信号轴在调控该亚型肿瘤细胞命运中的关键作用，这为理解其发病机理提供了新的分子视角。鉴于其为更正信息，无法评估其具体的研究方法、发现及创新性。该信息提示原始研究可能涉及重要的信号通路发现，但需查阅原文以获取完整科学内容。

## 60. 使用TMT-Integrator与FragPipe计算平台分析等重定量蛋白质组学数据

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771895)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41771895
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70118-7

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Analysis of isobaric quantitative proteomic data using TMT-Integrator and FragPipe computational platform.

> **英文摘要：**
> Isobaric mass tags, such as isobaric tags for relative and absolute quantitation (iTRAQ) and tandem mass tag (TMT), are widely utilized for peptide and protein quantification in multiplex quantitative proteomics. We present TMT-Integrator, a bioinformatics tool for processing quantitation results from TMT and iTRAQ experiments, offering integrative reports at the gene, protein, peptide, and post-translational modification site levels. We demonstrate the versatility of TMT-Integrator using five publicly available TMT datasets: clear cell renal cell carcinoma (ccRCC) whole proteome and phosphoproteome datasets from the Clinical Proteomic Tumor Analysis Consortium, an E. coli dataset with 13 spike-in proteins, and two human cell lysate datasets showcasing the latest advances with the Thermo Orbitrap Astral mass spectrometer and TMTpro 35-plex reagents. Integrated into the widely used FragPipe computational platform (https://fragpipe.nesvilab.org/), TMT-Integrator is a core component of TMT and iTRAQ data analysis workflows. We evaluated the performance of FragPipe coupled with TMT-Integrator analysis pipeline against MaxQuant and Proteome Discoverer with multiple benchmarks, facilitated by the bioinformatics tool OmicsEV. Our results show that FragPipe coupled with TMT-Integrator quantifies more proteins in the E. coli and ccRCC whole proteome datasets, quantifies more phosphorylated sites in the ccRCC phosphoproteome dataset, and overall delivers more robust quantification performance compared to other tools.

> **中文摘要：**
> 等重质量标签，例如相对和绝对定量等重标签（iTRAQ）和串联质量标签（TMT），被广泛用于多重定量蛋白质组学中的肽段和蛋白质定量。我们推出了TMT-Integrator，这是一个用于处理TMT和iTRAQ实验定量结果的生物信息学工具，可在基因、蛋白质、肽段和翻译后修饰位点水平提供整合报告。我们使用五个公开可用的TMT数据集展示了TMT-Integrator的多功能性：来自临床蛋白质组肿瘤分析联盟的透明细胞肾细胞癌（ccRCC）全蛋白质组和磷酸化蛋白质组数据集、一个包含13种掺入蛋白的大肠杆菌数据集，以及两个展示Thermo Orbitrap Astral质谱仪和TMTpro 35-plex试剂最新进展的人细胞裂解液数据集。TMT-Integrator已集成到广泛使用的FragPipe计算平台（https://fragpipe.nesvilab.org/）中，是TMT和iTRAQ数据分析工作流程的核心组件。我们在生物信息学工具OmicsEV的辅助下，通过多个基准测试，评估了FragPipe结合TMT-Integrator分析流程相对于MaxQuant和Proteome Discoverer的性能。我们的结果表明，与其他工具相比，FragPipe结合TMT-Integrator在大肠杆菌和ccRCC全蛋白质组数据集中定量了更多的蛋白质，在ccRCC磷酸化蛋白质组数据集中定量了更多的磷酸化位点，并且总体上提供了更稳健的定量性能。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在介绍并验证一个集成于FragPipe平台的新型生物信息学工具TMT-Integrator，用于处理基于TMT/iTRAQ等重标签的定量蛋白质组学数据。其核心创新在于提供了一个从基因到翻译后修饰位点的多层次整合分析框架，并通过整合多个公开数据集（包括临床肿瘤样本和标准品）展示了其通用性。性能评估表明，该流程在蛋白质和磷酸化位点的鉴定数量及定量稳健性上优于MaxQuant和Proteome Discoverer等主流工具，为高通量蛋白质组学数据分析提供了一个有力的解决方案。然而，摘要未提及该工具在计算效率、用户友好性方面的具体表现，也未讨论其在处理更复杂修饰或与其他组学数据整合方面的潜力。

## 61. 通过平铺碱基编辑的等位基因读出实现调控元件的核苷酸分辨率图谱绘制。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771871)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41771871
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-69918-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Nucleotide-resolution mapping of regulatory elements via allelic readout of tiled base editing.

> **英文摘要：**
> CRISPR tiling screens have enabled the characterization of regulatory sequences but are limited by low resolution arising from the indirect readout of editing via guide RNA sequencing and enrichment analysis. This study introduces an end-to-end experimental assay and computational pipeline, which leverages targeted sequencing of CRISPR-introduced alleles at the endogenous target locus following dense base-editing mutagenesis. As a proof of concept, we studied a putative CD19 enhancer, an immunotherapy target in leukemia, and identified alleles and single nucleotides crucial for CD19 regulation. Our visualization tools revealed transcription factor motifs corresponding to the top-ranked nucleotides. Validation experiments confirmed that mutations in MYB, PAX5, and EBF1 binding sites reduce CD19 expression. Critically, editing MYB and PAX5 motifs conferred resistance to CD19 CAR-T cell therapy, revealing how non-coding variants can drive immunotherapy escape. Taken together, this approach achieves nucleotide-resolution genotype-phenotype mapping at regulatory elements beyond conventional gRNA-based screens.

> **中文摘要：**
> CRISPR平铺筛选技术已能表征调控序列，但其分辨率较低，原因在于需要通过向导RNA测序和富集分析间接解读编辑结果。本研究引入了一种端到端的实验检测方法和计算流程，该方法利用密集碱基编辑诱变后，对内源性靶位点上CRISPR引入的等位基因进行靶向测序。作为概念验证，我们研究了一个假定的CD19增强子（白血病免疫治疗靶点），并鉴定出对CD19调控至关重要的等位基因和单个核苷酸。我们的可视化工具揭示了与排名靠前的核苷酸相对应的转录因子基序。验证实验证实，MYB、PAX5和EBF1结合位点的突变会降低CD19表达。关键的是，编辑MYB和PAX5基序会赋予对CD19 CAR-T细胞疗法的耐药性，揭示了非编码变异如何驱动免疫治疗逃逸。综上所述，该方法在调控元件上实现了超越传统基于gRNA筛选的核苷酸分辨率基因型-表型图谱绘制。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在克服传统CRISPR平铺筛选分辨率低的局限，开发了一种结合密集碱基编辑与内源等位基因靶向测序的新方法。其核心创新在于实现了对调控元件的核苷酸分辨率功能解析，并以CD19增强子为例，精准鉴定了关键核苷酸及对应的转录因子结合位点。最重要的发现是，编辑MYB和PAX5基序可导致CD19 CAR-T疗法耐药，直接揭示了非编码区变异介导免疫逃逸的机制。该方法将基因型-表型关联研究提升至单碱基水平，但作为概念验证，其普适性及在不同细胞/基因组环境下的表现仍需进一步评估。

## 62. 更正：扩大异基因干细胞移植对急性髓系白血病患者生存率的影响：一项基于人群的研究。

本文是一篇更正声明，其关联的原始研究旨在评估扩大异基因干细胞移植（allo-SCT）应用范围对急性髓系白血病（AML）患者群体生存结局的影响。研究采用基于人群的观察性研究方法，具有较好的外部真实性，能够反映真实世界的临床实践变化。其核心创新性在于从公共卫生和医疗政策层面，量化了扩大移植适应症所带来的生存获益。然而，作为观察性研究，其结论可能受到混杂因素的影响，且更正声明的具体内容未知，可能涉及数据、方法或结论的重要修正，读者需结合原始及更正文献审慎解读。

## 63. 亚介观尺度蛋白质复合物中大尺度转迁路径与中间构象的高效采样。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771853)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41771853
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-69809-y

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Efficient sampling of large-scale transition pathways and intermediate conformations in sub-mesoscopic protein complexes.

> **英文摘要：**
> Protein conformational changes are the cornerstone of biological function. While conformers captured experimentally represent metastable states, the pathways connecting them have been elusive for experiments and simulations alike. Nowadays, cryogenic Electron Microscopy is providing rich structural data on proteins trapped in different states for increasingly large systems, but these are out of scope for most computational methods which exhibit an N dependence on size. Based on our previous eBDIMS algorithm, here we present eBDIMS2, an optimized version with quasi-linear size dependence, able to simulate on a desktop computer particularly complex transitions for megadalton protein assemblies, like the rotary motion of ATP synthases. Not only eBDIMS2 pathways spontaneously visit experimental intermediates but also overlap with enhanced and microsecond Molecular Dynamics simulations requiring extensive supercomputing resources. By integrating Elastic Networks with Brownian Dynamics, eBDIMS2 allows an unprecedented exploration of conformational changes of sub-mesoscopic systems previously inaccessible.

> **中文摘要：**
> 蛋白质构象变化是生物功能的基石。虽然实验捕获的构象异构体代表了亚稳态，但连接它们的路径对于实验和模拟研究而言都难以捉摸。如今，冷冻电子显微镜正在为日益增大的蛋白质系统提供丰富的、捕获于不同状态的结构数据，但这些数据超出了大多数计算方法的适用范围，因为这些方法表现出与尺寸相关的N次方依赖性。基于我们之前的eBDIMS算法，本文提出了eBDIMS2，这是一个具有准线性尺寸依赖性的优化版本，能够在台式计算机上模拟兆道尔顿级蛋白质组装体的特别复杂的转迁过程，例如ATP合酶的旋转运动。eBDIMS2的路径不仅能自发地访问实验观察到的中间态，而且与需要大量超级计算资源的增强采样及微秒级分子动力学模拟的结果相吻合。通过将弹性网络与布朗动力学相结合，eBDIMS2使得对先前无法触及的亚介观尺度系统的构象变化进行前所未有的探索成为可能。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决大尺度蛋白质复合物构象转迁路径采样的计算瓶颈。其核心是开发了eBDIMS2算法，通过整合弹性网络与布朗动力学，实现了计算复杂度从N次方到准线性的优化，从而能在普通台式机上模拟如ATP合酶旋转等兆道尔顿级复合物的复杂运动。研究发现，该算法不仅能自发重现实验观测的中间构象，其预测路径也与资源密集型的增强分子动力学模拟结果高度一致，验证了其有效性。其创新性在于极大地降低了对超大生物分子系统进行构象动力学探索的计算门槛，但局限性在于该方法本质上是粗粒化模型，其精度与原子细节仍需结合全原子模拟或实验数据进行验证与补充。

---

## 64. 脂肪干细胞分泌的Lamp2a偶联RNA可阻断三阴性乳腺癌中ENO1-乳酸化-糖酵解反馈环路及细胞恶性行为。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771848)
**期刊：** Cell death & disease
**PMID：** 41771848
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41419-026-08517-3

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A Lamp2a-linked RNA secreted by ADSCs prevents ENO1-lactylation-glycolysis feedback and cell malignant behavior in triple-negative breast cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Triple-negative breast cancer (TNBC) is a subtype characterized by the absence of common BC receptors and is closely associated with a hypoxic tumor microenvironment. However, the mechanisms through which TNBCs adapt to hypoxia remain elusive. This study revealed elevated ENO1 levels in various BC datasets and revealed ENO1 protein lactylation in BC samples through 4D label-free lactylation quantitative proteomics analysis. The results indicated that lactylation increases ENO1 protein stability and enzyme activity, which promotes glycolysis. Notably, as lactate levels increased, a positive feedback loop was established, further promoting lactylation of ENO1. This positive feedback mechanism enables TNBC cells to adapt more efficiently to hypoxia and enhances their malignant behaviors. Lactylation prevented the lysosomal degradation of ENO1. In this study, the characteristics of ENO1, an RNA-binding protein, were assessed to determine how to interfere with its lactylation; specifically, an RNA ligand that can be specifically bound by ENO1 was identified. The RNA ligand was found to be linked to the Lamp2a protein in adipose stem cells (ADSCs) after stable transfection with Lamp2a-TAT and TRA-ligand plasmids. ADSCs seeded in a polyglycolic acid scaffold secreted exosomes containing the Lamp2a-linked ligand. This RNA ligand binds to ENO1 after it enters TNBC cells and further induces the lysosomal degradation of ENO1 by the Lamp2a protein. Consequently, glycolysis, which is associated with malignant cell behaviors, is inhibited. Overall, this study elucidated the role of ENO1 lactylation-mediated glycolysis in TNBC adaptation to hypoxia and provides a strategy for targeting ENO1.

> **中文摘要：**
> 三阴性乳腺癌（TNBC）是一种缺乏常见乳腺癌受体的亚型，与缺氧的肿瘤微环境密切相关。然而，TNBC适应缺氧的机制尚不清楚。本研究通过多种乳腺癌数据集揭示了ENO1水平升高，并通过4D非标记乳酸化定量蛋白质组学分析在乳腺癌样本中发现了ENO1蛋白的乳酸化。结果表明，乳酸化增加了ENO1蛋白的稳定性和酶活性，从而促进糖酵解。值得注意的是，随着乳酸水平升高，形成了一个正反馈环路，进一步促进了ENO1的乳酸化。这种正反馈机制使TNBC细胞能更有效地适应缺氧并增强其恶性行为。乳酸化阻止了ENO1的溶酶体降解。本研究评估了RNA结合蛋白ENO1的特性，以确定如何干扰其乳酸化；具体而言，鉴定了一种可被ENO1特异性结合的RNA配体。研究发现，在用Lamp2a-TAT和TRA-配体质粒稳定转染后，该RNA配体在脂肪干细胞（ADSCs）中与Lamp2a蛋白连接。接种在聚乙醇酸支架中的ADSCs分泌出含有Lamp2a偶联配体的外泌体。该RNA配体进入TNBC细胞后与ENO1结合，并进一步通过Lamp2a蛋白诱导ENO1的溶酶体降解。因此，与恶性细胞行为相关的糖酵解受到抑制。总之，本研究阐明了ENO1乳酸化介导的糖酵解在TNBC适应缺氧中的作用，并提供了一种靶向ENO1的策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明三阴性乳腺癌（TNBC）适应缺氧的分子机制，并开发靶向干预策略。核心发现是揭示了ENO1蛋白乳酸化通过稳定蛋白、增强活性来驱动糖酵解，并与乳酸生成形成正反馈环路，从而促进TNBC的恶性行为。其创新性在于，不仅解析了ENO1乳酸化在代谢重编程中的关键作用，还巧妙地利用ENO1的RNA结合特性，设计了一种基于脂肪干细胞外泌体递送的Lamp2a偶联RNA配体，通过诱导ENO1溶酶体降解来打破该反馈环路。然而，研究目前主要基于体外和模型系统，这种基于工程化干细胞的治疗策略在体内的安全性、递送效率及长期效果仍需进一步临床前验证。

---

## 65. 靶向FNIP2-SERCA2b轴可改善共济失调毛细血管扩张症中的代谢与线粒体缺陷。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771847)
**期刊：** Cell death & disease
**PMID：** 41771847
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41419-026-08507-5

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Targeting the FNIP2-SERCA2b axis improves metabolic and mitochondrial defects in Ataxia Telangiectasia.

> **英文摘要：**
> Ataxia telangiectasia (AT) is a rare multisystem disorder caused by the loss of functional ATM protein, leading to immunodeficiency, cancer predisposition, neurodegeneration, diabetes, heart failure, and premature aging. Although ATM's role as a sensor of DNA double-strand breaks (DSBs) is well established, the mechanisms underlying the diverse AT phenotypes remain incompletely understood, with evidence suggesting they extend beyond DSB sensing. Here, we uncover widespread glycogen accumulation as a key feature of AT cells and tissues, driven by dysregulated glucose metabolism and impaired mitochondrial respiration assessed with a multidimensional approach including metabolomics, flux analysis, histopathology, bioenergetic measurements, and electron tomography. These metabolic defects contribute to reduced cellular viability and premature senescence observed in AT patient-derived cells. Strikingly, inactivation of FNIP2, which controls mitochondrial respiration, partially rescues these defects in AT cellular models. We show that FNIP2 interacts with the SERCA2b calcium channel, and its inactivation enhances cytoplasmic calcium availability, stimulating mitochondrial respiration and increasing glucose consumption. This metabolic reprogramming prevents glycogen accumulation and improves survival in AT primary cells. Our findings provide novel insights into AT pathophysiology and indicate the FNIP2-SERCA2b axis as a novel potential target for mitigating the systemic effects of AT and improving outcomes in this complex disease.

> **中文摘要：**
> 共济失调毛细血管扩张症（AT）是一种由功能性ATM蛋白缺失引起的罕见多系统疾病，可导致免疫缺陷、癌症易感性、神经退行性变、糖尿病、心力衰竭和早衰。尽管ATM作为DNA双链断裂（DSBs）传感器的作用已得到充分证实，但导致多种AT表型的机制仍未完全阐明，有证据表明这些机制超出了DSB感知的范围。在此，我们通过代谢组学、通量分析、组织病理学、生物能量学测量和电子断层扫描等多维方法评估发现，葡萄糖代谢失调和线粒体呼吸受损驱动了广泛的糖原积累，这是AT细胞和组织的一个关键特征。这些代谢缺陷导致了在AT患者来源细胞中观察到的细胞活力降低和早衰。引人注目的是，失活控制线粒体呼吸的FNIP2，可在AT细胞模型中部分挽救这些缺陷。我们发现FNIP2与SERCA2b钙通道相互作用，其失活增强了细胞质钙的可用性，从而刺激线粒体呼吸并增加葡萄糖消耗。这种代谢重编程阻止了糖原积累，并提高了AT原代细胞的存活率。我们的发现为AT的病理生理学提供了新的见解，并指出FNIP2-SERCA2b轴是一个新的潜在靶点，可用于减轻AT的系统性影响并改善这一复杂疾病的预后。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在超越ATM蛋白经典的DNA损伤感知功能，深入探究共济失调毛细血管扩张症（AT）复杂表型背后的代谢与线粒体机制。研究团队采用多维技术组合，系统揭示了AT中葡萄糖代谢失调和线粒体功能障碍导致糖原累积的关键病理特征。其核心创新在于发现并验证了FNIP2-SERCA2b钙信号轴是调控这一代谢缺陷的关键节点，其失活可重塑细胞代谢、改善细胞存活，为AT提供了全新的潜在治疗靶点。然而，研究目前主要基于细胞模型，其治疗策略在动物模型和人体中的有效性与安全性仍需进一步验证。

---

## 66. Shp1磷酸酶调控CXCR2蛋白稳定性及IL8介导的乳腺癌侵袭性。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771840)
**期刊：** Cell death & disease
**PMID：** 41771840
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41419-026-08516-4

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Shp1 phosphatase regulates CXCR2 protein stability and IL8-mediated invasiveness in breast cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Shp1 is a cytosolic tyrosine phosphatase generally associated with antitumor effects through the inhibition of tyrosine kinase signaling. Herein, we shown that genetic and pharmacological inhibition of Shp1 in breast cancer cells induces accelerated cell migration and promotes a more invasive phenotype. Furthermore, we found that interleukin-8 (IL8), a chemokine with multiple pro-tumorigenic roles within the tumor microenvironment, directly modulates Shp1 activity. In breast cancer, IL8 elicits its functions through the binding to the CXCR2 receptor with the subsequent modulation of several intracellular signaling pathways. We show that in breast MCF7 cells, IL8 induces the PKC-mediated phosphorylation of Shp1 at Ser591, diminishing its enzymatic activity and impairing the dephosphorylation of PP2A; this enhances CXCR2 phosphorylation and alters receptor trafficking by promoting ubiquitination and degradation of CXCR2. This feedback mechanism limits IL8 signaling revealing a previously unrecognized mechanism of receptor turnover and signal attenuation. In addition, we found that Shp1-mediated regulation of CXCR2 directly influences IL8-driven invasiveness in a subtype-specific manner, affecting luminal and triple-negative breast cancer (TNBC) cells but not HER2-positive ones. Transcriptomic and pathway analyses further support Shp1 involvement in cytokine and GPCR signaling, particularly in TNBC, where its downregulation correlates with reduced survival and higher IL8 levels. Taken together, our findings elucidate a novel mechanism of IL8 signaling and identify Shp1 as a promising therapeutic target, highlighting the potential of modulating the CXCR2-Shp1 axis to limit invasiveness and metastasis in aggressive breast cancer subtypes, particularly TNBC.

> **中文摘要：**
> Shp1是一种胞质酪氨酸磷酸酶，通常通过抑制酪氨酸激酶信号传导而发挥抗肿瘤作用。本文中，我们发现，在乳腺癌细胞中通过遗传学和药理学手段抑制Shp1会诱导细胞迁移加速并促进更具侵袭性的表型。此外，我们发现白细胞介素-8（IL8）——一种在肿瘤微环境中具有多种促肿瘤作用的趋化因子——直接调节Shp1的活性。在乳腺癌中，IL8通过与CXCR2受体结合并随后调节多个细胞内信号通路来发挥其功能。我们在乳腺癌MCF7细胞中证明，IL8诱导PKC介导的Shp1在Ser591位点的磷酸化，从而降低其酶活性并损害其对PP2A的去磷酸化作用；这增强了CXCR2的磷酸化，并通过促进CXCR2的泛素化和降解来改变受体运输。这一反馈机制限制了IL8信号传导，揭示了一种先前未被认识的受体周转和信号衰减机制。此外，我们发现Shp1介导的CXCR2调控以亚型特异性方式直接影响IL8驱动的侵袭性，影响管腔型和三阴性乳腺癌（TNBC）细胞，但不影响HER2阳性细胞。转录组学和通路分析进一步支持Shp1参与细胞因子和GPCR信号传导，特别是在TNBC中，其下调与患者生存期缩短和IL8水平升高相关。综上所述，我们的研究结果阐明了一种新的IL8信号传导机制，并将Shp1确定为一个有前景的治疗靶点，突出了调节CXCR2-Shp1轴以限制侵袭性乳腺癌亚型（特别是TNBC）侵袭和转移的潜力。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在揭示Shp1磷酸酶在乳腺癌IL8/CXCR2信号轴中的新作用。通过遗传/药理学抑制、分子互作与信号通路分析，发现IL8通过PKC磷酸化抑制Shp1活性，形成一个负反馈环路，促进CXCR2泛素化降解以限制信号过度激活，并证明该调控具有亚型特异性（影响管腔型和TNBC，而非HER2阳性型）。其创新性在于颠覆了Shp1单纯作为抑癌因子的传统认知，揭示了其在受体稳定性调控中的双重角色，并提出了靶向CXCR2-Shp1轴的治疗新策略；局限性在于主要发现基于细胞模型，体内功能验证及临床转化潜力有待进一步探索。

## 67. 通过剪接转换靶向致癌性BCS1L异构体，通过破坏线粒体功能抑制卵巢癌进展。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771836)
**期刊：** Cell death & disease
**PMID：** 41771836
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41419-026-08495-6

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Splice-switching of the oncogenic BCS1L isoform suppresses ovarian cancer progression by disrupting mitochondrial function.

> **英文摘要：**
> Increasing evidences demonstrate that mitochondrial function is essential for cancer cell survival and metastasis. However, the role of mitochondrial metabolic reprogramming in ovarian cancer progression remains largely unknown. Here, we report that mitochondrial chaperone BCS1L generates two major alternative-spliced isoforms, a full-length isoform (BCS1L-L) and a short isoform lacking exon 2 (BCS1L-S). Interestingly, BCS1L-L is elevated in several human cancers, and it significantly increased oxidative phosphorylation and ATP production in the present work, which is required for the survival of cancer cells. In contrast, BCS1L-S was unable to localize to the mitochondria as BCS1L-L did, and this led to impaired metabolic function. Mechanistically, splicing factor USP39 promoted exon 2 inclusion, thus facilitating the generation of oncogenic BCS1L-L and, thereby, maintaining mitochondrial homeostasis and survival of ovarian cancer cells. Importantly, we developed splice-switch antisense oligonucleotides (ASOs) that successfully induced exon 2 skipping and decreased BCS1L-L abundance, resulting in impaired tumor growth. These findings suggest that targeting oncogenic BCS1L-L by ASOs is a novel approach for ovarian cancer treatment.

> **中文摘要：**
> 越来越多的证据表明，线粒体功能对于癌细胞的存活和转移至关重要。然而，线粒体代谢重编程在卵巢癌进展中的作用在很大程度上仍然未知。本研究报道，线粒体伴侣蛋白BCS1L产生两种主要的可变剪接异构体：全长异构体（BCS1L-L）和缺乏外显子2的短异构体（BCS1L-S）。有趣的是，BCS1L-L在多种人类癌症中表达升高，并且在本研究中，它显著增加了氧化磷酸化和ATP的产生，而这是癌细胞存活所必需的。相比之下，BCS1L-S无法像BCS1L-L那样定位于线粒体，这导致了代谢功能受损。从机制上讲，剪接因子USP39促进了外显子2的保留，从而促进了致癌性BCS1L-L的生成，进而维持了卵巢癌细胞的线粒体稳态和存活。重要的是，我们开发了剪接转换反义寡核苷酸（ASOs），成功诱导了外显子2的跳跃并降低了BCS1L-L的丰度，从而导致肿瘤生长受损。这些发现表明，通过ASOs靶向致癌性BCS1L-L是治疗卵巢癌的一种新方法。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索线粒体代谢重编程在卵巢癌进展中的作用，并开发靶向治疗新策略。其核心发现是，线粒体伴侣蛋白BCS1L的可变剪接异构体BCS1L-L具有致癌性，通过剪接因子USP39调控其生成，从而维持癌细胞线粒体功能与存活。研究创新性地开发了诱导外显子跳跃的ASOs，成功抑制了肿瘤生长，为卵巢癌治疗提供了新的潜在靶点。然而，研究主要基于体外和动物模型，其临床转化效果和潜在毒性仍需进一步评估。

---

## 68. GPR54通过多巴脱羧酶调控非小细胞肺癌的发展。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771825)
**期刊：** Signal transduction and targeted therapy
**PMID：** 41771825
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41392-026-02591-x

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** GPR54 regulates non-small cell lung cancer development via dopa decarboxylase.

> **英文摘要：**
> Non-small cell lung cancer (NSCLC), the most common type of lung cancer, is a leading cause of cancer death. G protein-coupled receptor 54 (GPR54) plays a role in cancer development by interacting with its endogenous ligand kisspeptin encoded by the KISS1 gene. However, the role of GPR54 in NSCLC development is not yet fully understood. Here, we demonstrate that GPR54 regulates NSCLC development via dopa decarboxylase (DDC). A mutant Kras-driven mouse lung cancer model revealed that adenoviral CMV-Cre-mediated Gpr54 deletion attenuated NSCLC development. Both Gpr54 deletion in mouse NSCLC tissues and GPR54 knockdown in human NSCLC cell lines caused apoptotic cell death. In addition, GPR54 regulation of NSCLC cell proliferation involves both the Gα/AKT and β-arrestin/ERK signaling pathways. RNA sequencing revealed that Gpr54 deletion altered a gene set related to glycolysis and genotype-dependently regulated Ddc gene expression. Moreover, the regulation of glycolysis and DDC expression by GPR54 was dependent on the Gα/PI3K/AKT/mTOR signaling pathway. Phosphoprotein arrays further revealed that DDC regulated NF-κB phosphorylation in NSCLC cells. Consistently, DDC regulated both NSCLC cell proliferation in vitro and tumor growth in vivo. Overall, our findings suggest that GPR54 could be a diagnostic marker for NSCLC and that therapeutics targeting GPR54 signaling may be useful for treating NSCLC.

> **中文摘要：**
> 非小细胞肺癌（NSCLC）是最常见的肺癌类型，也是癌症死亡的主要原因。G蛋白偶联受体54（GPR54）通过与KISS1基因编码的内源性配体kisspeptin相互作用，在癌症发展中发挥作用。然而，GPR54在NSCLC发展中的作用尚未完全阐明。本研究证明，GPR54通过多巴脱羧酶（DDC）调控NSCLC的发展。在Kras突变驱动的小鼠肺癌模型中，腺病毒CMV-Cre介导的Gpr54缺失减弱了NSCLC的发展。在小鼠NSCLC组织中删除Gpr54以及在人类NSCLC细胞系中敲低GPR54均导致细胞凋亡性死亡。此外，GPR54对NSCLC细胞增殖的调控涉及Gα/AKT和β-arrestin/ERK信号通路。RNA测序显示，Gpr54缺失改变了与糖酵解相关的基因集，并以基因型依赖性的方式调控了Ddc基因的表达。进一步发现，GPR54对糖酵解和DDC表达的调控依赖于Gα/PI3K/AKT/mTOR信号通路。磷酸化蛋白芯片分析进一步揭示，DDC调控了NSCLC细胞中NF-κB的磷酸化。与此一致的是，DDC在体外调控NSCLC细胞增殖，在体内调控肿瘤生长。总之，我们的研究结果表明，GPR54可能作为NSCLC的诊断标志物，而靶向GPR54信号通路的疗法可能有助于治疗NSCLC。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明GPR54在非小细胞肺癌（NSCLC）发展中的具体作用机制。研究综合运用了Kras突变小鼠模型、细胞系基因敲低、RNA测序和磷酸化蛋白芯片等多种技术方法，揭示了GPR54通过调控下游多巴脱羧酶（DDC）的表达，并经由Gα/PI3K/AKT/mTOR和β-arrestin/ERK等多条信号通路，影响糖酵解、NF-κB磷酸化，最终调控NSCLC细胞增殖与肿瘤生长的分子机制。其创新性在于首次将GPR54与DDC在NSCLC中联系起来，并系统描绘了其下游信号网络，为NSCLC的诊断和治疗提供了新的潜在靶点。然而，研究主要基于临床前模型，其转化应用价值仍需后续临床研究验证。

## 70. 纵向血浆代谢组学指导食管鳞状细胞癌化学免疫治疗的动态风险评估与饮食调控。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41771153)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41771153
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-1449

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Longitudinal Plasma Metabolomics Guides Dynamic Risk Assessment and Dietary Modulation for Esophageal Squamous Cell Cancer Chemoimmunotherapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> Esophageal squamous cell carcinoma (ESCC) exhibits heterogeneous responses to chemoimmunotherapy, with only a minority achieving durable benefit, necessitating dynamic precision monitoring. Through longitudinal plasma metabolomics of 541 serial samples from 252 ESCORT-1st trial patients receiving chemoimmunotherapy plus three independent cohorts of 288 samples, we established an integrated risk assessment framework spanning the entire therapeutic continuum: (1) a baseline predictor for initial responders based on metabolite signatures; (2) an on-treatment predictor in prognosticating long-term responders among initial ones based on treatment-induced metabolic shift patterns; (3) a real-time model based on dual alteration of sphingolipid and glycerophospholipid dynamically stratifying progression风险。 Meanwhile, two dietary metabolites, garlic-derived S-allyl-L-cysteine and cruciferous vegetable-derived indole-3-carbinol, were confirmed to improve outcomes by promoting NK cells infiltration and reversing CD8+ T cells exhaustion. In conclusion, we provide the first metabolomic roadmap for precision chemoimmunotherapy in ESCC, unifying baseline prediction, longitudinal surveillance, and dietary modulation into clinically actionable paradigm.

> **中文摘要：**
> 食管鳞状细胞癌（ESCC）对化学免疫治疗的反应具有异质性，仅少数患者能获得持久获益，因此需要动态的精准监测。通过对来自252名接受化学免疫治疗的ESCORT-1st试验患者的541份连续样本以及三个独立队列的288份样本进行纵向血浆代谢组学分析，我们建立了一个覆盖整个治疗过程的综合风险评估框架：（1）基于代谢物特征的基线预测因子，用于识别初始应答者；（2）基于治疗诱导的代谢模式变化，用于在初始应答者中预测长期应答者的治疗中预测因子；（3）基于鞘脂和甘油磷脂双重变化的实时模型，动态分层进展风险。同时，两种膳食代谢物——大蒜来源的S-烯丙基-L-半胱氨酸和十字花科蔬菜来源的吲哚-3-甲醇——被证实可通过促进NK细胞浸润和逆转CD8+ T细胞耗竭来改善预后。总之，我们为ESCC的精准化学免疫治疗提供了首个代谢组学路线图，将基线预测、纵向监测和饮食调控统一为临床可操作的范式。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决食管鳞癌（ESCC）化学免疫治疗疗效异质性的临床难题，核心目的是构建一个动态、精准的代谢组学监测与干预体系。研究团队通过大样本纵向血浆代谢组学分析，创新性地构建了覆盖治疗全程（基线、治疗中、实时）的三层次综合风险评估框架，实现了从静态预测到动态风险分层的跨越。其重要发现是明确了两种特定膳食代谢物（S-烯丙基-L-半胱氨酸和吲哚-3-甲醇）的免疫调节作用，将饮食干预与精准治疗范式相结合。该研究的核心创新在于首次为ESCC化学免疫治疗提供了整合预测、监测与调控的“代谢路线图”，具有显著的临床转化潜力；其局限性在于结论主要基于观察性关联分析，膳食代谢物的具体作用机制和最佳干预方案仍需前瞻性临床试验进一步验证。
