## 74. 基于无标记代谢显微技术的脂肪组织重塑单细胞代谢成像与数字化评分

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770889)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41770889
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202513042

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Single-Cell Metabolic Imaging and Digital Scoring of Fat Tissue Remodeling by Label-Free Metabolic Microscopy.

> **英文摘要：**
> Adipose tissue plasticity and functional heterogeneity play a central role in maintaining energy homeostasis, and their malfunction leads to metabolic disorders such as obesity, diabetes, and cardiometabolic disease. Rapid, single-cell metabolic imaging of intact fat tissue not only extends our understanding of metabolic dynamics and heterogeneity but also holds great potential as a tool for clinical diagnosis. However, the use of exogenous labels and dyes in conventional optical microscopy results in tissue deformation and requires time-consuming tissue preparation. Here, we demonstrated single-cell imaging of metabolic changes and heterogeneity in freshly excised adipose tissues that can distinguish tissue types without the need for exogenous labels using bond-specific, non-destructive, mid-infrared optoacoustic microscopy (MiROM) that allows preserving the native tissue architecture with minimal sample preparation time. Further leveraging MiROM, we monitored intracellular molecular and morphological changes during postnatal remodeling of adipose tissue when metabolic characteristics of adipocytes undergo a transient drastic change. Additionally, we developed a quantitative spatial tissue analysis tool (Q-SAT) to predict the spatial distribution of white fat- and brown fat-like features, providing a robust digital scoring method for adipose tissue phenotypic assessment. Collectively, we implemented MiROM as an enabling technology to provide fast, label-free metabolic imaging of unprocessed adipose tissue, opening a new perspective for understanding and characterizing the morpho-functional dynamics of adipose tissue remodeling.

> **中文摘要：**
> 脂肪组织的可塑性和功能异质性在维持能量稳态中起着核心作用，其功能障碍会导致肥胖、糖尿病和心脏代谢疾病等代谢紊乱。对完整脂肪组织进行快速、单细胞水平的代谢成像，不仅能拓展我们对代谢动态和异质性的理解，也具备作为临床诊断工具的巨大潜力。然而，传统光学显微镜中使用外源性标记物和染料会导致组织变形，且需要耗时的组织制备。在此，我们利用具有化学键特异性、非破坏性的中红外光声显微镜（MiROM），展示了新鲜切除的脂肪组织中代谢变化和异质性的单细胞成像，该方法无需外源性标记即可区分组织类型，并能以最短的样本制备时间保留天然的组织结构。进一步利用MiROM，我们监测了脂肪组织出生后重塑过程中，当脂肪细胞代谢特征发生短暂剧烈变化时的细胞内分子和形态学改变。此外，我们开发了一种定量空间组织分析工具（Q-SAT），用于预测白色脂肪样和棕色脂肪样特征的空间分布，为脂肪组织表型评估提供了一种稳健的数字化评分方法。总之，我们将MiROM作为一种使能技术，实现了对未经处理的脂肪组织进行快速、无标记的代谢成像，为理解和表征脂肪组织重塑的形态-功能动态开辟了新视角。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在开发一种快速、无标记的成像技术，以解析脂肪组织重塑中的单细胞代谢异质性。其核心创新在于应用了中红外光声显微镜（MiROM），该技术无需外源性标记即可实现化学键特异性成像，并最大限度地保留了组织原生结构。研究发现不仅实现了对脂肪细胞代谢动态的实时监测，还通过开发定量空间分析工具（Q-SAT）提供了数字化表型评分方法，为代谢疾病的病理研究提供了新工具。然而，该技术的临床应用潜力尚需在更广泛的样本和疾病模型中进一步验证，且其成像深度可能受限于光声显微技术本身的物理特性。

---

## 75. CDK8/CDK19抑制在原发性免疫性血小板减少症中恢复T细胞稳态

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770851)
**期刊：** Blood
**PMID：** 41770851
**DOI：** 10.1182/blood.2025031332

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** CDK8/CDK19 inhibition restores T-cell homeostasis in primary immune thrombocytopenia.

> **英文摘要：**
> CD4+CD25+Foxp3+ regulatory T cells (Tregs) are pivotal negative regulators of the adaptive immune system. Abnormalities in the number and/or function of Tregs contribute to the pathogenesis of primary immune thrombocytopenia (ITP). Strategies aimed at modulating Tregs offer potential therapeutic opportunities for ITP management. In this study, we demonstrated that inhibition of cyclin-dependent kinase 8 (CDK8) and CDK19 activity by the small-molecule inhibitor AS2863619 (AS) robustly promoted the conversion of CD4+CD25- effector T cells (Teffs) into CD4+CD25+Foxp3+ Tregs, endowing the converted Tregs with lineage stability and potent suppressive capacity. Mechanistically, AS rapidly augmented STAT5 phosphorylation and subsequent Foxp3 induction. STAT5 blockade completely abrogated this effect, confirming that the Treg-promoting activity of AS was critically dependent on STAT5 signaling. In parallel, AS suppressed STAT3 phosphorylation under IL-6-driven conditions, thereby attenuating Th17 polarization. These mechanistic findings were supported by global transcriptomic analysis, which revealed a profound transcriptional shift by broadly suppressing gene programs of Teff differentiation and function while simultaneously upregulating a robust signature characteristic of stable Tregs. Crucially, unbiased upstream analysis of these changes pinpointed STAT5, STAT3, and FOXP3 as the core transcription factors mediating the drug's effect. Functional metabolic analysis further revealed that AS mediated metabolic reprogramming in T cells by suppressing glycolysis, thereby providing the necessary metabolic adaptations for Treg conversion. In a murine model of active ITP, CDK8/CDK19 inhibition elevated Treg frequencies and ameliorated thrombocytopenia in a STAT5-dependent manner. Collectively, our study highlighted the therapeutic potential of CDK8/CDK19 inhibition in restoring immune homeostasis and managing ITP.

> **中文摘要：**
> CD4+CD25+Foxp3+调节性T细胞（Tregs）是适应性免疫系统的关键负向调节因子。Tregs数量和/或功能的异常参与了原发性免疫性血小板减少症（ITP）的发病机制。旨在调节Tregs的策略为ITP管理提供了潜在的治疗机会。在本研究中，我们证明小分子抑制剂AS2863619（AS）对细胞周期蛋白依赖性激酶8（CDK8）和CDK19活性的抑制，有力地促进了CD4+CD25-效应T细胞（Teffs）向CD4+CD25+Foxp3+ Tregs的转化，并赋予转化后的Tregs谱系稳定性和强大的抑制能力。从机制上讲，AS迅速增强了STAT5磷酸化及随后的Foxp3诱导。阻断STAT5完全消除了这一效应，证实了AS的Treg促进作用关键依赖于STAT5信号通路。同时，在IL-6驱动的条件下，AS抑制了STAT3磷酸化，从而减弱了Th17极化。这些机制发现得到了全局转录组分析的支持，该分析揭示了一种深刻的转录转变，即广泛抑制了Teff分化和功能的基因程序，同时上调了稳定Tregs的强健特征性标志。关键的是，对这些变化进行的无偏倚上游分析，确定了STAT5、STAT3和FOXP3是介导药物作用的核心转录因子。功能性代谢分析进一步揭示，AS通过抑制糖酵解介导了T细胞中的代谢重编程，从而为Treg转化提供了必要的代谢适应。在活动性ITP的小鼠模型中，CDK8/CDK19抑制以STAT5依赖的方式提高了Treg频率并改善了血小板减少症。总之，我们的研究强调了CDK8/CDK19抑制在恢复免疫稳态和管理ITP方面的治疗潜力。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索通过靶向CDK8/CDK19调控Treg细胞以治疗原发性免疫性血小板减少症（ITP）的新策略。研究采用小分子抑制剂AS2863619，结合分子机制探索、全局转录组分析、代谢分析及小鼠模型验证，系统性地揭示了该抑制剂通过激活STAT5/Foxp3通路、抑制STAT3/Th17轴并重塑细胞代谢，从而有效促进效应T细胞向稳定且功能强大的Treg细胞转化，并在动物模型中改善疾病表型。其创新性在于首次将CDK8/CDK19抑制与ITP的免疫稳态恢复联系起来，并提供了从转录调控到代谢重编程的多层次机制证据，为ITP的靶向治疗提供了新的候选途径；局限性在于研究主要基于临床前模型，其人体有效性和安全性尚待未来临床试验验证。

---

## 76. BET抑制通过削弱抗体产生和巨噬细胞介导的纤维化以恢复小鼠慢性移植物抗宿主病的肺功能。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770848)
**期刊：** Blood
**PMID：** 41770848
**DOI：** 10.1182/blood.2025031983

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** BET inhibition blunts antibody production and macrophage-mediated fibrosis to restore lung function in murine cGVHD.

> **英文摘要：**
> Chronic graft-versus-host disease (cGVHD) significantly contributes to late mortality after allogeneic stem cell transplantation, with bronchiolitis obliterans syndrome (BOS) being a particularly lethal and treatment-resistant complication despite available therapies. Bromodomain and Extra terminal (BET) proteins are epigenetic readers driving inflammatory transcriptional programs across multiple cell types. We hypothesized that BET inhibition would suppress inflammatory T and B cells while also decreasing macrophage polarization to a profibrotic phenotype, alleviating disease. In an established BOS cGVHD model, BET inhibition reduced germinal center formation and response through a reduction of the CXCL13:CXCR5 axis, inflammatory Tfh/GC B cells in the spleen along with a reduction in plasma cell infiltration within the lung. Mice with cGVHD had elevated pathogenic IgG1 and IgM, both in circulation and deposited on lung tissue, which was attenuated under BET inhibition. Single-cell RNA sequencing analysis revealed distinct cell states in the BOS lung vs. control. In cGVHD mice, GSEA analysis revealed upregulation of profibrotic Arginase1 and Tgfb1 expression in alveolar macrophages (AM) and interstitial macrophages (IM), which was significantly reduced with BET inhibition. Furthermore, BET inhibition targeted lung-infiltrating M2 macrophages, through selective depletion of CD206+FcgR+ IMs and AMs, ultimately resulting in reduced collagen deposition and improved lung function. Our findings reveal a previously unrecognized mechanistic axis of BET regulation during cGVHD fibrosis and highlight BET inhibition as a promising therapeutic strategy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 慢性移植物抗宿主病（cGVHD）是异基因干细胞移植后晚期死亡的重要原因，其中闭塞性细支气管炎综合征（BOS）尽管有现有疗法，仍是一种特别致命且难治的并发症。Bromodomain and Extra terminal (BET) 蛋白是驱动多种细胞类型炎症转录程序的表观遗传阅读器。我们假设BET抑制将抑制炎症性T细胞和B细胞，同时减少巨噬细胞向促纤维化表型的极化，从而缓解疾病。在一个已建立的BOS cGVHD模型中，BET抑制通过降低CXCL13:CXCR5轴、脾脏中的炎症性Tfh/GC B细胞以及肺内浆细胞浸润，减少了生发中心的形成和反应。患有cGVHD的小鼠在循环中和沉积在肺组织上的致病性IgG1和IgM均升高，而BET抑制减弱了这种升高。单细胞RNA测序分析揭示了BOS肺与对照肺之间不同的细胞状态。在cGVHD小鼠中，GSEA分析显示肺泡巨噬细胞（AM）和间质巨噬细胞（IM）中促纤维化的Arginase1和Tgfb1表达上调，而BET抑制显著降低了这种上调。此外，BET抑制通过选择性耗竭CD206+FcgR+的IM和AM，靶向了肺浸润的M2巨噬细胞，最终导致胶原沉积减少和肺功能改善。我们的研究结果揭示了一个先前未被认识的BET调控cGVHD纤维化的机制轴，并强调了BET抑制作为一种有前景的治疗策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索BET蛋白抑制在小鼠cGVHD相关BOS中的治疗潜力及机制。研究采用已建立的BOS cGVHD模型，结合单细胞RNA测序、GSEA分析及功能检测等方法，系统评估了BET抑制对免疫细胞（T/B细胞、巨噬细胞）及纤维化进程的影响。核心发现是BET抑制通过下调CXCL13:CXCR5轴削弱生发中心反应、减少致病抗体产生，并选择性清除促纤维化的M2巨噬细胞亚群，从而减轻肺纤维化并改善肺功能。其创新性在于首次揭示了BET蛋白通过调控巨噬细胞表型在cGVHD纤维化中的关键作用，为治疗提供了新靶点；局限性在于研究结论基于小鼠模型，其向临床转化的有效性及安全性仍需进一步验证。

---

## 77. 固定疗程VenO对比FCR/BR治疗初治、体能状态良好的慢性淋巴细胞白血病患者：3期CRISTALLO试验的主要分析。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770817)
**期刊：** Blood
**PMID：** 41770817
**DOI：** 10.1182/blood.2025030630

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Fixed-duration VenO vs FCR/BR in fit patients with untreated CLL: primary analysis of the phase 3 CRISTALLO trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> The phase 3 CRISTALLO trial (NCT04285567) compared first-line fixed-duration venetoclax-obinutuzumab (VenO) vs fludarabine, cyclophosphamide, and rituximab (FCR)/bendamustine-rituximab (BR) in patients with chronic lymphocytic leukemia, using undetectable minimal residual disease (uMRD) as the sole primary endpoint. Previously untreated patients with a cumulative illness rating scale score ≤6, creatinine clearance ≥70 mL/min, without del(17p)/TP53 mutations were randomized 1:1 to VenO or FCR/BR. The primary endpoint was uMRD (<10-4) in peripheral blood (PB) using next-generation sequencing at month 15. Key secondary endpoints included uMRD (<10-4) in PB and bone marrow (BM) at end of treatment (EOT), and progression-free survival (PFS). uMRD at deeper cutoffs were explored. At data cutoff (March 19, 2024), 80 patients received VenO and 86 received FCR/BR. Baseline characteristics were generally balanced across arms. The primary endpoint was met: 81.3% (VenO) and 54.7% (FCR/BR) achieved uMRD (<10-4) in PB at month 15 (P = .0004). uMRD (<10-4) in PB and BM at EOT was also higher with VenO vs FCR/BR. Short follow-up precluded evaluation of PFS at the first planned interim analysis; however, fewer patients progressed/died with VenO vs FCR/BR (7 vs 13). At month 15, 65.0% (VenO) and 25.6% (FCR/BR) achieved uMRD (<10-6) in PB. The overall safety profile was consistent with the known safety profile of each drug. No patient in the VenO arm was deemed high-risk for tumor lysis syndrome following obinutuzumab debulking; no clinical TLS occurred. These results confirm and extend the findings from the GAIA-CLL13 trial, validating increased depth of response with VenO vs chemoimmunotherapies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 3期CRISTALLO试验（NCT04285567）比较了一线固定疗程维奈克拉-奥妥珠单抗（VenO）与氟达拉滨、环磷酰胺和利妥昔单抗（FCR）/苯达莫司汀-利妥昔单抗（BR）在慢性淋巴细胞白血病患者中的疗效，并将检测不到微小残留病（uMRD）作为唯一主要终点。既往未经治疗、累计疾病评定量表评分≤6分、肌酐清除率≥70 mL/min、无del(17p)/TP53突变的患者被1:1随机分配至VenO组或FCR/BR组。主要终点是第15个月时使用二代测序检测外周血（PB）中的uMRD（<10-4）。关键次要终点包括治疗结束时（EOT）PB和骨髓（BM）中的uMRD（<10-4），以及无进展生存期（PFS）。还探索了更深阈值下的uMRD。截至数据截止日（2024年3月19日），80例患者接受了VenO治疗，86例接受了FCR/BR治疗。各组的基线特征总体平衡。主要终点达成：第15个月时，VenO组和FCR/BR组分别有81.3%和54.7%的患者在PB中达到uMRD（<10-4）（P = .0004）。EOT时，VenO组在PB和BM中达到uMRD（<10-4）的比例也高于FCR/BR组。由于随访时间短，在首次计划的中期分析中无法评估PFS；然而，VenO组相比FCR/BR组进展/死亡的患者更少（7例 vs 13例）。第15个月时，VenO组和FCR/BR组分别有65.0%和25.6%的患者在PB中达到uMRD（<10-6）。总体安全性特征与各药物的已知安全性特征一致。VenO组中无患者在奥妥珠单抗减瘤后被评估为肿瘤溶解综合征高风险；未发生临床TLS。这些结果证实并扩展了GAIA-CLL13试验的发现，验证了VenO相比化学免疫疗法能带来更深的缓解深度。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究（CRISTALLO试验）旨在比较固定疗程VenO方案与传统FCR/BR化学免疫疗法作为一线治疗在体能状态良好的初治CLL患者中的疗效，其创新性地将uMRD作为唯一主要终点，直接评估治疗深度。结果显示，VenO在诱导深度分子学缓解（包括uMRD<10-4和<10-6）方面显著优于化学免疫疗法，且初步显示了更优的疾病控制趋势。该研究验证并强化了GAIA-CLL13试验的结论，支持靶向联合方案在深度缓解方面的优势。主要局限性在于随访时间尚短，无法提供成熟的PFS数据，且研究排除了高危del(17p)/TP53突变患者，限制了结论的普适性。

---

## 78. CSF-1R抑制剂与来那度胺协同作用以促进自体干细胞移植后骨髓瘤的控制。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770790)
**期刊：** Blood
**PMID：** 41770790
**DOI：** 10.1182/blood.2025030207

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** CSF-1R inhibition and lenalidomide synergize to promote myeloma control after autologous stem cell transplantation.

> **英文摘要：**
> Autologous stem cell transplantation (ASCT) with maintenance lenalidomide remains the mainstay of consolidation therapy for eligible multiple myeloma (MM) patients but preventing disease relapse remains a critical unmet need. Here we investigated whether immunosuppressive myeloid populations in bone marrow (BM) correlated with ASCT outcomes. We identified a subset of CD64+CD169+CD163+ macrophages that expressed CSF-1R, PD-L1, and CD155, and were expanded in patients who relapsed post-ASCT. Using a preclinical ASCT model with suboptimal endogenous anti-myeloma activity, we demonstrated that while neither CSF-1R inhibition nor lenalidomide monotherapy significantly improved outcomes, their combination synergistically attenuated disease progression and prolonged survival. Single-cell RNA sequencing revealed that lenalidomide expanded NK-like CD8+ T-cells but paradoxically also increased the frequency of Csf1r+ macrophages. Cell-cell communication analyses identified Csf1r+ macrophages as suppressors of these NK-like and effector-like exhausted (Tphex) CD8 T-cell populations through CD94/NKG2A and PD-L1/PD-1, respectively. CSF-1R blockade depleted these immunosuppressive macrophages, which correlated with decreased expression of inhibitory receptors and enhanced expression of activation markers in Tphex. Given the FDA approval of axatilimab for chronic GVHD, combining CSF-1R blockade with lenalidomide maintenance represents a readily testable strategy to improve progression-free survival after ASCT.

> **中文摘要：**
> 自体干细胞移植（ASCT）联合来那度胺维持治疗仍然是适合的多发性骨髓瘤（MM）患者巩固治疗的基石，但预防疾病复发仍是一个关键的未满足需求。本研究旨在探讨骨髓（BM）中的免疫抑制性髓系细胞群是否与ASCT的预后相关。我们鉴定出一个表达CSF-1R、PD-L1和CD155的CD64+CD169+CD163+巨噬细胞亚群，该亚群在ASCT后复发的患者中扩增。使用一个内源性抗骨髓瘤活性欠佳的临床前ASCT模型，我们证明，虽然单独使用CSF-1R抑制剂或来那度胺均未显著改善预后，但两者联合能协同性地减缓疾病进展并延长生存期。单细胞RNA测序显示，来那度胺扩增了NK样CD8+ T细胞，但矛盾的是也增加了Csf1r+巨噬细胞的频率。细胞间通讯分析确定Csf1r+巨噬细胞分别通过CD94/NKG2A和PD-L1/PD-1通路抑制这些NK样和效应样耗竭（Tphex）CD8 T细胞群。CSF-1R阻断耗竭了这些免疫抑制性巨噬细胞，这与Tphex细胞中抑制性受体表达降低和活化标志物表达增强相关。鉴于axatilimab已获FDA批准用于慢性移植物抗宿主病，将CSF-1R阻断与来那度胺维持治疗相结合，代表了一种易于测试的、旨在改善ASCT后无进展生存期的策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决多发性骨髓瘤ASCT后复发这一临床难题，创新性地将免疫微环境机制与联合治疗策略相结合。其核心发现是，在ASCT后复发的患者骨髓中，存在一个表达CSF-1R的免疫抑制性巨噬细胞亚群，它通过多重抑制性通路削弱了抗肿瘤T细胞功能。研究的关键创新点在于，揭示了来那度胺在扩增有益T细胞的同时，也意外地促进了这些有害巨噬细胞的扩增，从而为联合CSF-1R抑制剂提供了直接的理论依据，并在临床前模型中验证了该联合方案的协同疗效。然而，该结论仍需在临床试验中验证其安全性与有效性，且其机制探索主要聚焦于巨噬细胞与T细胞，其他免疫细胞的作用可能未被充分揭示。

---

## 79. 慢性非感染性腹泻：综述

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770539)
**期刊：** JAMA
**PMID：** 41770539
**DOI：** 10.1001/jama.2026.0872

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Chronic, Noninfectious Diarrhea: A Review.

> **英文摘要：**
> IMPORTANCE: Chronic diarrhea is defined as loose or watery stools lasting longer than 4 weeks and affects approximately 6% to 7% of adults in the US. More than 90% of patients with chronic diarrhea have a noninfectious etiology.
> 
> OBSERVATIONS: The most common causes of chronic, noninfectious diarrhea are irritable bowel syndrome with diarrhea (IBS-D) and functional diarrhea. IBS-D typically presents with recurrent abdominal pain relieved or worsened after defecation. Functional diarrhea is a condition in which more than 25% of bowel movements in the preceding 3 months are loose or watery, but it is not associated with significant abdominal pain. Chronic diarrhea due to a small-bowel source, such as celiac disease or small intestinal bacterial overgrowth, is typically associated with large-volume diarrhea and weight loss, with or without steatorrhea. Celiac disease is an autoimmune condition defined by enteropathy precipitated by exposure to dietary gluten in genetically predisposed individuals, and small intestinal bacterial overgrowth is characterized by excessive bacteria in the small bowel. Chronic diarrhea due to colon pathology, such as bile acid diarrhea and microscopic colitis, typically presents with frequent, low-volume stools, with or without urgency and excess mucus. Bile acid diarrhea is characterized by excess bile acids in the colon, and microscopic colitis is characterized by chronic inflammation on colon biopsies despite normal endoscopic appearance. Evaluation of chronic diarrhea includes serological testing for celiac disease (tissue transglutaminase immunoglobulin A, along with total immunoglobulin A) and stool testing for fecal calprotectin to evaluate for inflammatory bowel disease. Patients with gastrointestinal bleeding, unexplained weight loss, 45 years or older, nocturnal diarrhea, steatorrhea, and/or iron deficiency anemia should undergo colonoscopy to evaluate for colorectal cancer as well as upper endoscopy. During colonoscopy, random biopsies are recommended to evaluate for microscopic colitis, which affects 13% of patients with chronic diarrhea. If evaluation does not identify a cause of chronic diarrhea, likely diagnoses are IBS-D or functional diarrhea and the patient should be treated with lifestyle modification, such as regularly scheduled meals, exercise, intake of at least 8 cups of noncaffeinated fluids daily, limiting caffeine to 3 cups or fewer daily, and avoiding alcohol and carbonated beverages. For general treatment of chronic diarrhea, dietary modifications, such as consuming a diet low in fermentable oligosaccharides (legumes, wheat, onions, garlic), disaccharides (lactose), and monosaccharides (fructose), and polyols (sorbitol, mannitol), or medications, such as opiate agonists (loperamide), anticholinergics (hyoscyamine, dicyclomine), or 5-hydroxytryptamine 3 receptor (5-HT3) antagonists (ondansetron), can be prescribed. These therapies typically improve diarrhea in 50% to 80% of patients.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS AND RELEVANCE: The most common causes of chronic, noninfectious diarrhea include IBS-D and functional diarrhea. Diagnostic testing should include consideration of celiac disease, inflammatory bowel disease, and microscopic colitis. Empiric therapies for chronic diarrhea include lifestyle and dietary modifications and medications, including opiate agonists, anticholinergics, and 5-HT3 antagonists.

> **中文摘要：**
> 重要性：慢性腹泻定义为持续超过4周的稀便或水样便，影响美国约6%至7%的成年人。超过90%的慢性腹泻患者病因是非感染性的。
> 
> 观察结果：慢性非感染性腹泻最常见的病因是腹泻型肠易激综合征（IBS-D）和功能性腹泻。IBS-D通常表现为排便后缓解或加重的复发性腹痛。功能性腹泻是指过去3个月中超过25%的排便为稀便或水样便，但不伴有显著腹痛。源于小肠的慢性腹泻，如乳糜泻或小肠细菌过度生长，通常伴有大量腹泻和体重减轻，伴或不伴脂肪泻。乳糜泻是一种自身免疫性疾病，定义为遗传易感个体因接触膳食麸质而诱发的肠病；小肠细菌过度生长的特征是小肠内细菌过多。源于结肠病变的慢性腹泻，如胆汁酸腹泻和显微镜下结肠炎，通常表现为频繁、少量排便，伴或不伴便急和黏液过多。胆汁酸腹泻的特征是结肠内胆汁酸过多，显微镜下结肠炎的特征是尽管内镜下表现正常，但结肠活检显示慢性炎症。慢性腹泻的评估包括针对乳糜泻的血清学检测（组织转谷氨酰胺酶免疫球蛋白A，以及总免疫球蛋白A）和粪便钙卫蛋白检测以评估炎症性肠病。对于有胃肠道出血、不明原因体重减轻、年龄45岁或以上、夜间腹泻、脂肪泻和/或缺铁性贫血的患者，应进行结肠镜检查以评估结直肠癌，并进行上消化道内镜检查。结肠镜检查期间，建议进行随机活检以评估显微镜下结肠炎，该病影响13%的慢性腹泻患者。如果评估未发现慢性腹泻的病因，可能的诊断是IBS-D或功能性腹泻，患者应接受生活方式调整治疗，例如规律进餐、锻炼、每日摄入至少8杯无咖啡因液体、每日限制咖啡因摄入量在3杯或以下、避免酒精和碳酸饮料。对于慢性腹泻的一般治疗，可以处方饮食调整，例如摄入低可发酵寡糖（豆类、小麦、洋葱、大蒜）、双糖（乳糖）、单糖（果糖）和多元醇（山梨糖醇、甘露醇）的饮食，或药物，如阿片受体激动剂（洛哌丁胺）、抗胆碱能药（莨菪碱、双环胺）或5-羟色胺3受体（5-HT3）拮抗剂（昂丹司琼）。这些疗法通常可使50%至80%患者的腹泻得到改善。
> 
> 结论与相关性：慢性非感染性腹泻最常见的病因包括IBS-D和功能性腹泻。诊断性检测应包括考虑乳糜泻、炎症性肠病和显微镜下结肠炎。慢性腹泻的经验性治疗包括生活方式和饮食调整以及药物，包括阿片受体激动剂、抗胆碱能药和5-HT3拮抗剂。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文是一篇发表于《JAMA》的综述，旨在系统梳理慢性非感染性腹泻的流行病学、病因、诊断路径与治疗策略。其核心目的是为临床医生提供基于证据的实践框架，强调功能性肠病（IBS-D、功能性腹泻）是主要病因，并系统区分了小肠源性（如乳糜泻）与结肠源性（如显微镜下结肠炎）腹泻的临床特征。文章创新性地整合了从血清学、粪便标志物到内镜活检的阶梯式诊断流程，并详细阐述了生活方式干预及分层药物治疗方案。其局限性在于作为一篇叙述性综述，未采用系统综述或荟萃分析的方法论，且主要基于美国人群数据，结论的普适性可能受限。

---

## 80. 帕博利珠单抗单药治疗经索拉非尼治疗和初治的晚期肝细胞癌：开放标签、II期KEYNOTE-224研究的长期随访结果。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770235)
**期刊：** Clinical cancer research : an official journal of the American Association for Cancer Research
**PMID：** 41770235
**DOI：** 10.1158/1078-0432.CCR-25-3528

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Pembrolizumab Monotherapy in Sorafenib-Treated and Treatment-Naive Advanced Hepatocellular Carcinoma: Long-Term Follow-Up of Open-Label, Phase 2 KEYNOTE-224 Study.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: In the phase 2 KEYNOTE-224 study, pembrolizumab showed durable antitumor activity and manageable safety in participants with sorafenib-treated (cohort 1) or treatment-naive (cohort 2) advanced hepatocellular carcinoma (HCC). We present data after a median follow-up of ~7 years for cohort 1 and ~5 years for cohort 2. PARTICIPANTS AND METHODS: Adults with advanced HCC received pembrolizumab 200 mg intravenously every 3 weeks until disease progression or unacceptable toxicity for ≤35 cycles. Primary end point was objective response rate (ORR) per RECIST v1.1 by blinded independent central review (BICR). Secondary end points included overall survival (OS), progression-free survival (PFS), and safety. RESULTS: Overall, 155 participants received ≥1 dose of pembrolizumab (cohort 1, n = 104; cohort 2, n = 51). Median follow-up was 83.0 months (range, 79.3-87.3) for cohort 1 and 58.8 (range, 55.3-60.8) for cohort 2. Median OS was 13.2 months (95% CI, 9.7-15.3) and 16.9 (95% CI, 8.3-23.1), respectively; 24/48-month OS rates were 31%/17% and 34%/20%. Median PFS was 4.9 months (95% CI, 3.5-7.0) and 4.3 (95% CI, 2.1-7.8), respectively. Treatment-related adverse events occurred in 76 participants (73.1%; grade 3-5, 27 [26.0%]) in cohort 1 and 28 participants (54.9%; grade 3-5, 8 [15.7%]) in cohort 2. CONCLUSION: Pembrolizumab continued to show durable response and manageable safety in participants with advanced HCC with or without prior systemic therapy, with long-term effects on OS lasting beyond 48 months in some participants despite receiving study treatment for ≤2 years.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：在II期KEYNOTE-224研究中，帕博利珠单抗在经索拉非尼治疗（队列1）或初治（队列2）的晚期肝细胞癌（HCC）参与者中显示出持久的抗肿瘤活性和可管理的安全性。我们报告队列1中位随访约7年、队列2中位随访约5年后的数据。参与者与方法：晚期HCC成人患者每3周静脉接受帕博利珠单抗200 mg治疗，直至疾病进展或出现不可接受的毒性，治疗周期≤35个。主要终点是盲态独立中心审查（BICR）根据RECIST v1.1评估的客观缓解率（ORR）。次要终点包括总生存期（OS）、无进展生存期（PFS）和安全性。结果：总体而言，155名参与者接受了至少1剂帕博利珠单抗（队列1，n = 104；队列2，n = 51）。队列1的中位随访时间为83.0个月（范围，79.3-87.3），队列2为58.8个月（范围，55.3-60.8）。中位OS分别为13.2个月（95% CI，9.7-15.3）和16.9个月（95% CI，8.3-23.1）；24/48个月OS率分别为31%/17%和34%/20%。中位PFS分别为4.9个月（95% CI，3.5-7.0）和4.3个月（95% CI，2.1-7.8）。队列1中有76名参与者（73.1%；3-5级，27名[26.0%]）发生治疗相关不良事件，队列2中有28名参与者（54.9%；3-5级，8名[15.7%]）。结论：帕博利珠单抗在无论既往是否接受过系统治疗的晚期HCC参与者中，继续显示出持久的缓解和可管理的安全性，部分参与者的OS长期获益持续超过48个月，尽管接受研究治疗的时间≤2年。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究提供了帕博利珠单抗单药治疗晚期肝细胞癌的长期随访数据，中位随访时间长达7年，在免疫治疗领域极为罕见。其核心发现是，无论患者既往是否接受过索拉非尼治疗，帕博利珠单抗均能带来持久的抗肿瘤活性和可控的安全性，且部分患者的总生存获益可长期持续（超过48个月），这提示免疫治疗可能具有“拖尾效应”。研究的主要局限性在于其为单臂、II期设计，缺乏对照组，且样本量相对较小，尤其是初治队列。这些长期数据为帕博利珠单抗在晚期HCC中的疗效持久性提供了重要证据，并支持了免疫检查点抑制剂在该疾病中的治疗价值。

---

## 81. 儿童H3 G34突变弥漫性半球胶质瘤：临床、影像及分子预后因素、MGMT表达与替莫唑胺反应

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770225)
**期刊：** Acta neuropathologica
**PMID：** 41770225
**DOI：** 10.1007/s00401-026-02992-w

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Pediatric H3 G34-mutant diffuse hemispheric glioma: clinical, imaging and molecular prognostic factors, MGMT expression, and temozolomide response.

> **英文摘要：**
> Previous studies have demonstrated poor outcomes in pediatric patients with H3 G34-mutant diffuse hemispheric glioma (DHG). However, the biological basis for this therapeutic resistance remains poorly understood. Furthermore, the effectiveness of temozolomide (TMZ) and the role of surgery in pediatric patients remain uncertain. Therefore, we performed a multi-institutional retrospective analysis of the clinical, imaging, and molecular characteristics of 36 pediatric (≤ 18 years) patients with newly diagnosed H3 G34-mutant DHG. The median age of the cohort was 14 years (8-18 years). The median progression-free survival (PFS) was 0.7 years (95% CI 0.4-1.2 years), and the median overall survival (OS) was 1.8 years (95% CI 1.1-3.2 years). Gross total resection (GTR) was associated with improved PFS (p = 0.0046). Infiltration of three or more brain lobes (gliomatosis cerebri) was noted in 22.6% (7/31) of patients at presentation. Twenty-one patients (58.3%) received frontline TMZ and had improved PFS (p = 0.0049) compared to those who did not. Low MGMT expression was associated with better PFS (p = 0.0039) and better OS (p < 0.0001). In pediatric DHG, gene body/intronic CpG methylation, rather than promoter methylation, correlated with MGMT expression (p < 0.0001). MGMT promoter methylation was not significantly associated with PFS or OS. PDGFRA alterations (n = 13) were associated with inferior OS (p = 0.0035). Post-radiation local (± distant) recurrence occurred in 81.0% (17/21) of patients. Our findings reaffirm the dismal outcomes of pediatric H3 G34-mutant DHG, which exhibits radiation resistance, frequent widespread disease, and a novel mechanism of MGMT regulation. Our data support the use of frontline TMZ in pediatric patients and underscore the importance of GTR when feasible.

> **中文摘要：**
> 既往研究表明，患有H3 G34突变弥漫性半球胶质瘤（DHG）的儿童患者预后不良。然而，这种治疗抵抗性的生物学基础仍知之甚少。此外，替莫唑胺（TMZ）的有效性以及手术在儿童患者中的作用仍不明确。因此，我们对36例新诊断的儿童（≤18岁）H3 G34突变DHG患者的临床、影像和分子特征进行了多机构回顾性分析。该队列的中位年龄为14岁（范围8-18岁）。中位无进展生存期（PFS）为0.7年（95% CI 0.4-1.2年），中位总生存期（OS）为1.8年（95% CI 1.1-3.2年）。大体全切除（GTR）与改善的PFS相关（p=0.0046）。22.6%（7/31）的患者在就诊时发现浸润了三个或更多脑叶（大脑胶质瘤病）。21名患者（58.3%）接受了一线TMZ治疗，与未接受者相比，其PFS有所改善（p=0.0049）。低MGMT表达与更好的PFS（p=0.0039）和更好的OS（p<0.0001）相关。在儿童DHG中，与MGMT表达相关的是基因体/内含子CpG甲基化，而非启动子甲基化（p<0.0001）。MGMT启动子甲基化与PFS或OS无显著相关性。PDGFRA改变（n=13）与较差的OS相关（p=0.0035）。81.0%（17/21）的患者在放疗后出现局部（±远处）复发。我们的研究结果再次证实了儿童H3 G34突变DHG的预后极差，其表现出放疗抵抗、频繁的广泛播散以及一种新的MGMT调控机制。我们的数据支持在儿童患者中使用一线TMZ，并强调了在可行情况下进行GTR的重要性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过多中心回顾性分析，阐明儿童H3 G34突变弥漫性半球胶质瘤的临床、影像及分子预后因素，并评估替莫唑胺疗效与手术价值。研究发现，该肿瘤预后极差，具有放疗抵抗和广泛播散倾向；低MGMT表达与更好的生存相关，但其调控机制独特，由基因体/内含子甲基化而非启动子甲基化介导。研究创新性地揭示了该亚型独特的MGMT调控模式，并支持一线使用替莫唑胺和最大程度安全切除，但作为回顾性研究，其结论有待前瞻性验证，且样本量有限可能影响部分亚组分析的统计效力。

---

## 82. 靶向APE1的氧化还原功能可逆转食管腺癌中SOX9介导的化疗耐药。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770176)
**期刊：** Gastroenterology
**PMID：** 41770176
**DOI：** 10.1053/j.gastro.2025.12.019

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Targeting APE1-Redox Function Reverses SOX9-mediated Chemoresistance in Esophageal Adenocarcinoma.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND & AIMS: Gastroesophageal reflux disease is the leading risk factor for esophageal adenocarcinoma (EAC), a malignancy that exhibits marked resistance to chemotherapy and results in poor clinical outcomes. This study aims to define and overcome the mechanisms underlying chemoresistance in EAC to enable the development of novel therapeutic strategies.
> 
> METHODS: The study included analysis of RNA sequencing and public datasets. Experimental models consisted of 3-dimensional organotypic cultures, tumorospheres, patient-derived organoids, and de-identified tissue microarrays. In vivo experiments utilized the pL2-IL1β, Krt7CreER;R26rtTA;otet-CDX2, and patient-derived xenograft mouse models.
> 
> RESULTS: RNA sequencing revealed a significant enrichment of the SRY-Box Transcription Factor 9 (SOX9) molecular signature in patients with EAC. We identified an apurinic/apyrimidinic endonuclease (APE1)-dependent mechanism that activates SOX9 signaling on exposure to acidic bile salts, mimicking reflux conditions. Genetic knockdown or pharmacological inhibition of APE1's redox activity suppressed SOX9 activation under both reflux-mimicking conditions and oxaliplatin treatment. The redox function of APE1 was required to stabilize the SOX9 protein. Immunostaining demonstrated co-overexpression of APE1 and SOX9 in mouse and human EAC lesions, accompanied by Aldehyde Dehydrogenase 1 Family Member A1 expression, a SOX9 transcriptional target implicated in chemotherapeutic resistance. Clinically, patients with high SOX9 signature expression had significantly worse relapse-free survival. Moreover, in vivo treatment with the APE1-redox-specific inhibitor APX2009 enhanced the response of patient-derived xenograft tumors to oxaliplatin by downregulating SOX9.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: Activation of SOX9 through the APE1-redox function is a key driver of EAC chemoresistance. Targeting APE1's redox activity offers a promising therapeutic strategy to overcome resistance by inhibiting the otherwise "undruggable" SOX9 transcription network.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景与目的：胃食管反流病是食管腺癌（EAC）的主要风险因素，该恶性肿瘤表现出显著的化疗耐药性，导致临床预后不良。本研究旨在阐明并克服EAC化疗耐药的潜在机制，以推动新型治疗策略的开发。
> 
> 方法：本研究包括对RNA测序和公共数据集的分析。实验模型包括三维器官型培养物、肿瘤球、患者来源的类器官以及去标识化的组织微阵列。体内实验使用了pL2-IL1β、Krt7CreER;R26rtTA;otet-CDX2以及患者来源的异种移植小鼠模型。
> 
> 结果：RNA测序显示，EAC患者中SRY盒转录因子9（SOX9）分子特征显著富集。我们发现了一种依赖于脱嘌呤/脱嘧啶核酸内切酶（APE1）的机制，该机制在暴露于模拟反流条件的酸性胆汁酸盐时激活SOX9信号通路。通过基因敲低或药物抑制APE1的氧化还原活性，可在模拟反流条件和奥沙利铂治疗下均抑制SOX9的激活。APE1的氧化还原功能是稳定SOX9蛋白所必需的。免疫染色显示，在小鼠和人类EAC病变中，APE1和SOX9存在共过表达，并伴有醛脱氢酶1家族成员A1的表达，后者是SOX9的转录靶点，与化疗耐药相关。临床上，SOX9特征高表达的患者无复发生存期显著更差。此外，在体内使用APE1氧化还原特异性抑制剂APX2009治疗，通过下调SOX9增强了患者来源的异种移植肿瘤对奥沙利铂的反应。
> 
> 结论：通过APE1的氧化还原功能激活SOX9是EAC化疗耐药的关键驱动因素。靶向APE1的氧化还原活性提供了一种有前景的治疗策略，通过抑制原本“不可成药”的SOX9转录网络来克服耐药性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明并克服食管腺癌（EAC）化疗耐药的机制。研究通过整合RNA测序、多维度体外模型（如类器官）和多种体内模型（包括基因工程鼠和PDX模型），系统性地揭示了在模拟反流条件下，APE1通过其氧化还原功能稳定并激活转录因子SOX9，进而驱动化疗耐药的关键通路。其创新性在于，不仅将临床风险因素（反流）与分子机制（APE1-SOX9轴）直接关联，还提出了靶向“不可成药”转录因子SOX9上游调控蛋白APE1的精准治疗策略，并提供了特异性抑制剂APX2009的临床前疗效证据。然而，研究结论主要基于临床前模型，其向临床转化的有效性和安全性仍需进一步验证。

---

## 83. PET/CT引导下替雷利珠单抗联合化疗/放化疗新辅助治疗可切除食管鳞状细胞癌：RATIONALE-213研究的最终分析。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770095)
**期刊：** Clinical cancer research : an official journal of the American Association for Cancer Research
**PMID：** 41770095
**DOI：** 10.1158/1078-0432.CCR-25-2367

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** PET/CT-Guided Neoadjuvant Tislelizumab Plus Chemotherapy/Chemoradiotherapy for Resectable Esophageal Squamous Cell Carcinoma: RATIONALE-213 Final Analysis.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: To assess positron emission tomography/computed tomography (PET/CT)-guided neoadjuvant treatment with tislelizumab plus chemotherapy/chemoradiotherapy in patients with resectable esophageal squamous cell carcinoma (ESCC). PATIENTS AND METHODS: RATIONALE-213, a multicenter, open-label, two-cohort phase II study, enrolled 70 patients with resectable ESCC. After one induction chemotherapy cycle, patients were categorized as PET responders (PET maximum standardized uptake value decrease ≥35%) or PET nonresponders (<35%). Subsequently, all patients received three cycles of tislelizumab 200 mg intravenously. In addition, PET responders received chemotherapy and PET nonresponders received chemoradiotherapy as neoadjuvant treatment followed by surgery. The primary endpoint was pathological complete response (pCR) rate. RESULTS: As of October 25, 2024 (median follow-up 25.5 months), pCR rates were 30.0% (95% CI, 11.9-54.3) in PET responders and 34.4% (95% CI, 18.6-53.2) in PET nonresponders. Higher pCR rates associated with higher baseline programmed cell death ligand 1 (PD-L1) Tumor Area Positivity (TAP) scores in both cohorts. One-year disease-free survival rates were 79.0% and 74.2%, and event-free survival rates were 87.1% and 67.8% respectively. Any-grade and grade ≥3 treatment-related adverse events (TRAEs) occurred in 93.3% and 50.0% of PET responders and 97.5% and 82.5% of PET nonresponders, with no new safety signals. The most common grade ≥3 TRAE was decreased neutrophil count (36.7% and 70.0%, respectively). CONCLUSIONS: Tislelizumab with chemotherapy/chemoradiotherapy as neoadjuvant treatment for resectable ESCC yielded promising pCR rates and favorable survival outcomes with a tolerable safety profile in both PET-/CT-guided responders and PET nonresponders.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：评估PET/CT引导下替雷利珠单抗联合化疗/放化疗新辅助治疗在可切除食管鳞状细胞癌（ESCC）患者中的应用。患者与方法：RATIONALE-213是一项多中心、开放标签、双队列II期研究，入组了70例可切除ESCC患者。经过一个周期的诱导化疗后，患者被分为PET应答者（PET最大标准化摄取值下降≥35%）和PET无应答者（<35%）。随后，所有患者均接受三个周期的替雷利珠单抗200 mg静脉输注。此外，PET应答者接受化疗，PET无应答者接受放化疗作为新辅助治疗，之后进行手术。主要终点是病理完全缓解（pCR）率。结果：截至2024年10月25日（中位随访25.5个月），PET应答者和PET无应答者的pCR率分别为30.0%（95% CI，11.9-54.3）和34.4%（95% CI，18.6-53.2）。在两个队列中，较高的pCR率与较高的基线程序性细胞死亡配体1（PD-L1）肿瘤区域阳性（TAP）评分相关。一年无病生存率分别为79.0%和74.2%，无事件生存率分别为87.1%和67.8%。PET应答者中任何级别和≥3级治疗相关不良事件（TRAEs）的发生率分别为93.3%和50.0%，PET无应答者中分别为97.5%和82.5%，未发现新的安全信号。最常见的≥3级TRAE是中性粒细胞计数下降（分别为36.7%和70.0%）。结论：对于可切除ESCC，无论PET/CT引导下的应答者还是无应答者，替雷利珠单抗联合化疗/放化疗作为新辅助治疗均获得了有前景的pCR率和良好的生存结局，且安全性可耐受。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究创新性地采用PET/CT早期代谢反应（SUVmax下降≥35%）作为生物标志物，对可切除食管鳞癌患者进行新辅助治疗分层，即应答者继续化疗联合免疫，无应答者则升级为放化疗联合免疫。最终分析显示，这种基于PET/CT的适应性策略在两组中均取得了有前景的病理完全缓解率（约30%-34%）和生存获益，且安全性可控。其核心价值在于探索了精准、动态的个体化新辅助治疗模式，但作为II期研究，样本量有限，且PET应答定义（35%阈值）的普适性仍需更大规模研究验证。

---

## 84. Belantamab Mafodotin联合硼替佐米与地塞米松在复发/难治性多发性骨髓瘤患者中的疗效与安全性：DREAMM-6研究B组试验

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770089)
**期刊：** Clinical cancer research : an official journal of the American Association for Cancer Research
**PMID：** 41770089
**DOI：** 10.1158/1078-0432.CCR-25-3216

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Efficacy and Safety of Belantamab Mafodotin with Bortezomib Plus Dexamethasone in Patients with Relapsed/Refractory Multiple Myeloma: the DREAMM-6 Arm B Trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: The Phase 1/2 DREAMM-6 Arm B study (NCT03544281) explored belantamab mafodotin combined with bortezomib/dexamethasone (BVd) in relapsed/ refractory multiple myeloma (RRMM). PATIENTS AND METHODS: Adults with RRMM were enrolled sequentially in two belantamab mafodotin (intravenous) dose-escalation (DE) cohorts (2.5 then 3.4 mg/kg every 3 weeks [Q3W]). Additional patients enrolled sequentially to eight dose-expansion cohorts: 1.9, 2.5, or 3.4 mg/kg Q3W; 2.5 or 3.4 mg/kg Q3W split dose (Days 1 and 8); 1.9 or 2.5 mg/kg Q6W; or 2.5 mg/kg in cycle 1 stepped down to 1.9 mg/kg Q6W thereafter. Patients received bortezomib twice weekly and dexamethasone four times weekly. Endpoints were dose-limiting toxicities (DLT; DE), adverse events (AEs), serious AEs (SAEs; DE and expansion), overall response rate (ORR; expansion), and pharmacokinetics. RESULTS: 107 patients (median 4 prior lines of therapy) received BVd (n=12-18/ cohort). Median follow-up was 15.2-25.4 months. No DLTs occurred during DE. The most common Grade 3/4 AE was keratopathy (53%). Protocol-defined ocular events (change in best corrected visual acuity and/or corneal examination findings) were reported in 93% of patients (Grade 3/4: 77%). Twenty-eight (26%) patients experienced any study treatment-related SAEs; 3 of 7 fatal SAEs had a treatment-related primary cause. ORR was 70% (95% CI: 60.5, 78.6). Higher initial exposures had higher probabilities of response and ocular events; lower exposures resulted in fewer deep responses, with small differences in ocular events. CONCLUSION: BVd demonstrated manageable safety and clinical activity across all dosing cohorts in heavily pretreated RRMM, supporting the 2.5 mg/kg Q3W dose.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的： 1/2期DREAMM-6研究B组（NCT03544281）探索了belantamab mafodotin联合硼替佐米/地塞米松（BVd）在复发/难治性多发性骨髓瘤（RRMM）中的应用。患者与方法： RRMM成人患者依次入组两个belantamab mafodotin（静脉注射）剂量递增（DE）队列（先2.5 mg/kg，后3.4 mg/kg，每3周一次[Q3W]）。额外患者依次入组八个剂量扩展队列：1.9、2.5或3.4 mg/kg Q3W；2.5或3.4 mg/kg Q3W分次给药（第1天和第8天）；1.9或2.5 mg/kg Q6W；或第1周期2.5 mg/kg，之后降至1.9 mg/kg Q6W。患者接受硼替佐米每周两次和地塞米松每周四次给药。终点包括剂量限制性毒性（DLT；DE）、不良事件（AEs）、严重不良事件（SAEs；DE和扩展期）、总体缓解率（ORR；扩展期）和药代动力学。结果： 107名患者（既往中位治疗线数为4）接受了BVd治疗（每队列n=12-18）。中位随访时间为15.2-25.4个月。DE期间未发生DLT。最常见的3/4级AE是角膜病变（53%）。93%的患者报告了方案定义的眼部事件（最佳矫正视力变化和/或角膜检查结果）（3/4级：77%）。28名（26%）患者经历了任何与研究治疗相关的SAEs；7例致命性SAEs中有3例的主要原因为治疗相关。ORR为70%（95% CI：60.5, 78.6）。较高的初始暴露量具有较高的缓解概率和眼部事件发生率；较低的暴露量导致深度缓解减少，而眼部事件发生率差异较小。结论： 在经重度预处理的RRMM患者中，BVd在所有剂量队列中均显示出可控的安全性和临床活性，支持2.5 mg/kg Q3W的剂量。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在评估新型抗体药物偶联物Belantamab Mafodotin联合标准方案（硼替佐米+地塞米松）在复发/难治性多发性骨髓瘤中的安全性与疗效。研究创新性地设计了复杂的多队列剂量探索方案，包括不同剂量、给药间隔和分次给药策略，以精细评估暴露-效应关系。核心发现是联合方案在重度预处理患者中显示出高达70%的总体缓解率，但眼部毒性（尤其是角膜病变）发生率极高（93%），且与药物暴露量相关。研究的主要局限性在于其1/2期设计，样本量有限且队列分散，需要更大规模的随机对照试验来确认疗效与安全性的平衡，并优化眼部毒性的管理策略。

## 85. NSD1介导的PPARγ甲基化通过增强PTEN活性抑制子宫内膜癌的糖酵解和肿瘤进展。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41770031)
**期刊：** Cancer research
**PMID：** 41770031
**DOI：** 10.1158/0008-5472.CAN-25-3289

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** NSD1-Mediated PPARγ Methylation Enhances PTEN Activity to Suppress Glycolysis and Tumor Progression in Endometrial Cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Metabolic reprogramming is a defining feature of endometrial cancer (EC). The upstream molecular mechanisms driving altered metabolism in EC represent potential therapeutic targets. Here, we identified the lysine methyltransferase NSD1-frequently mutated in EC-as a key epigenetic regulator of tumor metabolism. NSD1 directly monomethylated PPARγ at lysine 98 (K98), which enhanced the nuclear localization of PPARγ and promoted transcriptional activation of the tumor suppressor gene PTEN. The resulting elevated PTEN levels led to reduced glycolytic metabolism, cellular proliferation, and invasive potential in EC cells. Loss-of-function mutations in NSD1 abolished PPARγ K98 methylation, resulting in its cytoplasmic retention and impaired PTEN transcription. The consequent depletion of PTEN amplified glycolysis and drove tumor progression. Remarkably, restoration of PTEN expression or pharmacological inhibition of AKT effectively reversed the heightened glycolytic activity and malignant phenotype associated with NSD1 deficiency. Together, these findings reveal a critical epigenetic-metabolic axis in EC, wherein NSD1-mediated methylation of PPARγ at K98 orchestrates tumor-suppressive metabolic control via PTEN. These insights not only elucidate a regulatory pathway in EC pathogenesis but also highlight potential therapeutic targets for intervention in metabolically driven tumors.

> **中文摘要：**
> 代谢重编程是子宫内膜癌的一个决定性特征。驱动子宫内膜癌代谢改变的上游分子机制是潜在的治疗靶点。在此，我们鉴定出在子宫内膜癌中频繁突变的赖氨酸甲基转移酶NSD1是肿瘤代谢的关键表观遗传调控因子。NSD1直接在赖氨酸98位点（K98）单甲基化PPARγ，这增强了PPARγ的核定位并促进了抑癌基因PTEN的转录激活。由此升高的PTEN水平导致子宫内膜癌细胞中糖酵解代谢、细胞增殖和侵袭潜能降低。NSD1的功能丧失性突变消除了PPARγ K98的甲基化，导致其滞留在细胞质中并损害PTEN转录。随之而来的PTEN耗竭放大了糖酵解并驱动了肿瘤进展。值得注意的是，恢复PTEN表达或药理学抑制AKT能有效逆转与NSD1缺陷相关的糖酵解活性增强和恶性表型。总之，这些发现揭示了子宫内膜癌中一个关键的表观遗传-代谢轴，其中NSD1介导的PPARγ K98甲基化通过PTEN协调了肿瘤抑制性代谢控制。这些见解不仅阐明了子宫内膜癌发病机制中的一条调控通路，也突出了干预代谢驱动型肿瘤的潜在治疗靶点。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索子宫内膜癌代谢重编程的上游表观遗传调控机制。通过分子生物学方法，研究者发现甲基转移酶NSD1通过单甲基化修饰PPARγ的K98位点，增强其核定位并激活PTEN转录，从而抑制糖酵解和肿瘤进展。其创新性在于揭示了一条连接表观遗传修饰、代谢调控和经典抑癌通路（PTEN/AKT）的新轴，为靶向代谢的干预提供了新思路。局限性在于研究主要基于细胞模型，其临床转化价值和在体内微环境中的调控网络有待进一步验证。

---

## 86. 用于癌症免疫治疗的高亲和力Siglec配体一步法糖工程化改造NK细胞。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41769870)
**期刊：** Advanced science (Weinheim, Baden-Wurttemberg, Germany)
**PMID：** 41769870
**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202522474

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** One-Step Glycoengineering of NK Cells With High-Affinity Siglec Ligands for Cancer Immunotherapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> Siglecs, a family of sialic acid (Sia)-binding immunomodulatory receptors selectively expressed on immune cells, are promising immunotherapeutic targets. While synthetic Sia derivatives can manipulate the Sia-Siglec axis with high affinity, their therapeutic application has been hampered by the poor substrate tolerance of wild-type CMP-sialic acid synthase (CSS) for sterically demanding analogs. Here, we report a structure-guided engineering strategy to evolve Neisseria meningitidis CMP-Sia synthetase (NmCSS) for enhanced activity with bulky substrates. Coupling this optimized NmCSS variant with a sialyltransferase enabled a scalable "one-pot two-enzyme" (OPTE) synthesis of diverse sialoside analogs. Screening this library on glycan microarrays revealed novel high-affinity ligands with selective Siglec binding profiles. Leveraging the OPTE system, we achieved single-step glycoengineering of natural killer (NK)-92MI cells with tailored Siglec-2 or Siglec-3 ligands, which exhibited potent cytotoxicity against B-cell lymphoma (Siglec-2) and acute myeloid leukemia (Siglec-3) models. These engineered NK cells displayed significantly enhanced tumor killing capacity, mediated by enhanced granzyme release and cytokine production while maintaining excellent cell viability. This modular platform addresses critical limitations in enzymatic synthesis of modified sialosides and their efficient display on therapeutic cells. Our work establishes a versatile and practical platform for developing next-generation immunotherapies that precisely target the Sia-Siglec axis with improved specificity and functionality.

> **中文摘要：**
> Siglecs是一类选择性表达于免疫细胞上的唾液酸结合免疫调节受体家族，是有前景的免疫治疗靶点。尽管合成的唾液酸衍生物能以高亲和力调控Sia-Siglec轴，但其治疗应用一直受到野生型CMP-唾液酸合酶对空间位阻大的类似物底物耐受性差的阻碍。在此，我们报告了一种结构引导的工程策略，用于改造脑膜炎奈瑟菌CMP-Sia合成酶，以增强其对大体积底物的活性。将此优化的NmCSS变体与唾液酸转移酶偶联，实现了可规模化的“一锅双酶”合成多种唾液酸苷类似物。在糖芯片上筛选该文库，发现了具有选择性Siglec结合谱的新型高亲和力配体。利用OPTE系统，我们实现了对自然杀伤细胞NK-92MI的单步糖工程化改造，为其配备了定制的Siglec-2或Siglec-3配体，这些细胞在B细胞淋巴瘤和急性髓系白血病模型中分别表现出强大的细胞毒性。这些工程化的NK细胞显示出显著增强的肿瘤杀伤能力，其机制是增强了颗粒酶释放和细胞因子产生，同时保持了优异的细胞活力。这一模块化平台解决了修饰唾液酸苷的酶法合成及其在治疗细胞上高效展示的关键限制。我们的工作为开发下一代免疫疗法建立了一个通用且实用的平台，该平台能以更高的特异性和功能性精确靶向Sia-Siglec轴。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决高亲和力唾液酸-Siglec轴调节剂在免疫治疗中应用的合成瓶颈。核心创新在于通过结构引导的酶工程策略，改造关键合成酶，构建了可规模化的“一锅双酶”平台，高效合成多样化唾液酸苷类似物文库。研究发现并验证了选择性Siglec配体，并成功将其一步展示于NK细胞表面，显著增强了其对特定血液肿瘤模型的杀伤效力。该工作将合成生物学与细胞工程紧密结合，为开发基于Siglec靶向的下一代细胞免疫疗法提供了强有力的通用技术平台，但研究目前限于体外和模型验证，其体内安全性与长期疗效有待进一步评估。

---

## 87. 更正：表达HPV16的肿瘤释放多种IL1配体以协调系统性免疫抑制，破坏此机制可使治疗性疫苗生效。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41766435)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41766435
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-26-0046

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Correction: HPV16-Expressing Tumors Release Multiple IL1 Ligands to Orchestrate Systemic Immunosuppression Whose Disruption Enables Efficacy of a Therapeutic Vaccine.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无摘要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

## 90. 转录组学亚型与从不吸烟肺腺癌患者的临床结局相关。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41766432)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41766432
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-2137

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Transcriptomic Subtypes Are Associated with Clinical Outcomes for Patients with Lung Adenocarcinoma Who Have Never Smoked.

> **英文摘要：**
> Lung adenocarcinoma arising in individuals who have never smoked is understudied, represents a substantial global health burden, and is genomically distinct from smoking-associated disease. Zhao and colleagues have identified transcriptomic subtypes with prognostic value, including in stage I disease, supporting phenotypic state as an important determinant of outcome for lung adenocarcinoma in individuals who have never smoked. See related article by Zhao et al., p. 460.

> **中文摘要：**
> 发生于从不吸烟个体的肺腺癌研究不足，构成了巨大的全球健康负担，并且在基因组学上与吸烟相关疾病不同。Zhao及其同事鉴定出了具有预后价值的转录组学亚型，包括在I期疾病中，这支持了表型状态是影响从不吸烟个体肺腺癌结局的重要决定因素。参见Zhao等人的相关文章，第460页。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索从不吸烟肺腺癌患者的分子特征与临床结局的关系。研究团队通过对患者样本进行转录组分析，成功鉴定出具有独立预后价值的分子亚型。核心发现是，这些转录组亚型，甚至在早期（I期）患者中，也能有效预测临床结局，强调了肿瘤的分子表型状态是影响此类患者预后的关键因素。该研究的创新性在于为研究不足的从不吸烟肺腺癌提供了新的分子分型框架，但局限性在于其发现主要基于回顾性分析，需在前瞻性队列和不同种族人群中进一步验证。

## 91. 终末期肾病中炎症驱动的区域癌化。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41766431)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41766431
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-2276

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Inflammation-Driven Field Cancerization in End-Stage Kidney Disease.

> **英文摘要：**
> In this issue, Takahashi, Tanaka, and colleagues provide a comprehensive genomic, transcriptomic, and spatial analysis of renal cell carcinomas (RCC) associated with end-stage renal disease. They demonstrate that the clonal expansion of a subset of proximal tubule cells, supported by an inflammatory microenvironment, gives rise to the cysts of acquired cystic kidney disease as well as to acquired cystic disease-associated RCC. See related article by Takahashi et al., p. 478.

> **中文摘要：**
> 在本期中，Takahashi、Tanaka及其同事对与终末期肾病相关的肾细胞癌（RCC）进行了全面的基因组学、转录组学和空间分析。他们证明，在炎症微环境的支持下，一部分近端肾小管细胞的克隆性扩增，导致了获得性囊性肾病囊肿以及获得性囊性病相关肾细胞癌的发生。参见Takahashi等人的相关文章，第478页。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在通过多组学及空间分析，揭示终末期肾病背景下肾细胞癌的发生机制。作者发现，炎症微环境驱动的近端肾小管细胞克隆扩增是获得性囊性肾病及其相关肾癌的共同起源，这为理解“区域癌化”提供了直接证据。该研究的创新性在于整合了基因组、转录组和空间信息，系统阐述了从炎症到囊肿再到癌变的连续病理过程。然而，摘要未提及研究队列的具体规模或验证策略，其结论的普适性有待进一步确认。

## 92. 早期驱动，晚期旁观：DNMT3A R882突变在人类AML中的阶段特异性作用被揭示

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41766430)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41766430
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-2277

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Early Driver, Late Bystander: Stage-Specific Roles of DNMT3A R882 Mutations Unveiled in Human AML.

> **英文摘要：**
> In this issue, Köhnke, Karigane, and colleagues applied allele-specific CRISPR/Cas9 correction in human acute myeloid leukemia samples to dissect the stage-specific functions of DNA methyltransferase 3A (DNMT3A) arginine 882 (R882) mutations. They demonstrate that DNMT3A R882 mutations are required to sustain self-renewal and inflammatory programs in preleukemic cells but become largely dispensable once leukemia is established, while still influencing leukemia stem cell frequency, thereby providing a strong preclinical rationale to reconsider the therapeutic window for targeting DNMT3A-mutant clones early in leukemogenesis. See related article by Köhnke et al., p. 592.

> **中文摘要：**
> 在本期中，Köhnke、Karigane及其同事在人急性髓系白血病样本中应用等位基因特异性CRISPR/Cas9校正技术，以剖析DNA甲基转移酶3A（DNMT3A）精氨酸882（R882）突变的阶段特异性功能。他们证明，DNMT3A R882突变对于维持白血病前细胞中的自我更新和炎症程序是必需的，但一旦白血病形成，这些突变在很大程度上变得可有可无，尽管仍会影响白血病干细胞频率，从而为重新考虑在白血病发生早期靶向DNMT3A突变克隆的治疗窗口期提供了强有力的临床前依据。参见Köhnke等人的相关文章，第592页。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过等位基因特异性CRISPR/Cas9校正技术，精准解析了DNMT3A R882突变在AML发生发展中的动态角色。核心发现是，该突变在白血病前阶段是维持恶性潜能的关键驱动因子，而在白血病形成后则转变为“旁观者”，但仍影响干细胞库大小。这一发现具有重要的创新性，它挑战了传统上持续靶向该突变的概念，并提出了在疾病早期进行干预的精准治疗新策略。局限性在于，研究主要基于临床前模型，其结论向临床转化的具体时机和方案仍需进一步探索。

## 94. 多胺代谢作为超生理雄激素治疗前列腺癌的代谢脆弱性。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41766411)
**期刊：** Cancer research
**PMID：** 41766411
**DOI：** 10.1158/0008-5472.CAN-25-4807

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Polyamine Metabolism as a Metabolic Vulnerability in Prostate Cancer Treated with Supraphysiological Androgens.

> **英文摘要：**
> Prostate cancer progression is predominantly driven by androgen receptor (AR) signaling, and despite initial benefits of androgen deprivation therapy (ADT), most patients eventually develop lethal castration-resistant disease. Cyclic administration of supraphysiologic androgen (SPA) with ADT paradoxically suppresses tumor growth; however, responses are heterogeneous, and the mechanisms underlying the antitumor effects of SPA remain incompletely understood. In this issue of Cancer Research, Kumar and colleagues demonstrate that SPA induces a distinct metabolic response, characterized by AR-dependent induction of polyamine biosynthesis via ODC1 and AMD1. This metabolic rewiring elevates polyamine synthesis while concurrently depleting the methyl donor S-adenosylmethionine (SAM). Although increased polyamine metabolism by SPA may promote adaptive resistance, genetic or pharmacologic inhibition of ODC1 using difluoromethylornithine (DFMO) enhances SPA-induced growth suppression by disrupting protective polyamine pools and further exacerbating SAM depletion, revealing a metabolic vulnerability in SPA-treated prostate cancer cells. Supporting these findings, a clinical trial combining DFMO with bipolar androgen therapy (BAT) demonstrated reduced circulating polyamines in patients, confirming polyamine pathway suppression in patients with different genomic features. Together, this研究揭示了雄激素信号、多胺代谢和治疗反应之间的机制联系，为靶向代谢依赖性以提高SPA疗效提供了理论依据。 See related article by Kumar et al., p. 1148.

> **中文摘要：**
> 前列腺癌进展主要由雄激素受体（AR）信号驱动，尽管雄激素剥夺疗法（ADT）初期有效，但大多数患者最终会发展为致命的去势抵抗性疾病。ADT联合周期性超生理雄激素（SPA）给药能矛盾性地抑制肿瘤生长；然而，治疗反应存在异质性，且SPA抗肿瘤作用的机制尚不完全清楚。在本期《癌症研究》中，Kumar及其同事证明，SPA诱导了一种独特的代谢反应，其特征是通过ODC1和AMD1进行AR依赖性诱导多胺生物合成。这种代谢重编程在提升多胺合成的同时，也耗竭了甲基供体S-腺苷甲硫氨酸（SAM）。尽管SPA增加的多胺代谢可能促进适应性抵抗，但使用二氟甲基鸟氨酸（DFMO）对ODC1进行遗传或药理学抑制，可通过破坏保护性多胺池并进一步加剧SAM耗竭，从而增强SPA诱导的生长抑制，揭示了SPA治疗的前列腺癌细胞中的代谢脆弱性。支持这些发现的是，一项将DFMO与双极雄激素疗法（BAT）相结合的临床试验显示患者循环多胺水平降低，证实了在不同基因组特征的患者中多胺通路受到抑制。总之，这项研究揭示了雄激素信号、多胺代谢和治疗反应之间的机制联系，为靶向代谢依赖性以提高SPA疗效提供了理论依据。参见Kumar等人的相关文章，第1148页。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明超生理雄激素（SPA）治疗前列腺癌的抗肿瘤机制，并探索其代谢脆弱性。研究者通过分子生物学方法揭示了SPA通过AR依赖途径诱导多胺合成酶ODC1/AMD1，导致多胺合成增加与甲基供体SAM耗竭这一独特的代谢重编程。核心发现是，抑制多胺合成关键酶ODC1（使用DFMO）能协同增强SPA的疗效，揭示了“多胺代谢”可作为联合治疗的靶点，这一发现通过临床试验初步验证。研究的创新性在于将雄激素信号、代谢重编程与治疗反应机制性关联，为改善SPA疗法提供了新策略；局限性在于临床数据尚属初步，其长期疗效、耐药机制及在更广泛患者群体中的适用性仍需进一步研究。

---

## 97. 追随“DOTs”：Vδ1+ γδ T细胞作为癌症免疫治疗的效应细胞

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41670625)
**期刊：** The Journal of experimental medicine
**PMID：** 41670625
**DOI：** 10.1084/jem.20252289

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Follow the "DOTs": Vδ1+ γδ T cells as effectors of cancer immunotherapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> Cancer immunotherapy has mostly relied on conventional T cells to achieve success in a limited set of tumor types. A promising avenue to expand the repertoire of cancers effectively treated through immune intervention is to mobilize other anti-tumor effectors, such as γδ T cells. Among these, the Vδ1+ subset commonly predominates within peripheral tissues and within tumors, typically associating with good prognosis. In this Found in Translation, we discuss how to leverage the biological properties of Vδ1+ γδ T cells for cancer immunotherapy, with special focus on the delta one T (DOT) cell approach.

> **中文摘要：**
> 癌症免疫治疗主要依赖常规T细胞，仅在有限的肿瘤类型中取得成功。通过免疫干预有效治疗更多癌症的一个有前景的途径是动员其他抗肿瘤效应细胞，例如γδ T细胞。其中，Vδ1+亚群通常在周围组织和肿瘤内占主导地位，并且通常与良好的预后相关。在这篇“转化发现”文章中，我们讨论了如何利用Vδ1+ γδ T细胞的生物学特性进行癌症免疫治疗，特别聚焦于delta one T（DOT）细胞疗法。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文旨在探讨将Vδ1+ γδ T细胞，特别是其DOT细胞疗法，作为癌症免疫治疗新策略的潜力。其核心方法是利用该细胞亚群在肿瘤组织中富集且与良好预后相关的生物学特性，以突破当前依赖常规T细胞的疗法在肿瘤类型上的局限。创新性在于将研究焦点从主流αβ T细胞转向组织驻留型γδ T细胞，为实体瘤治疗提供了新思路。局限性在于，作为一篇观点性评述，它主要基于现有观察提出概念框架，其具体临床转化路径、疗效及潜在毒性仍需后续实验和临床试验数据来验证。

## 103. 随机试验揭示免疫治疗成功与给药时间相关。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41632563)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41632563
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-NW2026-0010

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Randomized Trial Links Time of Day to Immunotherapy Success.

> **英文摘要：**
> Morning administration of checkpoint inhibitors significantly extended survival in patients with advanced non-small cell lung cancer, in the first randomized trial of immunotherapy timing. The results provide prospective support for aligning treatment with circadian biology as a simple way to improve cancer outcomes.

> **中文摘要：**
> 在首个关于免疫治疗时机的随机试验中，早晨给予检查点抑制剂显著延长了晚期非小细胞肺癌患者的生存期。该结果为将治疗与昼夜节律生物学同步作为一种改善癌症结局的简单方法提供了前瞻性支持。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究首次通过随机对照试验，前瞻性地探讨了免疫检查点抑制剂给药时间对晚期非小细胞肺癌患者生存结局的影响。核心发现是早晨给药能显著延长患者生存期，这为“时间疗法”在肿瘤免疫治疗中的应用提供了高等级循证依据。其创新性在于将基础的昼夜节律生物学原理直接转化为可操作的临床干预策略，方法简单且潜在获益显著。然而，摘要未提及具体药物、样本量及次要终点，其结论的普适性（如对其他癌种或不同免疫疗法的适用性）和长期安全性仍需更大规模的研究验证。

---

## 104. 个性化癌症疫苗在5年随访中显示出持久获益。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41632561)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41632561
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-NW2026-0009

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Personalized Cancer Vaccine Shows Durable Benefit at 5 Years.

> **英文摘要：**
> Five-year data from the phase IIb KEYNOTE-942 study show that the mRNA-based neoantigen vaccine intismeran autogene continues to reduce the risk of melanoma recurrence or death by roughly 49% when combined with pembrolizumab. This durability strengthens confidence in the personalized vaccine strategy, but a larger phase III trial will provide the decisive findings.

> **中文摘要：**
> 来自IIb期KEYNOTE-942研究的五年数据显示，基于mRNA的新抗原疫苗intismeran autogene与帕博利珠单抗联合使用时，持续将黑色素瘤复发或死亡的风险降低约49%。这种持久性增强了对个性化疫苗策略的信心，但更大规模的III期试验将提供决定性的发现。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在评估mRNA新抗原疫苗联合免疫检查点抑制剂治疗黑色素瘤的长期疗效。核心方法是利用IIb期临床试验（KEYNOTE-942）的五年随访数据进行分析。研究发现，该联合治疗方案能将复发或死亡风险持续降低约49%，证明了其长期获益的潜力。其创新性在于展示了基于mRNA的个性化疫苗策略的持久临床价值，但主要局限性在于目前数据仍来自IIb期研究，其最终结论有待更大规模的III期试验验证。

**PMID：** 41603817
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-NW2026-0008

> **英文摘要：**
> An AI system powered by structured oncology data matched oncologists' treatment choices in more than 90% of real clinical queries, besting a standard large language model. By focusing on a narrowly defined task-genomics-guided therapy selection-the platform demonstrates a practical pathway for deploying reliable AI tools in precision oncology.

> **中文摘要：**

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索人工智能在精准肿瘤学临床决策支持中的实际应用。其核心方法是通过结构化肿瘤学数据驱动AI系统，专注于基因组学指导的疗法选择这一具体任务。研究发现，该系统在超过90%的真实临床场景中与肿瘤学家的治疗决策一致，且性能优于通用大语言模型。其创新性在于通过限定任务范围，为AI在临床的可靠部署提供了可行范例；局限性在于其应用场景相对狭窄，结论的普适性有待在更广泛、更复杂的临床环境中进一步验证。

**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-NW2026-0007

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Base Editing Might Be Key to CAR T-cell Therapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> Researchers used a unique base-editing strategy to engineer chimeric-antigen receptor (CAR) T cells that engraft in the host and remain invisible to remaining antibody drugs. Of the 11 patients with T-cell acute lymphoblastic leukemia who received these BE-CAR7 T cells, all had complete morphogenic remission after 28 days, 82% underwent stem-cell transplantation, and 64% remain in remission 3 to 36 months after treatment.

> **中文摘要：**
> 研究人员采用了一种独特的碱基编辑策略，对嵌合抗原受体（CAR）T细胞进行改造，使其能在宿主体内定植，并对残留的抗体药物保持“隐形”。在接受这些BE-CAR7 T细胞治疗的11名T细胞急性淋巴细胞白血病患者中，所有人在28天后均达到完全形态学缓解，82%的患者接受了干细胞移植，64%的患者在治疗后3至36个月内仍保持缓解状态。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索利用碱基编辑技术改造CAR-T细胞，以克服现有疗法中抗体药物清除CAR-T细胞的局限性。核心方法是采用独特的碱基编辑策略，构建了能够定植宿主并对残留抗体药物“隐形”的BE-CAR7 T细胞。初步临床发现令人鼓舞，11名T-ALL患者全部实现快速形态学缓解，且多数患者获得长期缓解，展现了该策略在提高CAR-T疗法持久性和安全性方面的潜力。然而，研究样本量较小，随访时间有限，其长期疗效、安全性及在更广泛人群中的适用性仍需更大规模研究验证。

## 115. 一种抑制血液癌症风险的遗传制动机制

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41543509)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41543509
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-NW2026-0003

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A Genetic Brake on Blood Cancer Risk.

> **英文摘要：**
> A large genetic analysis uncovered a variant that restrains clonal hematopoiesis by slowing the growth of mutated blood stem cells linked to myeloid malignancies. The mechanisms involved may offer targets for therapies aimed at preventing cancer progression.

> **中文摘要：**

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过大规模遗传分析，旨在探索影响血液癌症风险的遗传调控因素。其核心发现是一种能够抑制克隆性造血的保护性基因变异，其机制是减缓致病性突变造血干细胞的增殖。这一发现具有重要的创新性，不仅揭示了血液癌症发生的内在遗传抵抗机制，还为开发以预防癌症进展为目标的治疗策略提供了潜在的分子靶点。然而，摘要未提及该变异的具体基因或通路，也未涉及其在人群中的分布频率，这些是未来研究需要阐明的重要细节。

## 116. 多药联合方案在结直肠癌治疗中优于单药免疫疗法。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41543507)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41543507
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-NW2026-0001

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Multiagent Combo Bests Immunotherapy Alone against Colorectal Cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Compared with atezolizumab monotherapy, a combination of chemotherapy, atezolizumab, and bevacizumab led to dramatically improved progression-free survival in patients with mismatch repair-deficient /microsatellite instability-high metastatic colorectal cancer. Because these patients often experience disease progression on immunotherapy, the results suggest that the combination approach could improve how they fare.

> **中文摘要：**
> 与阿替利珠单抗单药治疗相比，化疗、阿替利珠单抗和贝伐珠单抗的联合方案显著改善了错配修复缺陷/微卫星高度不稳定转移性结直肠癌患者的无进展生存期。由于这类患者在接受免疫治疗时常常出现疾病进展，该结果表明联合疗法有望改善他们的临床结局。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索针对错配修复缺陷/微卫星高度不稳定转移性结直肠癌的更优治疗策略。研究采用化疗联合免疫检查点抑制剂（阿替利珠单抗）及抗血管生成药物（贝伐珠单抗）的多药方案，并与单药免疫治疗进行对比。核心发现是该联合方案能显著提升患者的无进展生存期，为对免疫治疗应答不佳或进展的患者提供了新的治疗方向。其创新性在于将不同作用机制的药物进行协同组合，以克服单药免疫治疗的局限性，但摘要未提及总生存期获益及安全性数据，这是评估该方案临床价值时需要进一步明确的关键信息。

## 117. GLP-1受体激动剂在降低结直肠癌风险方面优于阿司匹林。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41543505)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41543505
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-NW2026-0002

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** GLP-1s Spur Greater Reduction in Colorectal Cancer Risk than Aspirin.

> **英文摘要：**
> In a large retrospective study, those taking a glucagon-like peptide 1 (GLP-1) receptor agonist drug were 36% less likely to develop colorectal cancer than those taking aspirin. Although the benefit seen for any one person was small, thousands could potentially see a benefit given the large number of people taking GLP-1s.d.

> **中文摘要：**
> 一项大型回顾性研究显示，与服用阿司匹林的人群相比，服用胰高血糖素样肽-1（GLP-1）受体激动剂药物的人群罹患结直肠癌的风险降低了36%。尽管对任何个体而言，观察到的益处较小，但考虑到服用GLP-1类药物的人群数量庞大，可能有数千人因此获益。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在比较GLP-1受体激动剂与阿司匹林在降低结直肠癌风险方面的相对效果。研究采用大型回顾性队列设计，核心发现是GLP-1受体激动剂使用者的结直肠癌风险比阿司匹林使用者低36%。其创新性在于首次在大规模人群中直接比较了这两种广泛使用药物的癌症预防潜力，为GLP-1类药物提供了新的潜在公共卫生价值。然而，作为回顾性研究，其结论存在混杂因素干扰的可能性，且个体绝对风险降低幅度有限，需前瞻性研究进一步验证。

---

## 118. 利用双重组酶等位基因重新表达FOXO1可挽救生发中心B细胞的类别转换重组。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41474973)
**期刊：** The Journal of experimental medicine
**PMID：** 41474973
**DOI：** 10.1084/jem.20241136

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** FOXO1 re-expression with a dual-recombinase allele rescues class switching in germinal center B cells.

> **英文摘要：**
> Modeling complex (patho)physiological processes by sequential targeted mutagenesis in mice is limited by the lack of precision of cellular targeting and complex breeding strategies. We present a new Cre/DreERT2 dual-recombinase germinal center B cell (GCBC)-specific strain, with co-expression of the recombinases from a single allele. This enables highly efficient Cre-mediated FOXO1 knockout in GCBCs in vivo, followed by time-controlled, efficient Dre-mediated FOXO1 re-expression in the same cells, leading to functional rescue of GC compartmentalization and class switch recombination. The present approach can be easily adapted to other cellular contexts.

> **中文摘要：**
> 通过在小鼠中进行序贯靶向诱变来模拟复杂的（病理）生理过程，受到细胞靶向精度不足和繁育策略复杂的限制。我们提出了一种新的Cre/DreERT2双重组酶生发中心B细胞（GCBC）特异性品系，其重组酶从单个等位基因共表达。这使得能够在体内对GCBC进行高效的Cre介导的FOXO1敲除，随后在同一细胞中进行时间可控的、高效的Dre介导的FOXO1重新表达，从而实现对生发中心区室化和类别转换重组的功能性挽救。本方法可轻松适用于其他细胞环境。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在解决在活体内对特定细胞类型进行精确、时序可控的基因功能研究的难题。其核心创新在于开发了一种新型双重组酶（Cre/DreERT2）单等位基因共表达小鼠品系，实现了在生发中心B细胞中先敲除、后时序性再表达FOXO1的精准操作。研究发现，FOXO1的再表达可以挽救因敲除而受损的生发中心结构和抗体类别转换功能，直接证明了FOXO1在该过程中的关键作用。该方法学创新性强，为在复杂生理环境中进行动态基因功能分析提供了强大工具，其设计思路具有普适性，可推广至其他细胞类型的研究。

---

## 119. 图卡替尼为转移性乳腺癌患者带来无进展生存期提升。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41405216)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41405216
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-NW2025-0111

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Tucatinib Gives PFS Boost for Metastatic Breast Cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> The addition of the HER2 tyrosine kinase inhibitor tucatinib to trastuzumab and pertuzumab as first-line maintenance therapy significantly increased progression-free survival (PFS) compared to a placebo plus mAb treatment for patients with HER2-positive metastatic breast cancer. The findings position it alongside trastuzumab deruxtecan and palbociclib as agents that have demonstrated impressive PFS improvements in phase III studies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 对于HER2阳性转移性乳腺癌患者，在曲妥珠单抗和帕妥珠单抗的基础上，加入HER2酪氨酸激酶抑制剂图卡替尼作为一线维持治疗，与安慰剂加单克隆抗体治疗相比，显著提高了无进展生存期。这一发现使其与曲妥珠单抗德鲁替康和哌柏西利并列，成为在III期研究中展现出显著无进展生存期改善的药物。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在评估图卡替尼联合曲妥珠单抗和帕妥珠单抗作为一线维持治疗对HER2阳性转移性乳腺癌的疗效。核心方法是在标准双靶向治疗基础上加用图卡替尼，并与安慰剂组进行对照。主要发现是该三联方案能显著延长患者的无进展生存期，其改善幅度使其跻身于少数几个在III期试验中证实有显著PFS获益的药物行列。其创新性在于验证了在现有高效双靶向治疗基础上，通过加入小分子TKI进行强化维持治疗的策略价值，但摘要未提及总生存期数据或安全性细节，这是其局限性。

## 120. 晚期宫颈癌一线降阶梯化疗联合派安普利单抗与安罗替尼治疗的分子与免疫应答相关性研究

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41297028)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41297028
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-1315

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Molecular and Immune Correlates of Response to First-Line De-escalated Chemotherapy plus Penpulimab and Anlotinib in Advanced Cervical Cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> UNLABELLED: The standard of care for advanced cervical cancer includes chemotherapy, antiangiogenic, and/or immune checkpoint blockade regimens. Although effective, it leads to pleiotropic side effects. Deescalation chemotherapy together with immunotargeted therapies has been proven effective and less toxic in other cancers. In this study, we conducted a multicenter, single-arm, phase II study of first-line deescalated platinum-based chemotherapy plus anlotinib and penpulimab, followed by maintenance therapy solely with anlotinib and penpulimab in patients with PD-L1-positive, persistent, recurrent, or metastatic cervical cancer. Of 32 efficacy-evaluable patients, 30 (93.8%, 95% confidence interval, 79.2%-99.2%) had an investigator-confirmed objective response. Single-nucleus RNA sequencing implied enhanced chemotaxis and proliferative activity of tumor-infiltrating T cells, and activated germinal center B cells portended optimal treatment response. Patients with a high tertiary lymphoid structure-to-tumor area ratio exhibited better survival. Our findings lay the groundwork for the feasibility of first-line de-escalated chemotherapy plus anlotinib and penpulimab in patients with metastatic, persistent, or recurrent cervical cancer.
> 
> SIGNIFICANCE: We recruited 34 patients with advanced cervical cancer receiving two cycles of platinum-based chemotherapy plus anlotinib and penpulimab, followed by maintenance therapy solely with anlotinib and penpulimab, and showed safety and efficacy of this deescalation regimen. This work highlights the potential for personalized treatment strategies and feasibility of reduced-toxicity regimens.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无标签：晚期宫颈癌的标准治疗包括化疗、抗血管生成和/或免疫检查点阻断方案。虽然有效，但会导致多效性副作用。降阶梯化疗联合免疫靶向治疗已在其他癌症中被证明有效且毒性较低。在本研究中，我们进行了一项多中心、单臂、II期研究，评估PD-L1阳性、持续性、复发性或转移性宫颈癌患者一线接受降阶梯铂类化疗联合安罗替尼和派安普利单抗治疗，随后仅使用安罗替尼和派安普利单抗进行维持治疗。在32例可评估疗效的患者中，30例（93.8%，95%置信区间，79.2%-99.2%）获得了研究者确认的客观缓解。单核RNA测序提示肿瘤浸润T细胞的趋化性和增殖活性增强，而活化的生发中心B细胞预示着最佳治疗反应。三级淋巴结构与肿瘤面积比值高的患者表现出更好的生存。我们的研究结果为转移性、持续性或复发性宫颈癌患者一线采用降阶梯化疗联合安罗替尼和派安普利单抗治疗的可行性奠定了基础。
> 
> 意义：我们招募了34例晚期宫颈癌患者，接受两个周期的铂类化疗联合安罗替尼和派安普利单抗治疗，随后仅使用安罗替尼和派安普利单抗进行维持治疗，并显示了该降阶梯方案的安全性和有效性。这项工作凸显了个性化治疗策略的潜力以及降低毒性方案的可行性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探索晚期宫颈癌一线降阶梯化疗联合免疫靶向治疗（安罗替尼+派安普利单抗）的疗效与生物标志物。通过一项多中心II期临床试验，研究者证实了该方案在PD-L1阳性患者中极高的客观缓解率（93.8%）和良好的安全性。其核心创新在于利用单核RNA测序揭示了治疗应答与肿瘤微环境中T细胞功能增强、B细胞活化及三级淋巴结构富集密切相关，为降阶梯治疗策略提供了关键的免疫学依据。然而，作为单臂II期研究，其结论仍需大规模随机对照试验验证，且研究人群限定于PD-L1阳性患者，限制了结果的普适性。

---

## 121. 一种整合肿瘤微环境特征的深度学习框架可精准预测肺癌病理图像中的多种驱动基因突变。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41289566)
**期刊：** Cancer research
**PMID：** 41289566
**DOI：** 10.1158/0008-5472.CAN-25-0582

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A Deep Learning Framework Integrating Tumor Microenvironmental Features Accurately Predicts Multiple Driver Gene Mutations in Lung Cancer Pathology Images.

> **英文摘要：**
> UNLABELLED: Deep learning (DL) has the potential to enable the prediction of gene mutations directly from routine histopathology slides in lung cancer. However, existing approaches have largely been limited to mutation-level prediction and have not achieved precise identification of driver mutation subtypes nor exonic variants, constraining the translation of DL into targeted therapy. In this study, we assembled a large multicenter dataset of paired pathology images and next-generation sequencing from 2,573 patients with lung cancer from four hospitals in China. The development of NAVF-Bio, an adaptive multiview feature fusion framework based on multiple instance learning, enabled the integration of tumor microenvironment (TME) features from whole-slide images (WSI) to predict driver mutations and tumor mutational burden (TMB). Benchmarking against 11 state-of-the-art DL methods indicated that NAVF-Bio consistently outperformed existing models in predicting driver mutations (TP53, EGFR, KRAS, ALK) and TMB status, achieving clinically relevant performance in external multicenter validation. Notably, NAVF-Bio accurately predicted the mutated driver gene exons across centers, whereas interpretability analyses using WSI visualization and TME quantification further demonstrated the ability of NAVF-Bio to elucidate pathologically relevant tumor features. Finally, a multigene mutation prediction platform for lung cancer was generated to facilitate the screening of driver gene mutations. Overall, NAVF-Bio mimics the workflow of pathologists when examining slides by observing multiscale features of WSIs and TME characteristics to predict driver gene mutations in lung cancer, which could guide the selection of targeted therapies for patients.
> 
> SIGNIFICANCE: The NAVF-Bio framework accurately predicts key driver gene mutations in lung cancer from routine pathology slides, offering opportunities for the application of AI in precision oncology.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无标签：深度学习（DL）有潜力直接从肺癌常规组织病理学切片中预测基因突变。然而，现有方法大多局限于突变层面的预测，未能实现对驱动突变亚型或外显子变异的精确识别，这限制了深度学习向靶向治疗的转化。在本研究中，我们整合了一个来自中国四家医院、包含2573名肺癌患者配对病理图像和二代测序数据的大型多中心数据集。我们开发了NAVF-Bio，这是一个基于多实例学习的自适应多视图特征融合框架，能够整合来自全切片图像（WSI）的肿瘤微环境（TME）特征来预测驱动突变和肿瘤突变负荷（TMB）。与11种最先进的深度学习方法进行基准测试表明，NAVF-Bio在预测驱动突变（TP53、EGFR、KRAS、ALK）和TMB状态方面持续优于现有模型，并在外部多中心验证中达到了临床相关性能。值得注意的是，NAVF-Bio能够跨中心准确预测突变的驱动基因外显子，而利用WSI可视化和TME量化的可解释性分析进一步证明了NAVF-Bio阐明病理相关肿瘤特征的能力。最后，我们构建了一个肺癌多基因突变预测平台，以促进驱动基因突变的筛查。总之，NAVF-Bio通过观察WSI的多尺度特征和TME特征来预测肺癌驱动基因突变，模拟了病理学家阅片的工作流程，这可以指导患者的靶向治疗选择。
> 
> 意义：NAVF-Bio框架能够从常规病理切片中准确预测肺癌的关键驱动基因突变，为人工智能在精准肿瘤学中的应用提供了机遇。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在开发一个能够从常规病理图像中精准预测肺癌驱动基因突变的深度学习框架。其核心创新在于构建了名为NAVF-Bio的多视图特征融合模型，该模型不仅整合了肿瘤微环境特征，还实现了对特定驱动基因（如TP53、EGFR等）及其外显子变异的精确识别，超越了既往仅能预测突变有无的模型。研究基于大规模多中心配对数据，验证了模型在预测突变和肿瘤突变负荷方面的优越性与临床实用性，并通过可解释性分析揭示了其病理学关联。然而，该框架的性能仍需在前瞻性临床试验和更多样化的患者群体中进一步验证，以评估其在真实世界临床决策中的可靠性和普适性。

---

## 122. 营养可用性决定基于癌症代谢的非肿瘤药物的治疗反应。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41289560)
**期刊：** Cancer research
**PMID：** 41289560
**DOI：** 10.1158/0008-5472.CAN-25-1123

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Nutrient Availability Dictates Cancer Metabolism-Based Therapeutic Responses to Nononcology Drugs.

> **英文摘要：**
> UNLABELLED: Metabolic dysregulation is a major hallmark of cancer, making interventions that modify tumor nutrient availability attractive adjuvants for improving clinical outcomes for patients with cancer. Clarifying how the nutritional status of individual patients affects the metabolic vulnerability of tumors to drugs is needed to inform personalized treatment guidelines. Working toward the goal of oncometabolic precision medicine, we developed the cancer metabolism-based synthetic lethality platform (CM-SLP), a high-throughput screening platform that explores the metabolic vulnerability of cancer cells to nononcology drugs induced by altered nutrient availability and predicts potential synthetic lethal interactions with nutrient conditions. Promising CM-SLP candidates included propafenone and biguanides as representative nononcology drugs that cooperatively enhanced cytotoxicity via dysregulated metabolic pathways. Furthermore, the mTOR and Hippo pathways mediated the response to combined propafenone/hypoglycemia or biguanides/hypoglycemia treatments, respectively, and mTOR or TEAD inhibitors circumvented the need for dietary interventions to enhance cancer cell death. Together, these results indicate that CM-SLP represents a promising approach for integrating metabolic profiling into precision oncology, offering therapeutic avenues tailored to individual patient needs.
> 
> SIGNIFICANCE: A high-throughput screening approach investigating drug vulnerabilities dependent on nutrient status supports repurposing FDA-approved compounds as metabolically informed therapies for next-generation oncometabolic precision medicine.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无标签：代谢失调是癌症的一个主要标志，这使得改变肿瘤营养可用性的干预措施成为改善癌症患者临床结局的有吸引力的辅助手段。需要阐明个体患者的营养状况如何影响肿瘤对药物的代谢脆弱性，以指导个性化治疗指南。为了实现肿瘤代谢精准医学的目标，我们开发了基于癌症代谢的合成致死平台（CM-SLP），这是一个高通量筛选平台，旨在探索由营养可用性改变诱导的癌细胞对非肿瘤药物的代谢脆弱性，并预测其与营养条件之间潜在的合成致死相互作用。有前景的CM-SLP候选药物包括普罗帕酮和双胍类药物，它们作为代表性非肿瘤药物，通过失调的代谢通路协同增强了细胞毒性。此外，mTOR和Hippo通路分别介导了对普罗帕酮/低血糖或双胍类药物/低血糖联合治疗的反应，而mTOR或TEAD抑制剂则绕过了饮食干预的需要来增强癌细胞死亡。总之，这些结果表明CM-SLP代表了一种将代谢谱分析整合到精准肿瘤学中的有前景的方法，提供了针对个体患者需求量身定制的治疗途径。
> 
> 意义：一项研究依赖于营养状态的药物脆弱性的高通量筛选方法，支持将FDA批准的化合物重新用作代谢信息疗法，用于下一代肿瘤代谢精准医学。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在推进肿瘤代谢精准医学，核心是开发了CM-SLP高通量筛选平台，用于系统性探索营养条件如何影响癌细胞对非肿瘤药物的敏感性。研究发现普罗帕酮和双胍类药物在特定营养（如低血糖）条件下能协同杀伤癌细胞，并揭示mTOR和Hippo通路是关键的调控机制，且可通过抑制剂模拟营养干预效果。其创新性在于将营养环境与药物重定位相结合，为个体化治疗提供了新策略，但局限性在于目前发现主要基于体外筛选，其临床转化效果及患者营养状态的精准调控仍需后续研究验证。

---

## 123. CDK12缺陷通过诱导BRD4S增强相分离和染色质结合以促进癌症转移。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41289556)
**期刊：** Cancer research
**PMID：** 41289556
**DOI：** 10.1158/0008-5472.CAN-25-1761

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** CDK12 Deficiency Induces BRD4S to Promote Cancer Metastasis by Enhancing Phase Separation and Chromatin Engagement.

> **英文摘要：**
> UNLABELLED: CDK12 is frequently deleted and/or mutated in human cancers, and CDK12 inactivation is associated with aggressive phenotypes, including the tendency to metastasis. In this study, we showed that CDK12 deficiency induced intronic polyadenylation (IPA) usage in BRD4 to upregulate expression of the bromodomain-containing protein 4 (BRD4) short isoform (BRD4S). BRD4S demonstrated an enhanced capacity to form phase separation despite lacking the intrinsically disordered region located in the C-terminal of full-length BRD4. Oligomerization of BRD4S mediated phase separation through a base-interacting structural domain. CUT&Tag and RNA sequencing analyses revealed that BRD4S preferentially bound to the promoters of TGFβ signaling genes, including TGFB2 and LTBP1, driving their expression. Consistently, BRD4S drove cancer cell dissemination in vitro and metastasis in vivo, which could be blocked by BET or TGFβ signaling pathway inhibitors. Overall, this study identifies IPA usage at the BRD4 gene locus induced by CDK12 deficiency as a mechanism responsible for BRD4S genesis, which represents an important mechanism driving cancer metastasis and a potential target for therapeutic intervention in CDK12-deficient cancers.
> 
> SIGNIFICANCE: The CDK12-BRD4S-TGFβ signaling axis represents a key regulatory module that promotes metastatic progression and can be targeted by BET or TGFβ pathway inhibitors for treating CDK12-deficient cancers.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无标签：CDK12在人类癌症中经常发生缺失和/或突变，且CDK12失活与侵袭性表型相关，包括转移倾向。在本研究中，我们发现CDK12缺陷诱导了BRD4基因的内含子多聚腺苷酸化（IPA）使用，从而上调了含溴结构域蛋白4（BRD4）短亚型（BRD4S）的表达。尽管缺乏位于全长BRD4 C端的固有无序区域，BRD4S仍表现出更强的形成相分离的能力。BRD4S通过一个基础相互作用结构域介导寡聚化，从而驱动相分离。CUT&Tag和RNA测序分析显示，BRD4S优先结合TGFβ信号通路基因（如TGFB2和LTBP1）的启动子，并驱动其表达。一致地，BRD4S在体外驱动了癌细胞扩散，在体内驱动了转移，而这一过程可被BET抑制剂或TGFβ信号通路抑制剂所阻断。总之，本研究确定了CDK12缺陷诱导的BRD4基因位点IPA使用是BRD4S生成的一种机制，这代表了驱动癌症转移的重要机制，也是CDK12缺陷型癌症治疗干预的潜在靶点。
> 
> 意义：CDK12-BRD4S-TGFβ信号轴代表了一个促进转移进展的关键调控模块，可通过BET抑制剂或TGFβ通路抑制剂靶向治疗CDK12缺陷型癌症。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明CDK12缺陷促进癌症转移的分子机制。通过结合分子生物学、基因组学（CUT&Tag、RNA-seq）和细胞/动物模型，研究者发现CDK12失活通过诱导BRD4基因的内含子多聚腺苷酸化（IPA）上调其短亚型BRD4S的表达。创新性地揭示了BRD4S虽缺乏固有无序区，却能通过寡聚化增强相分离能力，并特异性结合TGFβ通路基因启动子驱动转移。该工作构建了从基因缺陷（CDK12）到转录调控（BRD4S）再到信号通路（TGFβ）的完整促转移轴，并验证了其药物敏感性，为CDK12缺陷型癌症提供了新的治疗思路。局限性在于主要结论基于实验模型，其临床转化价值及在更广泛癌症类型中的普适性有待进一步验证。

## 124. 空间多组学分析揭示终末期肾病中的致癌通路。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41263668)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41263668
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-0472

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Spatial Multiomic Analyses Reveal Carcinogenic Pathways in End-Stage Renal Disease.

> **英文摘要：**
> UNLABELLED: Patients with end-stage renal disease (ESRD) are at increased risk of acquired cystic kidney disease (ACKD) and renal tumors, but the molecular basis of such disorders remains elusive. In this study, we performed spatial immunogenomic analyses on 268 specimens from 43 patients with ACKD and associated tumors. The molecular landscape of ESRD-associated tumors is different from that of sporadic renal cell carcinoma. Single-cell and spatial analyses have shown that ACKD is under an inflammatory environment and that the renal cysts in ACKD are derived from proximal tubular cells that have survived the destructive effects of inflammation. Interestingly, we revealed that cysts are formed by clonal expansion and that paracrine activation of the MET tyrosine kinase pathway by the surrounding environment nurtures cysts. Collectively, our results identify the oncogenic mechanisms of ESRD-associated renal tumors and will pave the way for improving the prognosis of patients with ESRD.
> 
> SIGNIFICANCE: We elucidated the molecular basis of renal cancer arising in patients with ESRD and show that the inflammatory environment of ESRD gives rise to field cancerization. See related commentary by Sager et al., p. 426.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无标签：终末期肾病（ESRD）患者发生获得性囊性肾病（ACKD）和肾脏肿瘤的风险增加，但此类疾病的分子基础仍不清楚。在本研究中，我们对来自43名ACKD及相关肿瘤患者的268份样本进行了空间免疫基因组学分析。ESRD相关肿瘤的分子图谱与散发性肾细胞癌不同。单细胞和空间分析表明，ACKD处于炎症环境中，且ACKD中的肾囊肿来源于在炎症破坏作用下存活下来的近端肾小管细胞。有趣的是，我们发现囊肿是通过克隆扩增形成的，并且周围环境通过旁分泌方式激活MET酪氨酸激酶通路，从而滋养囊肿。总之，我们的研究结果揭示了ESRD相关肾肿瘤的致癌机制，并将为改善ESRD患者的预后铺平道路。
> 
> 意义：我们阐明了ESRD患者发生肾癌的分子基础，并表明ESRD的炎症环境导致了区域癌化。参见Sager等人的相关评论，第426页。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在阐明终末期肾病（ESRD）背景下获得性囊性肾病（ACKD）及肾肿瘤的分子机制。研究团队采用空间多组学分析（包括空间免疫基因组学、单细胞分析）对大量临床样本进行了系统性解析。核心发现是：ESRD相关肿瘤具有独特的分子图谱；其发生始于炎症环境中存活下来的近端肾小管细胞，这些细胞通过克隆扩增形成囊肿，并依赖微环境旁分泌激活的MET通路驱动生长，揭示了“区域癌化”的具体路径。该研究的创新性在于整合空间技术与多组学数据，动态解析了从炎症到囊肿再到肿瘤的连续致癌过程，为ESRD患者的肾癌风险监测和靶向干预（如MET抑制剂）提供了直接理论依据；局限性在于结论主要基于观察性关联分析，其因果机制及临床转化价值有待后续功能实验和前瞻性研究验证。

---

## 125. DNMT3A R882H突变并非原发性人急性髓系白血病疾病维持所必需，但与白血病干细胞频率增加相关。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41263425)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41263425
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-24-1604

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** DNMT3A R882H Is Not Required for Disease Maintenance in Primary Human AML but Is Associated with Increased Leukemia Stem Cell Frequency.

> **英文摘要：**
> UNLABELLED: Genetic mutations are being thoroughly mapped in human cancers, yet a fundamental question in cancer biology is whether such mutations are functionally required for cancer initiation, maintenance of established cancer, or both. In this study, we examine this question in the context of human acute myeloid leukemia (AML), in which DNMT3AR882 missense mutations often arise early, in preleukemic clonal hematopoiesis, and corrupt the DNA methylation landscape to initiate leukemia. We developed CRISPR-based methods to directly correct DNMT3AR882 mutations in leukemic cells obtained from patients. Surprisingly, DNMT3AR882 mutations were largely dispensable for disease maintenance. Replacing DNMT3AR882 mutants with wild-type DNMT3A did not impair the ability of AML cells to engraft in vivo and minimally altered DNA methylation. Taken together, DNMT3AR882 mutations are initially necessary for AML initiation but are largely dispensable for disease maintenance. The notion that initiating oncogenes differ from those that maintain cancer has important implications for cancer evolution and therapy. SIGNIFICANCE: Understanding which driver mutations are required for cancer initiation, maintenance, or both phases remains poorly understood. In this study, we uncover that highly prevalent preleukemic DNMT3A mutations are only required during disease initiation but become dispensable after leukemic transformation, uncovering the context-specific role of this driver mutation with important therapeutic implications. See related commentary by Zhou and Huang, p. 428.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无标签：人类癌症中的基因突变正被全面绘制，但癌症生物学的一个基本问题是，这些突变在功能上是否为癌症起始、已形成癌症的维持或两者所必需。在本研究中，我们在人急性髓系白血病（AML）的背景下探讨了这个问题。在AML中，DNMT3A R882错义突变常在白血病前克隆性造血阶段早期出现，并通过破坏DNA甲基化格局来启动白血病。我们开发了基于CRISPR的方法，直接纠正从患者体内获取的白血病细胞中的DNMT3A R882突变。出乎意料的是，DNMT3A R882突变在很大程度上对于疾病维持是非必需的。用野生型DNMT3A替换DNMT3A R882突变体，并未损害AML细胞在体内的定植能力，且对DNA甲基化的改变极小。综上所述，DNMT3A R882突变最初是AML起始所必需的，但在很大程度上对于疾病维持是非必需的。起始癌基因与维持癌症的癌基因不同的这一概念，对癌症进化和治疗具有重要意义。意义：目前尚不清楚哪些驱动突变是癌症起始、维持或两个阶段所必需的。在本研究中，我们发现高度普遍的白血病前DNMT3A突变仅在疾病起始阶段是必需的，而在白血病转化后变得非必需，这揭示了该驱动突变具有情境特异性的作用，并具有重要的治疗意义。参见Zhou和Huang的相关评论，第428页。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究旨在探究DNMT3A R882突变在AML发生与维持中的功能必要性。研究者创新性地采用基于CRISPR的基因直接纠正技术，在患者来源的原代AML细胞中进行功能验证。核心发现是，该突变是白血病起始所必需的，但在已建立的AML中对于疾病维持却非必需，这挑战了驱动突变在癌症全程中均发挥关键作用的传统观点。该发现具有重要的理论价值，揭示了癌基因作用的阶段特异性，为理解肿瘤进化及制定靶向治疗策略提供了新视角，但研究主要聚焦于DNMT3A R882突变，其结论是否适用于其他驱动突变或AML亚型仍需进一步探索。

---

## 126. BESTDR实现机制特异性药物反应的贝叶斯量化

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41248483)
**期刊：** Cancer research
**PMID：** 41248483
**DOI：** 10.1158/0008-5472.CAN-25-1181

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** BESTDR Enables Bayesian Quantification of Mechanism-Specific Drug Responses.

> **英文摘要：**
> UNLABELLED: Understanding drug responses at the cellular level is essential for elucidating mechanisms of action and advancing preclinical drug development. Traditional dose-response models rely on simplified metrics, limiting their ability to quantify parameters like cell division, death, and transition rates between cell states. To address these limitations, we developed Bayesian Estimation of STochastic processes for Dose-Response (BESTDR), a framework modeling cell growth and treatment response dynamics to estimate concentration-response relationships using longitudinal cell count data. BESTDR enables quantification of rates in multistate systems across multiple cell lines using hierarchical modeling to support high-throughput screening. Validation of BESTDR with synthetic and experimental datasets demonstrates its accuracy and robustness in estimating drug response. By integrating mechanistic modeling of cytotoxic, cytostatic, and other drug effects, BESTDR enhances dose-response studies, facilitating robust drug comparisons and mechanism-specific analyses. BESTDR offers a versatile tool for early-stage preclinical research, paving the way for drug discovery and informed experimental design.
> 
> SIGNIFICANCE: BESTDR leverages time-course cell count data to provide mechanistic insights into drug actions, distinguishing cytostatic, cytotoxic, and state transitions, thus advancing dose-response modeling crucial for preclinical research and development of targeted therapies. This article is part of a special series: Driving Cancer Discoveries with Computational Research, Data Science, and Machine Learning/AI .

> **中文摘要：**
> 无标签：在细胞水平理解药物反应对于阐明作用机制和推进临床前药物开发至关重要。传统的剂量反应模型依赖于简化的指标，限制了其量化细胞分裂、死亡以及细胞状态间转换速率等参数的能力。为了解决这些局限性，我们开发了用于剂量反应的随机过程贝叶斯估计（BESTDR），这是一个对细胞生长和治疗反应动态进行建模的框架，利用纵向细胞计数数据来估计浓度-反应关系。BESTDR通过分层建模，能够量化跨多个细胞系的多状态系统中的速率，以支持高通量筛选。使用合成和实验数据集对BESTDR进行的验证表明其在估计药物反应方面的准确性和稳健性。通过整合细胞毒性、细胞抑制性及其他药物效应的机制性建模，BESTDR增强了剂量反应研究，促进了稳健的药物比较和机制特异性分析。BESTDR为早期临床前研究提供了一个多功能工具，为药物发现和明智的实验设计铺平了道路。
> 
> 意义：BESTDR利用时间进程细胞计数数据，为药物作用提供机制性见解，区分细胞抑制、细胞毒性和状态转换，从而推进了对临床前研究和靶向疗法开发至关重要的剂量反应建模。本文是特刊系列“利用计算研究、数据科学和机器学习/人工智能驱动癌症发现”的一部分。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究开发了名为BESTDR的贝叶斯统计框架，其核心目的是超越传统剂量反应模型的简化指标，实现对细胞分裂、死亡及状态转换等机制特异性参数的量化。该方法通过整合纵向细胞计数数据与分层建模，能够系统分析多细胞系、多状态系统中的药物动力学，支持高通量筛选。其创新性在于将随机过程建模与贝叶斯推断相结合，为区分细胞毒性、细胞抑制等不同作用机制提供了定量工具，显著增强了临床前药物评价的解析深度。然而，该方法的性能高度依赖于输入数据的质量与规模，且其计算复杂度可能对常规实验室的应用构成一定门槛。
